NP_0.1^1	śrīmat veṅkaṭa nātha deśika maṇi prajñā sarit taraṅga paramparā pariṇāma bhūtam nyāya pariśuddhi abhidhānam prabandha ratnam idam jayati jīvitam iva nyāya vistarasya vidyā sthānasya śrī bhagavat rāma anuja muni vara kṣuṇṇa vartmanaḥ brahmamī māṃsā śāstrasya ca anupajīvya ca idam vidyā sthānam kaḥ vibhavaḥ sa panditum api śeṣasya vidyā sthāna jātasya  sarvam eva hi loke śrutam saṃśaya viparyayābhyām āhita pāriplavam vātyāspṛṣṭam iva tṛṇa śakalam na kathañcid api pratitiṣṭhati pramāṇa parīkṣayā tu yathāvat upapāditayā dṛṣadeva vyapoḍha vikṣobham niṣkampam avatiṣṭhate 
NP_0.1^2	 pramāṇa parīkṣā eva ca prathama avatāra padavī nyāya vistarasya pada vākya pramāṇa bhedena hi tredhāḥ vibhajanti śāstram śāstra vidaḥ tatra tat am nāma śabda anuśāsanam pāṇini ādi praṇītam vākyam ca vicāra pūrvaka śrauta vākya artha nirṇaya rūpam karma brahma ātmaka viṣaya vibhāga vibhaktam ubhayam mīmāsā śāstram pramāṇam tu kvacid api artheṣu anavagāḍha avaṣṭambhām sva ātmani api anupajāta visrambhām ḍolāyamānām buddhim kareṇum iva tarka śṛṅkhalābhiḥ ālānayat manana vyapadeśam śāstram yasya saṃjñā antaram nyāya vistaraḥ tarka śāstram ityādi 
NP_0.2^1	 tat etat pramāṇa pradhānam api pramāṇa gateḥ prameya svarūpa vivecana paryavasāna tayā prameyepi nyasta padam pravṛttam itaretara visaṃvāda saṃrabdha uddhuraiḥ āstikaiḥ nāstikaiḥ ca bahudhā vādibhiḥ sva sva= chanda anurodhena anyathā ca anyathā ca prameyam pratipadyamānaiḥ itas tatas parikṛṣyamāṇāni pramāṇāni api parāvṛtta rūpa tayā lakṣaṇataḥ durgrahāṇi abhūvan māna ābhāsa vyāmiśrāṇi hi mānāni na sukarāṇi vivektum tat evam śāstram eva paṅkilīkṛtam cakṣuḥ iva timira upasṛṣṭam vigalita artha grahaṇa apāṭava saṃvṛttam 
NP_0.2^2	 aviparyasta lakṣaṇam pramāṇa vargam parigṛhṇādbhiḥ api saugata arhataka apila cārvāka jaiminīya ādibhiḥ aṅgeṣu avāntara bhedeṣu canyūna atirekam āsthitaiḥ anekadhā upayogāt anekāntī kṛta matayaḥ kṛta matayā upi sva sva upadeśa pāramparī pratyayāt ekatamam pakṣam abhimanyamānāḥ sparigraha avasāda kātara tayā pakṣa antareṣu sa abhyasūyāḥ cirāya api garu kuleṣu pariśramya alabdha buddhi prasādāḥ vibhrāmyante eva anubhūyante atas sarva upayogāya doṣa guṇa hāna upādānābhyām śikṣaṇīyasya asya nyāya vistarasya pṛthakprasthānam nyāya darśanam nāma sūtra jātam gautamena muninā prathamam praṇītam yatra pramāṇa apramāṇa ādi vivecanayā tattva nirṇaya upāyāḥ tatra ca saṃbhavantaḥ guṇa doṣāḥ kathāsu ca grāhyā parihārya vibhāgāḥ sa viśeṣam pradarśitāḥ 
NP_0.3^1	 tat ca nyāya darśanam prathamam pramāṇa prameya ādi sūtreṇa ṣoḍaśadhā padārthān vibhajya tad parīkṣaṇena caritārthama tatra prameya tvasya kevala anvayinaḥ sarva padārtha sādhāraṇa tayā vibhājaka tvam anupapadyamānam manyamānena kaṇā ādena muninā kṛtsnam eva prameya jātam dravya ādi sapta padārtha parisaṃkhyānena asaṃkīrṇam vibhaktam tatra ca sāmānya viśeṣa samavāya abhāvān vitatham eva apadārthān padārthayatā tathāvidham eva ca anyat anyat ālapatā grāhyam agṛhṇatā tyājyam ca atyajatā kaṇa bhakṣeṇa dūram apathīkṛtaḥ śāstra pathaḥ iti brahmasūtra kāra ādibhiḥ pratikṣiptaḥ vaiśeṣikaḥ pakṣaḥ nyāya pakṣaḥ tu śaṅkyamāna upasarga upi kathañcid vyākhyāna ādheya saṃskāra tayā na atyartha parivarjanīyaḥ iti manyamānāḥ katipaya saṃskāra saṃskṛtam imam pakṣam parigṛhya nibandhāt nibabandhuḥ pūrve kecid ācāryāḥ 
NP_0.3^2	 te ca nibandhāḥ eṣu divaseṣu nāmnā eva kevalam avaśiṣyantaḥ tat yathā śrīmat nātha m uni miśra praṇītam nyāya tattvam śrīmat parāśara bhaṭṭāraka kṛtiḥ tattva ratna ākaraḥ śrī bhagavat yāmunā ācāryāṇām ācāryaiḥ śrīmat nātha muni caraṇa āśrayāṇām śrī puṇḍarīkākṣāṇām śiṣyaiḥ ca śrī rāma miśra gurubhiḥ viracitam vivaraṇam ṣaṣ artha saṃkṣepaḥ ca iti grantha dvayam avidita prabandhṛ vyapadeśam nyāya su darśanam prajñā paritrāṇām ca iti prabandha yugalam śrīmat nārāyaṇa muni viracita tvena ācārya upāttam nāmnā ca anuddiṣṭam kim api prabandha ratnam asya eva ca nyāya pariśuddhi praṇetuḥ ācāryasya ācāryeṇa mātulena ca vādi haṃsa ambuvāhaḥ iti praśasti nāma aṅkitena ātreya rāma anuja ācāryeṇa kṛtam sva pratibhā draviṇa nikṣepāyamāṇam nyāya kuliśa abhidhānam ca iti ete nibandhāḥ nyāya pariśuddhi kṛtā eva ācāryeṇa tatra tatra bhūyiṣṭham udāhriyante 
NP_0.3^3	 yat eva yāvat eva ca ācāryeṇa kvacid kvacid udāhṛtam vākyam vākya khaṇḍam vā tat atiriktam kiyat api ṭīkākṛtām api dṛṣṭi viṣayībhūtam na upalabhyate ayam atra hetuḥ pratibhāti ācārya saṃnihita kāleṣu api anatisaṃkṣepa vistara ramaṇīyāni prasphuṭa arthāni nitya prakāśāni ācārya śrī sūkti ratnāni avamṛśya rasa āsvāda vādi vijaya śiṣya pravacana adri pravaṇeṣu upari upari vyākhyāna ādi praṇayanaiḥ avistṛtya śāstram vitatham eva atipātita kāleṣu śiṣya praśiṣya vargeṣu kumāra vedānta ācārya ādiṣu atīte ca gaṇarātre kaiścid arvācīnaiḥ āvirbhūtaiḥ grantha kṛdbhiḥ ajñāta pūrva vṛttāntaiḥ yathā kathañcit vyākhyānena kaścid upakāraḥ kṛtaḥ iti 
NP_0.4^1	 hanta ! niḥśeṣa kṣālita akhila kalaṅkasya api asya śrī bhagavat rāma anuja siddhāntasya idam ekam śocanīyam vaiśasam yat tāvat ācārya pada abhiṣiktaiḥ api arvācīnaiḥ budha varaiḥ kāṇāda gautamīya ādi sāmānya śāstra pariśrameṇa vyayitavayobhiḥ antime vayasi kathañcid upajāta vedānta tṛṣṇaiḥ śiṣya saṃgrahaṇa kṛta kṣaṇaiḥ avaśya upādeya upadeśa śrībhāṣya ādi katipaya grantha grahaṇa carita arthaiḥ anādṛtāḥ prācām ācāryāṇām vāc vistarāḥ etarhi śrotum api durlabha tām gamita arḥ idṛśoyam vidyauvadhaḥ kasya vā vidyā vyasaninaḥ na dūnoti mānasam  athavā kṛtam prācām prabandha praṇāśa cintanena asya eva ācāryasya vāc madhu niṣyandaḥ mudhā eva kiyāt na visraṃsitaḥ sarva tantra svatantrāṇām ācārya caraṇānām śata adhikāḥ prabandhāḥ hāra vimalāḥ prasiddhāḥ 
NP_0.4^2	 saṃskṛta prākṛta drāviḍa bhāṣā abhiḥ tra rauśikāni kāvya nāṭaka stotrāṇi lokaśāstra vyavahāra nirūḍha saṃskṛta vyatikīrṇa drāviḍa bhāṣā mayāni ca caturtha rāśi niviṣṭā nilaukikānām api anugrāhakāni parīkṣakāṇām api sugraha sāṃpradāyika tattva hita puruṣa arthāni ādarśa vimalāni maṇi pravāla śabditāni niyata śrāvya tayā rahasya saṃjñitāni siddhānta niṣkarṣaṇa īdaṃparāṇi loka śreyase jātāni grantha jātāni tatra vedānte tāvat tat tvaṭīkā nāma śrī bhagavat rāma anuja muni vara viracitasya śārīrakamī māṃsa ābhāṣyasya vivṛtiḥ apūrvā artha viśeṣa vinyāsa paribhūṣitā traikālya saṃbhāvanīyānām aśeṣa ākṣepāṇām acala niścayān parihāra anupadarśayantī gaṅgena gaurī guroḥ etasmāt ācārya varyāt āvirbhūtā sā ca prathama sūtra mātram api yāvat asamagra upalabdha pracārā vedānta vidyā vicāra kāṅkṣiṇām cintā vyasanāya eva khaṇḍa bhūtā paridṛśyate vicitra āyodhanā kuṇṭha śaktau tejasvini svām śakti samagram adarśayitvā eva niyati yaiyātyena akasmāt uparatam yodha ratne taṭastha dṛṣṭe kasya vā vīra dharmam anutiṣṭhataḥ hṛdayam na dūyeta soyam asya nibandha ratnasya lope dṛṣṭāntaḥ 
NP_0.4^3	 kecid manyeran ācāryaiḥ eva na samāpūrita ayam granthaḥ iti tat etat sva upamānena sarvatra śakti paricchedam kalayatām pralapitam atra na kramate trividhāḥ khalu loke prabandha kṛtaḥ kecid guru kula cira pariśramaiḥ anekaśas śrutān yathāśrutam arthān patreṣu viniveśya prakāśayantaḥ lokam anugṛhṇanti atha itare ye punar jātyā eva sphaṭika avadāta buddhayaḥ sattva viśeṣa āvirbhāva nistuṣa āśayāḥ svatas svānta mukura tala sphuṭa saṃkrānta sarva artha praticchandāḥ api saṃpradāya parirakṣaṇa śraddhalu tayā guru upadeśa darśitām pada vīm avarjayantaḥ citta ghaṇṭā patheṣu sama samaya saṃcarat akhila pramāṇa tarka guru upadeśa saṃpradāya viśeṣā eka helayā bhūyasorthān ayatnena grahītum praṇetum api arhanti anye tu nirantara bhajana kṛta prasadanena bhagavatā sarva īśvareṇa dūra pratyūḍha pratyūha vipruṣaḥ niḥśreyasa avadhīni kuśala jātāni anubhavitum nija caraṇa śaraṇān api anubhāvayitum ca akuṇṭha śaktayaḥ tṛtīya kakṣyā niviṣṭāḥ 
NP_0.4^4	 te ete vyāsa parāśara vālmīki pramukhaiḥ mahā ṛṣi gaṇaiḥ api gaṇanīya anubhāvāḥ vilakṣaṇāḥ prabandha kṛtaḥ yeṣām eka pratibhā sūtra syūtāni prameya ratnāni punar punar pariśīlitāni api nava navāni iva prajñāvatām hṛdayeṣu kam api camatkāram āvahanti na ca kadācid purāṇa citra vat vicchāyāni bhavanti nyāpariśuddhi kṛt ācāryaḥ tu dvitīya tṛtīyayoḥ ubhayoḥ apri kakṣyayoḥ hāra āvalyoḥ iva nāyaka maṇiḥ prakāśate iti tattva vidām aparokṣam prakṛti siddham ca prakrāntasya anta gamanam śaktimatām loka anugraha mātra phalāḥ yeṣām sarvāḥ pravṛttayaḥ tādṛśānām ayatna nirvartanīye loka upakāra arthe samārambhe cikīrṣita vicchedaḥ katham upapadyate  evaṅguṇena ca ācārya cūḍāmaṇi pavanā śiṣya buddhim prasādayitum ārabdhā kṛtirasam āpya madhye apaviddhā bhavati iti kaḥ nukhalu prabhāva vedī pratipattum arhati  api ca nikhila nigama śreṇī cūḍā pariṣkṛti rūpiṇī nipuṇa manasām āśā sa odha sthalīṣu nibadhyate yatipati bhuvaḥ bhāṣyasya asau yathāśrata acintitaḥ pravacana vidhau= aṣṭāviṃśe jayadhvaja paṭṭikā 
NP_0.5	 iti sva kṛtasya bhāṣya pravacanasya aṣṭāviṃśya āmā vṛttau tattvaṭī kā nibandha praṇayanam ācāryaḥ tattvaṭīkā prārambhe svayam eva spaṣṭam āha saṃkalpa sūrya udaya prastāvanāyām ca viṃśati abde viśruta nānāvidha vidyaḥ triṃśat vāram śrāvita śārīraka bhāṣyaḥ śreyaḥ śrīmān veṅkaṭa nāthaḥ śruti pathyam nātha prītyai nāṭakam arthyam vyadhita etat 
NP_0.6^1	 iti sūtra dhāra vācā śārīraka bhāṣya pravacanam saṃkalpa sūrya udaya nirmāṇa kāle triṃśat vāra kṛtam prathayati tadānīm eva triṃśat vāram śārīraka bhāṣya pravacanam āsīt yadi tatas paścāt pravacana āvṛttayaḥ tata upi hi bhūyasyaḥ bhavitum arhanti kṛṣṇa miśra samāgama kālaḥ hi saṃkalpa sūrya udaya nirmāṇa samayaḥ tatas ca aṣṭāviṃśyāmā vṛttau tattvaṭīkā nirmāṇam kṛṣṇa miśra samāgamāt pūrvataram bhavati śata dūṣaṇyāḥ samanantaram tat tvaṭīkā kṛtā iti ca pratīyate uktam hi svayam eva ācāryaiḥ tattvaṭīkām prakramamāṇaiḥ śātitaḥ śata dūṣaṇyām śaṅkara ādi mudhā grahaḥ śarīraka śarīram tu vyaktam atra pradarśyate iti śruta prakāśikā bhūmau yena ādau parirakṣitā pravartitā ca pātreṣu tasmai śreṣṭhāya maṅgalam iti kumāra vedānta ācārya kṛta maṅgala āśāsana parāmarśane śruta prakāśikā pravacana tatpara tvam ācāryāṇām tattvaṭīka āpūraṇa vighātāya jātam syāt iti ca apāta ram aṇīyam 
NP_0.6^2	 śru prakāśika ācāryasya himlet cha bala upamarda lagnasya nija guru sabrahmacāriṇaḥ mumūrṣataḥ prārthanayā tad grantha rakṣaṇa pravacanayoḥ aṅgīkārepi na etāvatā svakīyam mahīyāṃsam prabandha praṇayana prayatnam ācāryaḥ vitathīkariṣyati na hmatratyam apūrvam artha jātam grantha antareṇa caritārtham bhavati tat idam ācārya granthe kṛta śramāṇām svatas eva su vyaktam idānīm upalabhyamāna paryantepi tattvaṭī kā grantha khaṇḍe ye viṣayāḥ pratipādyantu na ete śruta prakāśikāyām anyatra vā grantha antare pratipattum sulabhāḥ kiñca su ācāryaiḥ vādi haṃsa ambu vāha āryaiḥ praṇīte vidyamānaḥ eva hi nyāya kuliśa ākhye nyāya nibandha ratne nyāya pariśuddhim ācāryaḥ svayam nibabandha avaśya vaktavyeṣu ca artheṣu joṣaṃbhāvaḥ kathañcid api śāsra ācārya tāyāḥ sadṛśaḥ na bhavati na ca nava nava artha āviṣkaraṇam arvācām prācīnācārya paribhavāya api ca nikhila nigama śreṇī cūḍā pariṣkṛti rūpiṇī nipuṇa manasām āśā sa odha sthalīṣu nibadhyate 
NP_0.7	 iti prabandha upakrama pratijñānam eva pradarśayati grantha antaraiḥ acarita arthasya sarva vedānta artha saṃskārasya mahāmatibhiḥ api sarvajña sakāśāt śuśrūṣitasya pratipādana artham apūrvāyāḥ kṛteḥ samārambhaḥ iti sa katham na paripūryeta  kiñca nija nibandhasya śruta prakāśikā rakṣaṇa aṅgīkāra samayaḥ eva labdha prasara tām anusmṛtya parakīya grantha pravacanam aṅgīkṛtam ācāryaiḥ iti śakyam abhyūhitum tathā ca sati tattvaṭī kā grantha lopanidāna marvācām ācāryāṇām tatra apariśīlanam eva na tu grantha apari samāptiḥ yathā hi nyāya siddha añjanam api jaḍa dravya paricche dena eva paryavasitam sāṃpratam paridṛśyate adravya paricchedaḥ tu patitaḥ eva aśakyam ca tad pūraṇam anyaiḥ ittham amum artham śrīraṅga rāma anujaguruḥ eva nyāya siddha añjana vyākhyāne na kvāpi atas parama dṛsyata kośaśeṣaḥ tad śeṣa pūraṇa kṛtiḥ parihāsa hetuḥ jñātavyam anyat api taiḥ niraṇāyi samyak grantha antareṣu iti na kiñcid iha asti cintyam 
NP_0.8	 iti nigamayat nivedayati śata dūṣaṇī api hi na samagrā dṛśyate ṣaṭṣaṣṭiḥ eva vādāḥ loke pracaranti śeṣe tu mithyā eva kim api aitihyam kalpayitvā katipaye prajalpanti yat tāvat dvaita mata khaṇḍana paraḥ śeṣaḥ granthaḥ madhvamatasthena kenacid yatinā bhikṣām aṭa tā sa vinayam upasṛtya prārthitoyam ācāryaḥ tam tasya bhikṣā arthe prāyacchid iti tat api na vicāra kṣamam na hi ācārya grantheṣu kvacid api madhva matam nirasyate tattva viplava abhāvāt avāntareṣu ca artheṣu naiyāyika vaiśeṣika ādi pratipāditasya eva dvaitasya anuvādāt anatipracura tayā tasya matasya loka viplava prasaṃga abhāvāt cānā sthā eva ācāryāṇām tatra syāt atas catustriṃśadvādāḥ madhva mata khaṇḍana parāḥ iti kiṃvad antī mātram etat śatadūṣaṇī ca śaṅkā ādi kṛta sūtra vyākhyāna ādi nirāsa artham eva pravṛttā iti ca tad grantha mukhaḥ eva sphuṭībhavati tatra hi prācīm upetya padavīm yati rāja dṛṣṭām tad saṃnikṛṣṭam api vā matam āśrayantaḥ prājñāḥ yathā uditam idam śuka vat paṭhantaḥ pracchanna bauddha vijaye paritas yatadhvam 
NP_0.9–0.10	 iti pratiśrutam atra atad saṃnikṛṣṭam api vā matam āśrayantaḥ a iti anena dvaitinaḥ sva pakṣīkriyante advaita khaṇḍanam eva ca grantha pravṛtti prayojanam iti ca darśitam tathā ca vidyā araṇya akṣobhya muni vivāde nirṇayam bruvadbhiḥ ācāryeḥ asinā tattvam asinā para jīva prabhedinā vidyā araṇya mahā araṇyam akṣobhyam uniḥ acchinat iti uktam aśātitaḥ śata dūṣaṇyām śaṅkara ādi mudhā grahaḥ a iti atra tu śaṅkara ādi ityādi padam yādava bhāskarayoḥ saṃgrahāya iti sthitam tasmāt samagra grantha adarśanamarvācām ācāryāṇām pravacana viccheda nibandhanam prabandha lopahetuḥ iti spaṣṭam etat 
NP_0.11^1	 atra prasakta anuprasaktam ācāryasya kṛṣṇa miśra samāgama caritam kiñcid upanyasyate kṛṣṇa miśraḥ hi gauḍa deśīyaḥ paṇḍita cūḍāmaṇiḥ sarvāsu vidyāsu kalāsu ca sa viśeṣa kṛta śramaḥ kaviḥ ca brahmādvaitam siddhantam ātiṣṭhamānaḥ vāda kutūhalitayā sarvāḥ diśaḥ paryaṭan jita kāśī krameṇa dakṣiṇān diśamācakrāma tatra śrīraṅgam divya kṣetram viduṣām āvāsam ākarṇya deva sevā apadeśena vāda samaram arthayamānaḥ śrīraṅga rājasya bhava gataḥ prāsāda māsadāda 
NP_0.11^2	 tadānīm tatra bhāṣā mayīḥ gāthāḥ sa rāga tālam gīyamānāḥ niśamya tad kartṝṇām ca kavīnām varṇa avarāṇām api pratimāḥ tasmin devālaye deva upacāraiḥ ārādhyamānāḥ viditvā tatra sevā samavetān jñāna vṛddhān śrī vaiṣṇavān āmantrya abhoḥ prājñāḥ bhavatām anena apabhraṃśa pāṭhena varṇa avara pūjanena ca dūra apoḍham veṣṇavam tejaḥ kim anena ārādhanena  anthatha akṛtam akṛtam hi bhavati a iti sa ākṣepam papraccha yadā taiḥ militaiḥ api na kiñcid ākṣepa sadṛśam uttaram pratipannam tadā tad ātanāya tad deśa adhipataye tam artham āvedya pratiṣṭhā prabhṛti sarve eva ālaya saṃskāraḥ kāryaḥ pratyagraḥ eva iti ca niyamya tam divya ālayam gāḍha ghaṭita argala dvāram parityakta aśeṣa pūjā utsavam ca kārayāmāsa 
NP_0.11^3	 loka ācārya prabhṛtayaḥ ca bahavaḥ tatra darśana guravaḥ tādṛśam vaiśasam acintita upanatam anusmṛtya durante duḥkha sāgare nimagnāḥ tam ca prativādinam sarva vidyā viśāradam vādāhava navaśūram aprakampyam ākalayantaḥ sabhām abhinavām kām api saṃgamayya tasya anarthasya kiñcid api pratividhānam cintayāmāsuḥ tasmin mahati sadasi viduṣām saṃpradāya ācāryaḥ śrīmān loka ācāryaḥ sarveṣām sabhā sadām avadheya vacanaḥ samarthām abhyarhitām vācam ādade bhoḥ bhāgavata pradhānāḥ balavantam paripanthinam parāṅmukhīkartum upāyaḥ kaścid atra me pratibhāti sa tāvat ucyamānaḥ bhavadbhiḥ anumanyatām asti kila kāñcyām nagaryām veṅkaṭanātha āryaḥ nāma viduṣām prathamaḥ 
NP_0.11^4	 sa hi vṛṣa śaila nāthasya ghaṇṭā aṃśaḥ eva avatīrṇaḥ iti tattva vidām grahaṇam soyam pañca varṣa deśīyaḥ śiśuḥ eva san nija mātulena vādi haṃsa ambu vāhena ātreya rāma anuja ācāryeṇa śārīraka bhāṣya grahaṇāya varada guru sakāśam gacchatā priya bhāgineyena nītaḥ tatra bhāṣya viṣaye prasaktān bahūn saṃdeha śṛṅkhalā granthīn visraṃsayan= tayā tatra samavetayā prajñā vṛddha pariṣadā apūrva prasāda vismaya citrita cittayā sa bahu mānam avalokitaḥ śrīmatā ca vara da guruṇā śrī bhagavat rāma anuja siddhāntasya daivāt saṃprati saṃjātam avalambanam iti baddha āśvāsena apratiṣṭhāpita veda antaḥ pratikṣapta bahis mataḥ bhūyāḥ traividyamānyaḥ tvam bhūri kalyāṇa bhājanam 
NP_0.12	 a iti āśiṣam prayuñjānena aasya kumārasya svatas pratibhāta samasta śāstra artha sārasya vidyā saṃskāra mātra phalaḥ guru upadeśaḥ bhaviṣyati na tu jñāne kaścid api śakti leśaḥ ādheyaḥ bhavati bhagavān api hi devakīnandanaḥ vidyā grahaṇāya sāṃdī pineḥ ācāryasya sakāśe guru kula vāsam agrahīt kim ca asya śaiśavaḥ eva ayam prajñā prakarṣaḥ dāśaratheḥ iva vikramati śayaḥ janma siddhaḥ na asau puruṣa antara dṛṣṭi viṣayam prāpayitum yuktam sa abhyasūyāḥ sa vismāyāḥ vā dṛśaḥ na asmin bāla vayasi patitum arhanti dṛṣṭi doṣaiḥ hi viṣa analaiḥ iva prasaradbhiḥ taravaḥ iva avalāḍhāḥ kati nāma mahā guṇāḥ puruṣāḥ sva guṇaiḥ lokam anupakṛtya eva astam gatāḥ bhavān eva amum sarva śāstreṣu kṛta prajñam kartum arhati śrī bhagavat rāma anuja siddhāntasya eṣa jayadhvajaḥ samucchrīyatām a iyā ādiśya śiśuḥ asau nija mātule vādi haṃsa ambuda ācārye nyāsīkṛtaḥ 
NP_0.13^1–0.13^2^1	 atha asau vayasā viṃśati varṣa deśīyaḥ eva san sarvatomukha prasṛta prabodha tayā pareṣām anabhibhavanīyaḥ saṃvṛttaḥ evam akṣayya pratibhā draviṇena sarveṣu api ca tantreṣu nirāmayam panthānam avagantum prasādayitum ca alaṅkarmīṇena ca ācāryeṇā sārdham kadācid kāñcī nagare devadevasya bhagavataḥ śrī devarājasya vaiśākha māsike yātrā mahā utsave vidvat saṃvāda kutūhalitayā samāgataḥ sarva pathīna vaiduṣī vibhavaḥ prabandha ratna praṇetā ca akhila śāstreṣu vidyā araṇya iti kṛta praśasti nāmadheyaḥ mādhava ācāryaḥ nāma veda bhāṣya kṛt vāda āhave lagnaḥ niraṅkuśa niśita tarka śara āsāra varṣiṇaḥ ācāryasya agratas pratyavasthātum akṣamaḥ vismaya bahu māna bharita manāḥ vijaya nagaram prayātaḥ sva śiṣyasya rājñaḥ tam artham yathāvṛttam āvedya tathāvidha vidvat ratna darśana utkaṇṭhā tvaritasya prabhoḥ prārthanayā chatra cāmara prabhṛti samasta rāja paribarha paribṛṃhitam rāja aupavāhya puraḥsaram pradhāna saciva hasta arpita sa bahu mānasamāhvāna lekham ca caturaṅga balam praṇīyaḥ prārthitaḥ vairāgya pañcakam tasya pratyuttarayāñcakāra 
NP_0.13^1–0.13^2^2–1.1.1	 tena ca mādhava ācāryeṇa svīye sarva darśana saṃgrahe rāma anuja darśanam upakṣipatā atat uktam veṅkaṭa nāthena tattvam uktāka kalāpe a iti upakramya patyuḥ saṃyaminām praṇamya caraṇau tad pāda koṭīrayoḥ saṃbandhena samidhyamāna vibhavān dhanyān= tathā anyān gurūn śuddham saṃśrita bādarāyaṇa tanoḥ nārāyaṇasya ukti bhaḥ śrīmān veṅkaṭa nāyakaḥ sthiti padam nirmāti nīteḥ śubham vidyā sthāneṣu dharmyeṣu gaṇyate nyāya vistaraḥ sa ca viplau= itaḥ taiḥ taiḥ tatas atra pariśodhyate 
NP_1.1.2^1	 gautama sūtra bahiṣkāra pakṣaḥ yadi api kathañcid ākṣa pādam sat pakṣe nikṣeptu śakyam na ca kaṇabhakṣa pakṣa nikṣepa vat kleśaḥ na api tad kartā gautamaḥ tāmaseṣu paripaṭhyate na api ca vipralambhaka tva khyātiḥ tathā api brahmasūtra kāra ādi bahiṣkṛta tvāt na atīva vayam ādriyāmahe na khalu ārṣa tva ādibhiḥ tad ādaraḥ atiprasaṅgāt prājñānām prathamena eva guruṇā hi svayam purā lokāyata matam proktam loka viplava kāraṇam athavā pitāmahaḥ eva atra pramāṇam yaḥ indra virocanāyoḥ cārvāka matam upadiṣṭavān tathā gautamaḥ api saṃbhāvyate atha apikāṇāda śākī a pāṣaṇḍaiḥ trayī dharmaḥ vilopitaḥ tridaṇḍa dhāriṇā pūrvam viṣṇunā rakṣitā trayī iti smṛteḥ bahavaḥ puruṣāḥ rājan sāṃkhya yoga vicāriṇaḥ 
NP_1.1.2^2	 na ete icchanti puruṣam ekam kuru kula udbhavaḥ samāsena tu tat vyāsaḥ puruṣa aikātmyam uktavān iti mahābhārata ukteḥ ca yuktam tad tad bahiṣkāraḥ iha tu na tathā iti ced na tulya nyāyatayā vacanasya upalakṣaṇa artha tvāt na khalu tat vā tādṛś vā iti kaścid viśeṣaḥ yadi api kāśa kuśā avalamba nyāyena pakṣa antarāt ādhikyam asya pakṣasya atha api na tad vedānta saṃnidhau na khalu maśakāt baliṣṭhaḥ api mātaṅgaḥ kaṇṭhīravam uparuṇaddhi yat akṣapādaḥ pravaraḥ munīnām śamāya śāstram jagataḥ jagāda ku tārkikā jñāna nivṛtti hetuḥ kāriṣyate tasya mayā nibandhaḥ iti vākyam akṣapāda pakṣa pātena uktam iti anāstheyam uktam ca pūrva ācāryaiḥ kāṇāda mākṣa pādam vā kāpilam tantram eva vā 
NP_1.1.2^3	 tantrāṇi etāni sarvāṇi na tantrāṇi ātma nirṇarya iti atas eva hi etena śiṣṭa aparigrahāḥ api vyākhyātāḥ iti sūtre bhāṣitam etena veda aparigṛhīta sāṃkhya pakṣa kṣapaṇena śiṣṭāḥ ca veda aparigṛhītāḥ kaṇa bhakṣa akṣa pāda kṣa paṇa kabhipakṣāḥ kṣapitāḥ veditavyāḥ iti na ca sūtra nibaddham sarvam vidyā sthānam iti niyamaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ na ca ekaḥ eva ekasya vidyā sthānasya sūtrakṛt iti api vā ṛṣiḥ iti eva vā rāja ājñā anyaiḥ api ca tad karaṇa darśanāt pramāṇa śabdasya bhāve karaṇe ca vyutpattiḥ evam ca pramā eva pramāṇam iti eke pramākaraṇam eva iti apare tayoḥ anyatarat iti anye yathā avasthita vyavahāra anuguṇam jñānam pramāṇam yat ajñānāt saṃsāraḥ yat jñānāt tad nivṛttiḥ tat prameyam mumukṣubhiḥ prakarṣeṇa meya tvāt 
NP_1.1.2^4	 tat dvividham dravya adravya bhedāt sāmānyatas vā pramā viṣayaḥ prameyam āgantuka dharma āśrayaḥ dravayam atathābhūtam adravyam dravyam dvedhā jaḍam ajaḍam iti jaḍam ca dvedhā prakṛtiḥ kālaḥ iti ajaḍam ca tathā pratyak parāk iti pratyak api dvividham jīvar iśvaraḥ iti parāk api tathā dharma bhūta jñānam nitya vibhūtiḥ ca iti athavā dravyam dvividham ātmān ātma bhedāt tredhā vā bhoktṛ bhogya niyantṛ śruti anusārāt ṣoḍhā vā triguṇa kāla jīva īśvara śuddha sattvam ati bhedāt asvayaṃpraka aṃśam jaḍam svayaṃprakāśam ajaḍam miśra sattva āśrayaḥ prakṛtiḥ kālaḥ kṣaṇa lava ādi vyavahāra hetuḥ svasmai bhāsamānam pratyak 
NP_1.1.2^5	 parasmai bhāsamānam parāk paratantra cetanaḥ jīvaḥ svatantrar iśvaraḥ artha prakāśaḥ buddhiḥ prakṛti vyatirikta tve sati sattva āśrayaḥ nitya vibhūtiḥ adravyam anekadhā sattva śabda ādi vaicitryāt ekam vā itara viśiṣṭam prādhānyataḥ prameyam param brahma itareṣām sva niṣṭha brahma eka niṣṭha tvāt tasya eva ca tathā tvena mumukṣubhiḥ prakarṣeṇa meya tva śruteḥ avyavasthita vyavahāra kāraṇam jñānam saṃśayaḥ ayathā vyavahāra kāraṇam jñānam viparyayaḥ saṃskāra mātra jam jñānam smṛtiḥ tad vyatiriktam jñānam anubhavaḥ puruṣa pravṛtti uddeśyam prayojanam vyāpti adhigama sthānam dṛṣṭāntaḥ prāmāṇika tva abhimataiḥ parigṛhītoḥ athaḥ siddhāntaḥ 
NP_1.1.2^6	 para artha pramāṇa prayoga vākya avāntara vākyāni avayavāḥ vyāpya aṅgīkāreṇa vyāpaka aniṣṭa prasañjanam tarkaḥ tarka anugṛhīta pramāṇa pūrvaka tattva avadhāraṇam nirṇayaḥ vīta rāga kathā vādaḥ pakṣa dvaya sādhanavatī vijigīṣu kathā jalpaḥ pratipakṣa sthāpana hīnā tu sā vitaṇḍā hetu aṅga eka deśa vikalāḥ hetvābhāsāḥ avivakṣita śabda artha āropeṇa dūṣaṇam chalam sva vyāpi dūṣaṇam jātiḥ kathakā śakti liṅgam nigraha sthānam iti etādṛśāni vākyāni kim na sūtrāṇi syuḥ tat iha saṃkṣiptam lakṣaṇa ādi vākyam sūtram tad udāharaṇa ādi vākyam tu bhāṣya ādikam iti vibhāvya saṃtoṣṭavyam na ca pūrva prābalya vyavasthā tad pūrva saṃbhavāt vārtikasya ca anavatāra prasaṅgāt vyākaraṇa ādiṣu anyathā karaṇa svīkārāt ca 
NP_1.1.2^7	 na ca jaimineḥ pramāṇa lakṣaṇa ādiṣu audāsīnya mātreṇa gautama ukteṣu kāśyapa ukteṣu vā niḥśeṣa anumati siddhiḥ iti mantavyam anya para tayā loka prasiddha upajīvanāt para kalpita taṭāka upajīvana vat karma kāṇḍa vṛtti kāra ādayaḥ api hi losiddhām pramāṇa ādi vyavasthām yathāyatham anyathā saṃjagṛhuḥ atas yāvat iha yukti yuktam tāvat upajīvyate na khalu taṭāka sthaḥ paṅkaḥ api apaṅkila buddhibhiḥ ta tat avagāhibhiḥ upajīvyate atas siṃha vana gupti nyāyena yathā avasthita nyāya anugṛhītam vedam veda anumatam ca nyāyam anusarāmaḥ na punar nyāya mātram yat tu jñāta saṃbandhasya ityādi grantham upādāya anantaram uktam śrī viṣṇu citteḥ vyāpti dhīgarbha anubhavaḥ anumānam iti arthaḥ 
NP_1.1.2^8	 nyāya śāstre tu tad viśeṣa nirṇayaḥ iti tat api tad nirūpaṇa adhikṛta vidyā sthāna khyāpana param pramāṇa ādi sūtram upādāya vyācakṣāṇaiḥ tad pakṣa niṣṭhaiḥ api pūrvaiḥ kvacid sūtrāṇi nirākṛtāni tat nyāyasya na asmāsu sarpamāraḥ na api daṇḍa nivāraṇam tatas ca yathālokam yathāvedam laukike vaidike api ca yaḥ vaktā sa parigrāhyaḥ prāktanaḥ adyatanaḥ api vā vivakṣita artha avaiśadyam vyākula tvam apūrṇa tā ullokatā iti amī doṣāḥ guṇa koṭau jaḍaiḥ kṛtāḥ bhagavat na artha munibhiḥ nyāya tattva samāhvayā avadhīrya akṣa pāda ādi nyabandhi nyāya paddhatiḥ tad arvāgbhiḥ tathā ācāyaiḥ yatheṣṭam matam āsthitaiḥ praṇinye bahudhā taiḥ taiḥ pramāṇa ādi vicāraṇā tat ayam bhāṣya svaḥsa siddhaḥ bahiṣkāra pakṣaḥ 
NP_1.1.3^1	 gautama sūtra svīkāra pakṣaḥ aṅgīkāra kāṅkṣiṇām akṣapādīyam api asmat ukta ekānta tayā sthāsyati tathā eva sthāpayiṣyāmaḥ atas vayam api mahatām ayukta artha tātparya kalpanena na aparādhyema nyūna adhika viruddha vyapadeśa ādīnām alakṣaṇa lakṣaṇa uktīnām ca adhyāhāra ani aparyāmyām tad bhakteḥ api nirvāhāt tathā asmin yatra sphuṭaḥ śruti smṛti śārīraka virodhaḥ saḥ uddeśataḥ niruhyate yat tāvat sūtritam prathama adhyāye ghrāṇa rasana cakṣuḥ tvac śrotrāṇi indriyāṇi bhūtebhyaḥ iti atra jñāna indriya pañka upādānam na indriya antara pratikṣepa artham manasaḥ pṛthak prameya tayā uddeśāt anantaram eva ca yugapad jñāna anutpattiḥ manasaḥ liṅgam iti lakṣaṇa karaṇāt abhyupagama siddhānta nyāyena ca tad indriya tva parīkṣaṇāt atas ca uktena samāna yogakṣema yukti pramāṇakaḥ karmendriya vargaḥ upalakṣaṇīyaḥ pravṛttiḥ vāc buddhi śarīra ārambhaḥ iti sūtre vācaḥ kaṇṭha ukteḥ pāṇi ādi catuṣṭayasya śārīra vyāpāra karaṇa tayā sūcanāt iti 
NP_1.1.3^2	 śarīrake tu sapta gateḥ viśeṣita tvāt ca iti pūrva pakṣam upakṣipya asādhayat ca hasta ādīnām api indriya tvam bhagavān bādarāyaṇaḥ hasta ādayaḥ tu sthite atas na evam iti bhūtebhyaḥ iti ca na upādāna abhiprāyam ahaṅkāra upāttānām āpyāyaka bhūta vivakṣayā api tad upapatteḥ tathā ca veda artha saṃgrahe evam āhaṅkārikāṇām indriyāṇām bhūtaiḥ ca āpyāyanam mahābhārataḥ ucyate iti samādhānam ṛṣi antara vākyasya api samāna nyāyasya nirvāha artham paraspara viruddha pramāṇa vākyeṣu tātparya viśeṣa parikalpanayā parihāraḥ eva hi paṇḍita kṛtyam anitya manaḥ vādibhiḥ api hi anna mayam hi somya manaḥ iti śrutiḥ āpyāyana para tayā eva yojyā tulyam idam anyatra api iti yat tu bādhanā lakṣaṇam duḥkham tad atyanta vimokṣaḥ apavargaḥ iti tatra duḥkha atyanta nivṛtteḥ apavarga tvam sarva aṅgīkṛtam na ca tatra ānandaḥ śrautaḥ kaṇṭha uktyāḥ pratiṣidhyate 
NP_1.1.3^3	 tad abhiprāye ca ananyathā siddham kim api na liṅgam paśyāmaḥ atas eva hi bhūṣaṇa mate nitya sukha saṃvedana saṃbandha siddhiḥ apavarge sādhitā etena tasmāt sarva duḥkha vimākṣaḥ apavargaḥ iti caturtha adhyāya vākyam api nirvyūḍham tatra api ānanda niṣedha abhāvāt yat ca śārīraka dvitīya adhyāya viruddham iha dvitīya adhyāye avayavi samarthanam iva ābhāti tat api tad eka artham yojayitum śakyam tathā hi na ca eka deśa upalabdhiḥ avayavi sadbhāvāt sādhya tvāt avayavini saṃdehaḥ sarva agrahaṇam avayavi a siddheḥ dhāraṇa ākarṣaṇa upapatteḥ ca senā vana vat grahaṇam iti ced na atīndriya tvāt aṇūnām iti etāni hi tad sūtrāṇi na tāni virudhyante senā vana ādi vyāvṛtta avaya vyārambhaka tayā tad asamavāyi kāraṇa tva abhimata avasthā viśeṣa āpannaḥ saṃghāta viśeṣa eva avayavi śabdena nirdiṃśyate iti avirodhāt tāvatā eva upalambha vyavahāra viśeṣa ādeḥ carita artha tvāt 
NP_1.1.3^4	 atīndriya aṇu vacanam api pradīpa avayavānām iva aindriyikāṇām eva avasthā viśeṣeṇa atīndriya tva abhyupagamāt aviruddham avyaktam eva hi triguṇa dravyam avasthā viśeṣādravyaktam bhavati iti āgamikāḥ pratyekam upalambha ayogyānām api saṃhati viśeṣa rūpa avasthā bhedāt aindriyika tva tad tāratamya ādikam himānī cūrṇa puñja ādiṣu anārabdha a= ayaviṣu loka siddham upamāna ākhya pramāṇa antara samarthanam tu nyāya eka deśibhiḥ eva upamānasya anumāna antarbhāva pratikṣepa mātra para tayā nirvyūḍham yat ca pūraṇa pradāha pāṭana anupalabdheḥ ca saṃbandha abhāvaḥ iti śabda artha saṃbandha abhāvam upakṣipya pariharatā śabda artha vyavasthānāt apratiṣedhḥ na sāmayika tvāt śabdāt arthe pratyayasya ityādinā sāmayika tvam uktam tat api saṃpratipanna sāmayika tva dvārāḥ anumāna ādi vilakṣaṇa saṃbandha viśeṣa khyāpana artham iti yojyam anādi nidhana avicchinna saṃpradāya veda vartinām padānām manu ādi vacana viruddha sāṃketika tva upapādana kpti asaṃbhavāt 
NP_1.1.3^5	 yat ca mantra āyurveda prāmāṇya vat ca tad prāmāṇyam āpta prāmāṇyāt iti etat api anādi nidhanasya eva vedasya pratikalpam īśvareṇa āptatamena yathāpūrvam pravartanam abhisaṃdhāya iti sugamam varṇa anitya tva varṇanam tu na śruti ādi viruddham pratyuta anukūlam eva śārīraka devata adhikaraṇe varṇa anitya tvam abhyupagamya eva hi atas eka ca nitya tvam samāna nāma rūpa tvāt ca avṛttau= api avirodhaḥ darśanāt smṛteḥ ca iti veda nitya tvam sādhitam yat tu jaiminīye śabda adhikaraṇe varṇa nitya tva samarthanam vyācakhyuḥ sa tu vyākhyātṝṇām eva aparādhaḥ asāṃketika vācaka ākāra nitya tva paratvena anya paratvāt tasya adhikaraṇasya yat ca dvitīya adhyāya ante vyakti ākṛti jātayaḥ tu padārthaḥ iti uktam tatra api na vaiśeṣika abhyupagata jāti svīkāre liṅgam paśyāmaḥ na hi atra dravya guṇa ādi padārtha parisaṃkhyānam kriyate te vibhakti antāḥ padam iti pratipādita pada vācya pradarśana paratvāt 
NP_1.1.3^6	 anantaram catisṛṇām eva lakṣaṇam āha vyaktiḥ guṇa viśeṣa āśrayaḥ mūrtiḥ ākṛtiḥ jāti liṅga ākhyā samāna prasava ātmikā jātiḥ iti iha tu vastu svarūpa nirūpita svarūpa viśeṣaka dharma svarūpa nirūpaka dharma viṣaya tayā yathāsaṃbhavam yojyam atas na dvitīya adhyāye api vedānta virodhaḥ tṛtīye darśana sparśanābhyām ekārtha grahaṇāt iti ādikam bāhya antar indriya ādinirūpaṇa ādikam ca atyanta upayuktam na ca manaḥ nitya tva ādikam tatra sūtritam yena tad utpatti ādi śruti kopaḥ yat ca atra uktam gandha kleda pāka vyūha avakāśa dānebhyaḥ pāñcabhautikam śruti prāmāṇyāt ca iti etat eva yathāśrutam siddhānta tayā svīkāryam yat api gandha rasa rūpa sparśa śabdānām sparśa paryantāḥ pṛthivyāḥ ap tejaḥ vāyūnām pūrva pūrvam apohya ākāśasya uttaraḥ iti guṇa vyavasthāpanam tatra tu tathā eva abhyupagame api na vastu antara virodhaḥ 
NP_1.1.3^7	 tathā api ākāśa ādiṣu śabda ādeḥ eka dvi tri catuṣpañca krameṇa purāṇeṣu pāṭhāt ākāśa anupraveśāt anyatra śabdaḥ iti nirvāhe vārūvādi anupraveśāt uttarottareṣu sparśādiḥ iti nirvoḍhum śakya tvāt upalambha anvaya vyatirekābhyām vyavasthāpanasya api samatvāt gandha ādi sūtram pṛthivyāḥ te santi eva iti ayoga vyavacchedena nirvāhyam ākāśasya uttaraḥ iti atra tu tasya saḥ eva iti anya yoga vyavacchedena kati kati ca evam sūtrāṇi kliṣṭāni paraiḥ api niruhyante yat ca sva guṇāt na upalabhante indriyāṇi kasmāt iti ced sa guṇānam indriya bhāvāt iti atra na śabda guṇa upalabdheḥ iti uktam tatra api śrotra indriyasya ākāśa āpyāyitā tvāt āpyāyaka guṇasya tad guṇa tām paṭanailya pānīya saurabha ādi vat prakalpa uktam uttaram athavā yathāgamamāhaṅkārika tvam indriyāṇām ajānataḥ ca udye bhūta āpyāyita indriya pakṣe sthitvā eva idam uttaram gūḍha abhiprāyeṇa dadīyaḥ iti etat uktam bhavati bhavatā kim indriya guṇa upalambha abhāvaḥ ucyate kim vā tad āpyāyaka guṇa upalambha abhāvaḥ 
NP_1.1.3^8	 pūrvatra aṅgīkāraḥ eva uttaram śabda ādīnām anindriya guṇa tvāt uttaratra vyabhicāraḥ iti atas na vedānta virodha prasaṅgaḥ caturthe adhyāye pravṛtti rāga dveṣa ādi nirūpaṇam ātma nitya tva ādinā pretyabhāva ādi pratipādanam animitta bhāva utpatti sarva anitya tva sarva nitya tva ādinirūpaṇam ca atyanta anuguṇam avayavi prasaṅgaḥ ca prāc ukta nyāyena netavyaḥ pañcamaḥ tu jāti nigraha sthāna mātra upakṣīṇaḥ na kvacid tattvaḥ upakaroti vyavahāra aṅga vimarśa saundaryā saundarya ādikam tu vāstava lakṣya lakṣaṇa yukti ādi parāmarśa vaijñānikaiḥ artha sthiti mātra anusārāt anādaraṇīyam yat punar arvāgbhiḥ akṣa caraṇa pañcādhyāyyām kuśa kāśa avalambena kaṇa caraṇa kathām niveśya naigamikyaḥ padavyaḥ nirudhyante tatra tu nūnam saḥ eva gautamaḥ svayam antar prahasati iti svīkāra pakṣaḥ yat vā na atīva ca bahiṣkāraḥ na atīva ca parigrahaḥ sāṃkhya ādi vat iha api syāt samādhiḥ tauṣataṃṇḍulaḥ upajīvya bahutvena vidyā sthāna niveśanam viruddha aṃśa eka viṣayā sūtra ādiṣu bahiṣkriyā 
NP_1.1.4^1	 adhikāri vivecanam niyata adhikāraḥ ca ayam nyāya vistaraḥ adhikārāt ca niyataḥ syāt ayam nyāya vistaraḥ apratyavāyaḥ māhātmyāt dayāluḥ śāstram abravīt sarva adhikāram iti etat asamīkṣita bhāṣitam katham āgama vṛttāntam anadhīta āgamāḥ viduḥ niṣiddhe prerayan= tān vā katham kāruṇikaḥ bhavet na ca śakyā nara śiraḥ pāvitrya ādi anumākṣatiḥ vihāya āgamam akṣa ādyaiḥ dvidhā tatra api viplavaḥ śrutyām hi anadhikāri tvāt tad anyatra avyavasthiteḥ dharma kṣobhām umā bhaṅge katham śūdra ādayaḥ kṣamāḥ atha traivarṇikaiḥ ukte tu anyaḥ viśvasitī iti api svayam nyāya vicāre asya phalati anadhikāri tām pratyakṣa anumayoḥ yatra nityam vedānapekhatā tatra apaśūdra bhāṣya uktā śūdra ādeḥ api adhikriyā caturdaśā api sthānāni bhagavān dharma vidyayoḥ na spraṣṭavyāni śūdraiḥ iti abravīt āśvamedhike 
NP_1.1.4^2	 aṅgāni vedāḥ catvāraḥ mīmāṃsā nyāya vistaraḥ purāṇam dharma śāstram ca vidyāḥ hi etāḥ caturdaśa yāni uktāni mayā samyak vidyā sthānāni bhārata utpannāni pavitrāṇi pāvana artham tathā eva ca tasmāt tāni na śūdrasya spraṣṭavyāni kathañcana iti tasmāt etāni traivarṇikaiḥ adhyetavyāni tatra brāhmaṇena vidyā prāptaye dharma anuṣṭhānāya ca adhigantavyāni kṣatriya vaiśyābhyām dharma anuṣṭhānāya eva tathā śaṅkhena vidyā sthānāni anukramya uktam etāni brāhmaṇaḥ adhikurute sa ca vṛttim darśayati itareṣām iti evam eva dharma śāstra saṃgrāhakaiḥ samarthitam tatas ca yeṣām karma brahma mīmāṃsa avaseya tattva hita rūpa prameya cintā adhikāraḥ teṣām eva tātparya paryavasāyitayā dharma vidyā sthāna abhimata nyāyaṃvistara andhikā rapaḥ iti siddham 
NP_1.1.5^1	 prayojana nirūpaṇam pratyakṣa ādi pramāṇena śuddhiḥ padatad arthayoḥ māna meya ādi niyatiḥ nirdeṣa ukteḥ ca mānatā grāva plavana vākyāḥ dāvāni a paryam virodhataḥ citrā paśu phala tvāda avabādha dvāra saṃgrahaḥ anuvāda vidhāna ādi cintā prāpti ādi pūrvikā pratyakṣa ādiṣu asiddheṣu na kalpeta kathañcana evamādi upayogena munibhiḥ nyāya vistaraḥ veda anugrahaṇāt dharma vidyā sthāna tayā uditaḥ āgama ākhya pramāṇe tu saṃśuddhe nyāya vistarāt tad viśeṣasya mīmāṃsā sādhayet dharmam ānatām prameyasya api saṃśuddhiḥ antatas brahma cintanāt iha tasya niveśaḥ tu tādarthyādi prasiddhaye pramāṇam eva asya śāstrasya prādhānyataḥ viṣayaḥ 
NP_1.1.5^2	 tatra prekṣāvat adhi cikīrṣā siddhi artham prameya tattva jñānam hāna upādāna dvārāḥ niḥśreyasa hetuḥ tat ca sa parikarāt pramāṇāt iti paramparayā prayojana jñāpanāya pradarśana mātram iha abhimatam atas pradhāna viṣaya tayā prameya ādi sādhaka tayā ca pramāṇam prameyāt api pūrvam ucyate tatra vyavacchedyatva aṅga tva ādi mukhena saṃśaya ādayaḥ api caturdaśa yathāyatham nirūpyante na ca ṣoḍaśa tve nirbandhaḥ atathātva viparyaya tva ādi upādhi antara adhīna saṃgraha vibhajanābhyām nyūna adhika uddeśasya api śakya tvāt upayoga anupayoga aviśeṣāt ca etāvat eva gautamasya api hṛdayam iti 
NP_1.1.6^1	 pramāṇa apramāṇa vyavasthāpanam asti tāvat idam pramāṇam idam apramāṇam iti prasiddhaḥ laukika parīkṣaka vyavahāra ghaṇṭā pathaḥ tad anādare tu nirāśraya tayā parīkṣaṇasya api anudayaḥ vyavahāraḥ hi jagataḥ bhavati ālambane kvacid na tad sāmānyatas na asti kathantā tu parīkṣyate sāmānya niścita arthena viśeṣe tu bubhutsite parīkṣā hi ucitā sva iṣṭa pramāṇa utpādana ātmikā na sarvasya apramāṇa tvam sva pakṣasya svatas kṣateḥ na sarvasya pramāṇa tvam sva pakṣasya anyatas kṣateḥ siddhi asiddhyaḥ sva pakṣasya siddhā loka vyavasthitiḥ tad siddhi asiddhyoḥ tvad pakṣaḥ na kathañcana sidhyati pramāṇena pramāṇasya bādhaḥ sva vyāhateḥ hataḥ apramāṇena tad bādhe sādhanam ca tatas na kim apramāṇāt pramāṇāt vā māna siddhiḥ na ced na tat yatas pramāṇataḥ tasya siddhiḥ sva para rakṣiṇī bādhā bādha vyavasthā api mānataḥ syāt ravi avasthitāt 
NP_1.1.6^2	 anyathā tu avyavasthāyāḥ na vyavasthā iti avasthiteḥ sarvatra anirṇaye na staḥ saṃśaya utpatti nirṇayau yathā tad koṭi tad siddhiḥ tathā anyatra api yujyate dharmi sādhāraṇa ākāra koṭīnām pūrva niścaye asau= ayam ayam vā iti hi āvirbhavati saṃśayaḥ sarvatra saṃśayaḥ tāvat na sarvasya api dṛśyate sarvam saṃdigdham iti te nipuṇasya asti niścayaḥ saṃśayaḥ ca na saṃdigdhaḥ saṃdigdha advaitavādinaḥ dūram gatvā api durvāraḥ saṃśaye nirṇayaḥ tava māna āmāna vibhāge atas sāmānyena vyavasthite kvācitka saṃśaya ucchittyai lakṣaṇam saṃpracakṣate tatra vyutpatti vivakṣā bhedāt pramitim tad karaṇam ca yatheccham pramāṇam āhuḥ iti avocāma āśraya prāmāṇyasya anādeśika tvāt āpta prāmāṇyāt āpta ukta tva hetoḥ prāmāṇyāt iti arthaḥ na hi vaktṛ prāmāṇyam vākya prāmāṇya upayujyate laukika vākyeṣu kintu kāraṇa doṣa abhāvaḥ dvidhā api pramitiḥ eva śodhyāḥ 
NP_1.1.7^1	 pramā lakṣaṇa parīkṣaṇam tatra asmadīyāḥ eva kecid anyathā ākhyātim icchantaḥ smṛteḥ prāmāṇyam anicchantaḥ samyak anubhavaḥ pramā iti lakṣayanti ubhayam icchantaḥ yathārtha jñānam pramā iti ubhayam anicchantaḥ anubhūtiḥ pramā iti evaṃprāyāṇi ca vādi antara uktāni lakṣaṇāni vayam tu brūmaḥ yathā avasthita vyavahāra anuguṇam jñānam pramā iti yathārtha khyātim akhyātim anyathā ākhyātim eva vā icchadbhiḥ na vimantavyam idam loka anusārataḥ smṛti mātrāṃpramāṇa tvam na yuktam iti vakṣyate abādhita smṛteḥ loke pramāṇa tva parigrahāt buddha āgama ādi tyāge ca na hetuḥ smṛti mūla tā viśuddha smṛti mūle api mānava ādau prasaṅgataḥ bhrāntim pramātaḥ bhindantaḥ na ca āhuḥ smṛti mānatām smṛti tvam eva hi vyaktam aprāmāṇyam bhavat mate pīta śaṅkha bhrama ādau ca na hi etat upapadyate cakṣuṣā eva hi śaṅkha ādeḥ pītim ādeḥ ca tatra dhīḥ tatas ca pratipattau vā vyavahāra udaye api vā 
NP_1.1.7^2	 tathā abhāvānyathā tvābhyām pramā bhra antita vyavasthitiḥ viparyaya ādeḥ vyāvṛttiḥ evam eva hi sidhyati yat kiñcid anyathātvam hi vaiparītyam iti iṣyate ātma khyāti ādi vādeṣu api anyathātvam avāritam bhrama pravṛtti bādha ādeḥ anyathā na hi saṃbhavaḥ evam sati anyathā dhīḥ tad sāmagrī vā api lāghavāt ayathāvyavahārasya hetuḥ iti avaśiṣyate sarvaiḥ api anyathā khyātiḥ dustyaja tvāt laghīyasī tad vādinā api avarjya tvāt tatas api akhyāti lāghavam svārasyam anyathā ākhyāta avakhyātau lāghavam sthitam iti darśayitum bhāṣye dvitayam tad anujjhitam yat nātha muni miśra ādyaiḥ yathārtha khyāti sādhanam tad loka buddhi anārohāt vaibhavam kecid ūcire mānāt rūpi ādi sattve api tayoḥ anyatarat dhruvam kārya akṣamatva agrahaṇāt tad kṣama tva graheṇa vā khyāti antarāṇām doṣāḥ tu tad tad siddhānta śīlane svayam eva unmiṣanti eva saṃgrahāt kiñcid ucyate tatra ātma khyātau tāvat anyat vijñānam asti iti dhīḥ anyaviṣayā na vā 
NP_1.1.7^3	 ādyer athasya api tadvat dhīra nyatra ekā eva dhīḥ bhavet saṃtāna antara vijñānam sva saṃtāne kṣaṇa antaram yā dhīḥ sādhayate sā hi svatas bāhyam vigāhate saha upalambha niyamaḥ saṃvidaḥ grāhya lakṣma ca bodhe api arthaḥ iva iti evam jñāna artha aikyam na tat bhavet doṣa ādi hetu jālasya mithyāve api yathā iṣyate adhiṣṭhānasya mithyāve api anivāryaḥ tathā bhramaḥ tatas mādhyamikasya eva pakṣaḥ tatra avaśiṣyate na ca tatra api nistāraḥ sarvathā anupapattitaḥ asattvam laukikam brūṣe lokottaram atha api vā na niṣedhaḥ nirupadhiḥ pūrvatra anyat na dhī padam catuṣkoṭi vimuktam ca tattvam prāmāṇikam na vā pūrvatra tāvatī sattā na ced tat dhīra sat matiḥ anyeṣām ca niradhiṣṭhā na khyātau atra asat eva bhavatām atra iti khyāyate na vā ādye siddham adhiṣṭhānam dvitīye khyāti apahnavaḥ kim ca sva netra niṣṭhyūtam timiram timira arditaiḥ keśa stabaka sādṛśyāt tathā bhāti evam īdṛśāḥ 
NP_1.1.7^4–1.1.8	 yadi api avidya mānor atho vidyamāna tayā sphuret tathā api asau= adhiṣṭhānam sva deśa ādau mitaḥ hi saḥ idantvena pratīter athe tadāropam pare viduḥ tasmin nidantu āropaḥ te phalatas tulya tā dvayoḥ anirvacanīya khyātau anirvācya tayā vastu nirucyeta na vā tvayā ādye virodhaḥ vividhaḥ dvitīye asmad mata sthitiḥ sat asat vyatirekaḥ api viruddhaḥ yadi gṛhyate sat asat rūpa tā kim nu pratītā tu na gṛhyate anuṣṇa aśīta vat tucchāt brahmaṇaḥ ca atirekitā sādhyeta khyāti bādha ādeḥ yadi siddham tat atra naḥ na ca viśvasya bādhaḥ api svarasāt upajāyate apratiṣṭhita yuktyā tu bādhaḥ brahmā api saṃspṛśet nāśāt saditara tvam ca nāśa kāle yadi iṣyate sva kāle yadi bādhaḥ syāt na aśasya api anirūpaṇam nitya tvena śrutānām ca keṣām cit na hi nāśitā bhāga asiddhaḥ tatas hetuḥ na ca aikyam nāśa bādhayoḥ nirviṣaya khyātau viṣaya alīka bhāva ādau khyāti antara parigrahaḥ anullekhaḥ tu rūpya ādi dhīriti uktyā nibarhitaḥ nigamanam tatas ca atra anyathā adhīḥ vā tad hetumatiḥ eva vā bhrāntiḥ vastu virūpasya vyavahārasya kāraṇam 
NP_1.2.9	 tat iha anyathā ākhyāti pakṣe viparyayasya saṃśayasya ca vyavaccheda artham yathā avasthita vyavahāra anuguṇam jñānam iti pramāṇa lakṣaṇe yathā avasthita ādi viśeṣaṇam akhyāti pakṣe api tad sāmagrī anupraviṣṭam jñānam tacachabdena vyapadiśyate tat ca tatra apramāṇam iti loka siddha tvāt vyavacchedyam eva tatra api pratyeka aṃśe yāthārthyam na vihanyate 
NP_1.2.10^1	 viparyaya nirūpaṇam tatra ādye pakṣe anyasya anyathā adhyavasāyaḥ viparyayaḥ dvitīye tu pakṣe sāmānyatas dharmi sphuraṇe sati apratipanna tad virodha viruddha viśeṣa adhyavasāyaḥ iti sa ca ayam anekavidhaḥ eka aneka viruddha viśeṣa sphuraṇāt tatra eka viśeṣa sphuraṇam yathā pītaḥ śaṅkhaḥ ityādi aneka viśeṣa sphuraṇam yathā ekam eva bhinnam abhinnam ca ityādi anekānta vādinām prapañcaḥ sat vilakṣaṇaḥ asat vilakṣaṇaḥ ca ityādya dvaita vādinām paraspara viruddha aneka viśeṣavatar idṛśasya viparyayasya saṃśayāt bhedaḥ mithas virodha abhimāna viraheṇa samuccita adhyavasāyaḥ dharma virodhe paraspara aviruddha aneka viśeṣa sphuraṇam yathā vipula tva eka tva viśiṣṭe candre alpa tva dvi tva ādi grahaḥ viparyayam eva dharma antara dharmī antara bhedāt anyathā khyāti viparīta khyāti bhedena kvacid vyavaharanti yathā pīta śaṅkha rajju sarpa bhramau tayoḥ ca rajaḥ tamasī mūlam iti gīyate yayā dharmam adharmam ca kāryam ca akāryam eva ca 
NP_1.2.10^2	 ayathāvat prajānāti buddhiḥ sā pārtha rājasī adharmam dharmam iti yā manyate tamasā vṛtā sarva arthān viparītān= ca buddhiḥ sā pārtha tāmasī iti yadi api rajju sarpa ādi bhrame rajju tva ādi dharma viparīta sarpa tva ādi dharma adhyāsaḥ eva tathā api svarūpa nirūpaka dharma tvena antaraṅga tayā dharmi vaiparīti avyapadeśaḥ śvaitya ādeḥ tu nirūpita svarūpa viśeṣaka tvam eva vivaraṇe tu evam uktam trividham ajñānam svarūpa ajñānam anyathājñānam viparīta jñānam iti svarūpa ajñānam nāma vastunaḥ apratipattiḥ anyathājñānam vastunaḥ vastu antaratayā bhānam yathā śukteḥ rūpya tayā viparīta jñānam tu yathāvat vastuni bhāsamāne yuktibhiḥ tasya anyathā upapādanam yathā jñātṛ tayā ahantvena ātmani bhāsamāne api kuyuktibhiḥ asyabhrānti topa pādanam kudṛśām iti adharma indriya doṣa dustarka abhyāsa durvyāpti anusaṃdhāna vipralambhaka vākya śravaṇa ādibhiḥ tattva āgraha sahakṛtaiḥ viparyayasya yathāsaṃbhavam udbhavaḥ 
NP_1.2.11^1	 saṃśaya nirūpaṇam sāmānya dharmi sphuraṇe sati apratipanna tad virodha pratipanna mithas virodha aneka viśeṣa sphuraṇam saṃśayaḥ yathā ūrdhva vastu mātra grahaṇe sati tad virodhitayā ananusaṃdhīyamānayoḥ mithas sphuṭa virodhayoḥ sthāṇu tva puruṣa tvayoḥ sphuraṇam ayam sthāṇuḥ vā puruṣaḥ vā iti mithas virodha agrahaṇe tayoḥ vikalpaḥ na syāt tatas eva ḍolā vegavat atra sphuraṇa kramaḥ iti eke ekasmin yugapad anyonya pratikṣepasya dhī viruddha tvāt atra caitanyasya viṣayeṇa dṛḍha saṃyogaḥ hi niścayaḥ 
NP_1.2.11^2	 tasya eva bahubhiḥ yuga pada dṛḍha saṃyogaḥ saṃśayaḥ iti ātma siddhi granthaḥ api na viruddhaḥ itarathāḥ jñāna arthayoḥ dṛḍha adṛḍha saṃśleṣa nirūpaṇa anupapatteḥ yugapad iti tu śaighṣa mātra param yaugapadya abhyupagame api adṛḍha tvam paraspara pratikṣepa prakāra viśeṣaḥ eva anyathā ayam ūrdhvaḥ vā sthāṇuḥ vā ityādi saṃśaya prasaṅgaḥ yadi api aviruddheṣu api keṣucid adharma ādi mūlaka virodha grahaṇāt keṣāñcid īdṛśaḥ api saṃśayaḥ saṃbhavati yathā ātmā jñānam vā jñātā vā iti jñānam dharmaḥ dharmi vā ityādi tathā api ābhimānikam paraspara pratikṣepi tvam tatra api asti eva 
NP_1.2.11^3	 asya ca samāna dharma vipratipattibhyām eva asādhāraṇa kāraṇābhyām adharma ādi sahitābhyām yathāsaṃbhavam udbhavaḥ tat uktam tattva ratna ākare kaḥ ca eṣa saṃśayaḥ katividhaḥ ca ekasmin dharmiṇi viruddha aneka viśeṣa avabhāsaḥ saṃśayaḥ sa ca dvividhaḥ ityādinā tatra samāna dharmaḥ sādhāraṇaḥ dharmaḥ tat janitaḥ yathā ūrdhva tva aviśeṣāt sthāṇuḥ vā puruṣaḥ vā iti agṛhyamāṇa bala tāratamya viruddha aneka jñāpaka upasthāpanam iha vipratipattiḥ sā ca sajātīya vijātīya ābhāsa rūpa dvi tri catur ādi jñāpaka bhedāt bahu prakārāḥ 
NP_1.2.11^4	 pratyakṣa tad ābhāsa vipratipatteḥ saṃśayaḥ yathā cakṣuṣā samukham pratibhāti darpaṇa talam sparśanena tu anyathā kim idam samukham nirmukham vā iti anumāna tad ābhāsa vipratipatteḥ yathā dhūmavat tvāt parvataḥ agnimān nirāloka tvāt anagniḥ iti atra sa agniḥ anagniḥ vā iti śruti vipratipatteḥ yathā bheda abheda vyapadeśābhyām jīvaḥ brahmaṇaḥ bhinnaḥ abhinnaḥ vā ityādi vādi vipratipatteḥ yathā vaiśeṣika aupaniṣada vākya dvaya śrāviṇaḥ madhyastha buddheḥ kim indriyāṇi bhautikāni āhaṅkārikāṇi vā iti evam pāmara ādi vākya vipratipatteḥ api nadyāḥ tīre phalāni santi na santi vā ityādi 
NP_1.2.11^5	 pratyakṣa anumāna vipratipatteḥ yathā cakṣuṣā pīta śaṅkha bhrame śaṅkha tvāt ca sita tva anumāne kim ayam śaṅkhaḥ pītaḥ sitaḥ vā iti pratyakṣa āgama vipratipatteḥ yathā kim aham arthaḥ sthūlaḥ aṇuḥ ve ati anumāna āgama vipratipatteḥ yathā kim paramāṇu upādānam jagat uta brahma upādānam iti eṣā diś kecid tu vipratipatti śabda mātre muhyantaḥ vādi vipratipattim eva vipratipattim manyante tat ayuktam viśeṣa abhāvāt yat uktam prajñā paritrāṇe sādhāraṇa ākṛteḥ dṛṣṭyā aneka ākāra grahāt tathā vipaścitām vivādāt ca tridhā saṃśayaḥ iṣyate iti tat api nūnam para anukāra mātram dvitīya tṛtīyayoḥ akaiḥ āśyāt grāhaka ava antara bhedasya atiprasaṅgi tvāt aprayojaka tvāt ca atra ca aneka ākāra grahaḥ nānā ākāra grahaḥ vivakṣitaḥ na tu aneka vyāvṛtta asādhāraṇa ākāra grahaḥ anantaram artheṣu eṣu aviśeṣeṇa dvi ākāra grāhidhī dvayam ityādinā tasya eva udāharaṇāt asādhāraṇa dharmāt api kecid saṃśayam āhuḥ yathā gandhavat tvāt pṛthivī nityāḥ anityā vā ityādi 
NP_1.2.11^6	 atra gandhavat tvasya nitya ātma ādi vyāvṛtteḥ kṛtaka tva ādi vat anitya tva smāraka tvam anitya ābādi vyāvṛtteḥ niravayava tva ādi vat nitya tva smāraka tvam iti viruddha viśeṣa dvaya anvita samāna dharmasya iva tad ubhaya vyāvṛtta asādhāraṇa dharmasya api saṃśaya hetu tvam upapannam iti tat ayuktam na hi tatra gandhavat tva ādinā saṃśaya utpattiḥ api tu vyatireka nirūpaṇa vilambā prāk eva gandha ādi viśiṣṭa dravyasya nitya anitya sādhāraṇa tayā bhāsamānaiḥ dravya tva ādibhiḥ eva tatra anyatara śiraḥ nirṇinīṣayā viśeṣaka dharma cintāyām tu gandhavat tvam ubhayān anvita tvāt ubhayoḥ api aniṣkarṣam iti etāvat eva cintyate kevala vyatireki bhaṅge ca etat viśadam bhaviṣyati 
NP_1.2.11^7	 gandhavat tvāt pṛthivī nityāḥ vā anityā vā iti tu yadā kaścid vyavaharet tatra api gandhavat tvam nitya tva anitya tvayoḥ anyatarasya prayojakam na vā iti eva saṃdehaḥ saḥ api dharma tva ādi lakṣaṇa samāna dharmāt eva atha nitya vyāvṛtta dharmavat tvāt anitya tvam anitya vyāvṛtta dharmavat tvāt ca nitya tvam puraskṛtya nityāḥ anityā vā iti saṃśate tadā api hetu bhūta dharma dvaya nimittaḥ ayam saṃśayaḥ na hi ekaḥ eva atra hetuḥ gandhaḥ tu tatra sāmānya rūpaḥ taṭa sthaḥ na tu hetuḥ vipratipattim api kecid samāna dharmaḥ eva antar bhāvayanti yathā hi ūrdhva tvam ubhaya sādhāraṇam tathā vādi parigṛhīta tva ādeḥ api sādhāraṇa tvāt vimati viṣayasya dharmiṇaḥ vā sāmānya veṣasya tad ubhaya sādhāraṇyāt iti 
NP_1.2.11^8	 tathā api sādhāraṇa dharmasya saha anubhūta sthāṇu tva puruṣa tva smārakatva vat vipratipatteḥ apisamāna dharma unnīti nirapekṣāyā eva tad upajīvyatayā tad pūrva bhāvinyāḥ sākṣāt tad viśeṣa smāraka tva siddheḥ dvaidham uktam asmābhiḥ punar ca ayam dvi tri catur ādi śirodhi karaṇa bhedāt bahuvidhaḥ yathā ayam sthāṇuḥ vā puruṣaḥ vā iti ghaṭaḥ satyaḥ asatyaḥ nirvacanīyaḥ anirvacanīyaḥ vā ityādi tathā imau sthāṇū vā puruṣau vā ete padārthāḥ satyāḥ asatyāḥ nirvacanīyāḥ anirvacanīyā vā ityādi 
NP_1.2.11^9	 yaḥ tu dvayoḥ anyatarasya cora tve siddhe ayam coraḥ ayam vā coraḥ iti saṃdehaḥ sa tu ayam coraḥ na vā iti evaṃrūpa saṃśaya dvaya samāhāraḥ yat vā yaḥ ca uraḥ saḥ ayam ayam vā iti ekaḥ eva atha vā cora tvam etat niṣṭham etat niṣṭham vā iti yadi api ubhaya vyatirikta puruṣa cora tva abhāvaḥ tayoḥ anyatarasya cora tve vā tātparyāt nirṇaya garbha tvam tathā api ubhayoḥ anyatara viśeṣa nirṇaya abhāvāt tasmin= aṃśe saṃśayaḥ eva na ca ekasya api jñānasya saṃśaya nirṇaya ātma tā virodhaḥ sarvasmin= api saṃśaye dharmyaśādau nirṇayasya dustyaja tvāt punar dvividhaḥ ayam anyatara koṭi pariśeṣa yogya tva tada yogya tva bhedāt 
NP_1.2.11^10	 pūrvaḥ yathā sthāṇu ātmake vastuni sthāṇuḥ puruṣaḥ vā iti uttaraḥ tu palālakūṭe dviradaḥ giri śikharam vā iti tatra nirūpakāṇām prāyaśas pūrvaḥ eva bhavati tena eva ca pravṛttasya pākṣikor athalābhaḥ yat vā nirīhasya eva kadācid dvitīyena saṃśayena viparyayeṇa ca pravṛttasya daivāt tad ātana artha saṃnipātena abhimata lābhaḥ iti punar api imau saṃśaya viparyayau sāmānya dharmiṇaḥ viśeṣāṇām ca anubhūyamāna tva smaryamāṇa tva ādi bhedāt bahuvidha āvūhanīyau= iti kiṃsajñakaḥ ayam vṛkṣaḥ iti evamādi rūpaḥ anadhyavasāyaḥ nāmānyaḥ jñāna viśeṣaḥ iti kecid tad asāram tasya saṃjñā ādi viśeṣa saṃdeha samanantara bhāvita dviśeṣa bubhutsa ātmaka tvāt 
NP_1.2.11^11	 athavā avacchedaka adarśanāt anavacchinna koṭi viśeṣaḥ saṃśayaḥ eva ūhaḥ tu prāyas puruṣeṇa anena bhavitavyam ityādi rūpaḥ eka koṭi sahacarita bhūyodharma darśanāt anutkaṭa ani akoṭikaḥ saḥ eva prāyas puruṣeṇa bhavitavyam iti puruṣaḥ eva iti abhiprāyaḥ ced yathocitam pratyakṣa anumāna ādiṣu anupraveśaḥ tarka rūpam ūham tu anumāne vakṣyāmaḥ trividham pramāṇam pratyakṣa anumāna śabda bhedāt bhagavatā m anunā api uktam pratyakṣam anumānam ca śāstram ca vividha āgamam 
NP_1.2.11^12	 trayam su viditam kāryam dharma siddhim abhīpsatā iti āha ca bhagavān śaunakaḥ dṛṣṭa anumāna āgama jam dhyānasya ālambanam tridhā iti bhāṣya kāreṇa ca pratyakṣa ādi trayam sva śabdena upādāya pramāṇa saṃkhyā vivāde api sarva abhyupagata pramāṇa anām ayam eva viṣayaḥ iti na kena api pramāṇena nirviśeṣa vastu siddhiḥ iti anyeṣām anādaraḥ kṛtaḥ sarva abhyupagata pramāṇānām iti ca para abhyupagama mātram dyotayati tatra prativādinaḥ ṣaṣ pramāṇa abhyupagamāt pratyakṣa anumāna āgamānām eva ca mithas bhedaḥ veda artha saṃgrahe viśadam upapāditaḥ yat tu mattaḥ smṛti jñārnam apohanam ca iti atra bhāṣyam jñānam indriya liṅga āgama yoga jaḥ vastu niścayaḥ iti tatra api yoga jasya pratyakṣasya prādhānyāt pṛthak vyapadeśaḥ antarbhāvam ca vakṣyāmaḥ uktam ca śrī viṣṇu cittaiḥ prameya saṃgrahe pramāṇa saṃkhyā vivāde api iti atra tri pramāṇa tvam bhāṣya uktam iti bhāṣye ca keṣucid kośeṣu yathārtha khyāti samarthanadaśāyām athavā kim anena bahunā upapādana prakāreṇa 
NP_1.2.11^13	 pratyakṣa anumāna āgama ākhyam pramāṇa jātam āgama gamyam ca nirasta nikhila doṣa gandha mana vadhika atiśaya asaṃkhyeya kalyāṇa guṇa gaṇam sarvajñam satya saṃkalpam param brahma abhyupagacchatām kim na setsyati kim na upapadyate ityādiḥ pāṭhaḥ dṛśyate yadi api smṛtiḥ api yathārthā pramāṇam iti vakṣyate tathā api pratyakṣa ādi mūla tayā tad aviśeṣāt pṛthak anuktiḥ uktam ca tattva ratna ākare pratyakṣa ādi mūlānām smṛtīnām sva sva mūle antarbhāva vivakṣayā pramāṇa tritva avirodhaḥ catuṣṭve ca vaidika anuvādaḥ darśitaḥ iti sa ca ācamanuvādaḥ pūrva upāttaḥ smṛtiḥ pratyakṣam aitihyam anumānam catuṣṭayam iti pratyakṣa ādi a viśeṣeṇa veda anuvādāt ca iti 
NP_1.2.11^14	 prajñā paritrāṇe tu smṛti prāmāṇya anabhyupagame api jñānasya tāvat karaṇa bhedāt cāturvidhyam eva uktam tatra indriya artha saṃbandhaḥ liṅga śabda grahau tathā saṃskāra unmeṣaḥ iti ete saṃvidām janma hetavaḥ iti yat tu tatra eva svayaṃsiddhiḥ tathā divyam pratyakṣam anum āgamaḥ pañca santi pramāṇāni jaimini vyāsayoḥ hṛdi ityādinā svayaṃsiddhi divyayoḥ pṛthak nirūpaṇam kṛtam tat pratyakṣa avāntara vairūpya bodhana abhiprāyam yathā uktam śrī viṣṇu cittaiḥ bhagavat prasāda labdha yogi pratyakṣam divyam iti 
NP_1.2.12^1	 pratyakṣa lakṣaṇam tatra sākṣātkāri pramā pratyakṣam sākṣāt tvam ca jāti rūpaḥ upādhi rūpaḥ vā kaścid jñāna svabhāva viśeṣaḥ sva ātma sākṣikaḥ jñāta kāraṇa ja jñāna smṛti tva rahitā matiḥ aparokṣā iti niṣkarṣe na avyāpya ādi prasañjanam prameya saṃgrahe tu evam uktam sākṣāt anubhavaḥ pratyakṣam sākṣāt tvam jātiḥ ityādi tattva ratna ākare api evam uktam aparokṣa pramā adhi akṣamā parokṣyam ca saṃvidaḥ vyavahārya artha saṃbandhi jñāna ja tva vivarjanam iti pārokṣyam ca evam uktam pārokṣyam vyavahārya anantargata vastu vedana apekṣā tad anantargata liṅga ādi apekṣā pārokṣyamanum ādau iti vara da viṣṇu miśraiḥ mānaya artha ātmya nirṇaye tu evam uktam aparokṣa pramā pratyakṣam pramāyā āparokṣyam nāma viśada avabhāsa tvam iti brūmaḥ kim idam vaiśadyam nāma asādhāraṇa ākāreṇa vastu avabhāsaka tvam ityādi sākṣāt tvam dvidhā nityam ca anityam car iśvara nitya jñāna ādi niṣṭham nityam asmad ādi jñāna niṣṭham tu anityam asmad ādi pratyakṣam dvidhā yogi pratyakṣam ayogi pratyakṣam ca iti 
NP_1.2.12^2	 tatra yogi pratyakṣam prakṛṣṭa adṛṣṭa viśeṣa jam tat yukta avasthāyām manaḥ mātra janyam viyukta avasthāyām tu bāhya indriya janyam api tat ca bubhutsā ādi pratiniyatam āgama eka siddham ca bhāvanā balaja mātram jagat kartari pratyakṣam pratikṣiptam śāstra yoni adhikaraṇe anyatra bhāṣya kāraiḥ eva sākṣāt yogi pratyakṣasya kaṇṭha ukteḥ tasya saṃbhavataḥ api āgamikeśvara jñāna mūlasya āgama anuvāda tva āpādanā śaktyā tatra audāsīnyāt dharma ādayaḥ kasyacid indriya grāhyāḥ prameya tvāt ghaṭa vat mīmāṃsakānām apratyakṣa tvāt vā asmad sukha ādi vat iti ādi anumānānām vipakṣe bādhaka viraha ādibhiḥ ābhāsa tvāt āgama bādha prasaṅgasya eva puraskāre tu āgamena eva caritārtha tvāt anyathā dharma ādayaḥ kasyacid cakṣuḥ grāhyāḥ iti vadataḥ bauddhasya kim prativakṣyasi yaḥ ca anuvyavasāye sa viṣaya vyavasāya pratyakṣa tām icchati tasya asmad ādiṣu api dharma ādi vyavasāya anuvyavasāye dharma ādi pratyakṣa tva siddhau katham tad atirikta yogi pratyakṣa anumā siddhiḥ tad vyavacchedena prayoge 
NP_1.2.12^3	 api saugata ukta cākṣuṣa tva ādi sādhana prasaṅga syāt iti sa ca adṛṣṭa viśeṣaḥ yoga abhyāsa tapaḥ cārya ādibhiḥ jāyate tasmāt ārṣa abhimatam api prakṛṣṭa adṛṣṭa jatvā viśeṣāt tatra eva antarbhūtam yathā uktam prajñā paritrāṇe atra indriya anapekṣam yat jñānam artha avabhāsakam divyam pramāṇam iti etat pramāṇa jñāḥ pracakṣate parameśvara vijñānam muktānām ca dhiyaḥ tathā saṃjaya arjuna vālmīki prabhṛti ārṣadhiyaḥ api tat iti indriya anapekṣam iti adivyenḥ diya anapekṣam iti arthaḥ atas eva hi gīyate divyam dadāmi te cakṣuḥ ityādi yadvā aparameśvara ādi vijñāna saha pāṭhā ādibhiḥ tathā eva mantavyam anantaram ca evam uktam svābhāvikasya jñānasya svatas sarva avabhāsinaḥ avidyā pratibandhasya pratibandhaḥ akṣa yogataḥ avidyā hānitaḥ mukta puruṣāṇām hi saṃvidām svābhāvika svarūpeṇa nikhila artha avabhāsitā pratibandhaka bhāvasya pratyuttambhaka bhāvinā pareṇa anugṛhītā dhīḥ ṛṣīṇām sarva bhāsikā iti 
NP_1.2.12^4	 mānasa pratyakṣam api asmad ādīnām na asti eva iti vṛddha saṃpradāyaḥ ātma svarūpasya tad dharma bhūta jñānasya ca svayaṃprakāśa tvāt sukha duḥkha icchā dveṣa prayatnānām tad tad hetu tayā abhimata jñāna viśeṣānatiḥ ekasya veda artha saṃgrahe samarthita tvāt nitya tva ādi viśiṣṭa asmad ādi anubhavasya śāstra ādi prasiddha tvāt pūrva anubhava ādi jñānasya smṛti rūpa tvāt ātma sukha ādi vyatirikta bahis viṣayeṣu tasya bāhya indriya anapekṣa pravṛtti anupapatteḥ iti śāstra yoni adhikaraṇa bhāṣyasya anvāroheṇa api upapatteḥ iti tatas ca ādivya bāhya indriya prasūtam jñānam ayogi pratyakṣam 
NP_1.2.12^5	 tat sāmānya adṛṣṭa āloka viśeṣa ādi saha kṛta indriya janyam dṛṣṭa sāmagrī viśeṣāt pratiniyata aviṣayam tat śrotra ādi indriyāsādhāraṇa kāraṇa bhedāt pañcadhā viṣaya indriya saṃbandhaḥ ca dravyeṣu saṃyogaḥ dravya āśriteṣu rūpa ādiṣu tu saṃyukta āśrayaṇam yathā uktam tattva ratna ākare atra vṛddhāḥ vidāmāsuḥ saṃyogaḥ saṃnikarṣaṇam saṃyukta āśrayaṇam ca iti yathāsaṃbhavam ūhyatām iti punar pratyakṣam dvidhā sa vikalpakam nirvikalpakam ca iti sa pratyavamarśam pratayakṣam sa vikalpakam tat rahitam pratyakṣam nirvikalpakam 
NP_1.2.13^1	 naiyāyika nirvikalpaka nirākaraṇam ubhayavidham api etat viśiṣṭa viṣayam eva aviśiṣṭa vastu grāhiṇaḥ jñānasya anupalambhāt anupapatteḥ ca bāla mūka tiryak ādi vijñānam api hi saṃjñā vikalpa rahitam api viśiṣṭa vastu viṣayam eva anyathā teṣām heya upādeya vibhāga pūrvaka pravṛtti śeṣa anupapatteḥ vipratipannam viśiṣṭa jñānam viśeṣaṇa jñāna pūrvakam viśiṣṭa jñāna tvāt surabhi candanam ityādi viśiṣṭa jñāna vat iti ced na eka sāmagrī vedya viśeṣaṇeṣu tad nirapekṣa tvāt svarūpa saṃbandha pakṣe svarūpa graheṇa eva saṃbandhasya api grahaṇāt tāvatā eva viśiṣṭa grahaṇa siddheḥ samavāya vāde api tasya eva gṛhyamāṇasya viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāva rūpa tvāt samavāya viśiṣṭa pratyaye tathā eva abhyupagamāt tad vaiśiṣṭya grahe ca guṇa vaiśiṣṭya grahasya āvarjanīya tvāt 
NP_1.2.13^2	 na ca samavāyasya sa vikalpakaika viṣaya tā iti vācyam nirvikalpake dharma vat dharmi vat ca tad saṃbandhasya api aindriyika tva aviśeṣeṇa grahaṇa saṃbhavāt yogyasya saṃnikṛṣṭa gṛhyamāṇa saṃbandhinaḥ saṃbandhasya agrahaṇa anupapatteḥ anyathā nityam tad agraha āpātāt prathama akṣa saṃnipāta jā buddhiḥ viśiṣṭa viṣayā buddhi tvāt saṃpratipanna vat ityādi api cintyam 
NP_1.2.14^1	 sa vikalpaka nirūpaṇam na ca sa vikalpakam na pratyakṣam iti vācyam sākṣātkāra ābādhādya viśeṣāt sahakāri viśeṣeṇa na vaijātyam prasajyate tad jātīye tu yat kiñcid vaiṣamyam saṃbhavet api yatra dṛśyeta vaijātyam tathā tatra abhyupeyate tāvatā na eva sarvatra bhavet etasya kalpanam kevala indriya jam ca api na kiñcid jñānam iṣyate sahakāri viśeṣām hi vibhidyante pratīndriyam atas saṃskāra saṃbhede api aparokṣa tva yogataḥ pratyakṣa tvam vikalpasya na kvacid vinivartate nirvikalpakam eka jātīyeṣu dravyeṣu prathama piṇḍa grahaṇam ityādi bhāṣyam tu udāharaṇa param yojyam 
NP_1.2.14^2	 atas eva hi śrī viṣṇu cittaiḥ uktam saṃskāra udbodha saha kṛta indriya janyam jñānam sa vikalpakam eka jātīyeṣu prathama piṇḍa grahaṇam dvitīya ādi piṇḍa grahaṇeṣu prathama akṣa saṃnipāta jam ca jñānam nirvikalpakam iti anyatra ca uktam kevala cakṣuḥ ādi indriya janyam nirvikalpakam ityādi yat tu uktam tattva ratna ākare viśeṣaṇānām svāyoga vyāvṛttiḥ avikalpake sa vikalpe anya yogasya vyāvṛttiḥ saṃjñitā tathā iti tatra api saṃskāra nirapekṣa tva sāpekṣa tvayoḥ pradarśana paratvam grāhyam pratyakṣasya ca evam vibhāgaḥ abhihitaḥ dvividham ca etat pratyakṣam arvācīnam anarvācīnam ca yugapad aśeṣa viṣaya sākṣātkārakṣamama narvācīnam tat yogi mukteśvarāṇām prabhāva viśeṣa adhīnam upapādayiṣyata iityādi 
NP_1.2.14^3	 atas eva kudṛṣṭīnām sat mātra grāhi pratyakṣam iti avilakṣa jalpitam nirastam krama yaugapadyādi dūṣaṇam tu bhrānti vikalpe api samānam bhrānti rūpaḥ api hi vikalpaḥ kṣaṇika tvāt na viramya vyāpartum alam na ca pūrva jñāna vārtām jānāti na ca svayam dharmi pratiyogi grahaṇa abhāve bheda grahaṇam manyase tathā api yadi kalpanā bheda viśiṣṭam yugapad gṛhṇāti kā pratyakṣe sarpa mṛtiḥ atas dharmi vat yogya tvāt jāti a ādi rūpa bhedaḥ api yugapad grāhyeḥ abhedaḥ iva bhedaḥ api svarūpataḥ pratītau na pratiyogi sākāṅkṣaḥ bheda vyavahāraḥ tu abheda vyavahāra vat tat sa ākāṅkṣaḥ atas prathamam eva bheda dhīḥ yuktā 
NP_1.2.14^4	 atas eva dharma dharmiṇoḥ dharmi pratiyoginoḥ anyeṣām ca pratītau= anyonya āśrayaḥ nirastaḥ tatas ca vyupatteḥ tad vyavahāre api na tad prasaṅgaḥ bheda śabdena vyavahārasya tu pratisaṃbandhi nirūpita ākāre vyutpanna tvāt tad apekṣā bheda tvam hi bhedānām pratiyoginā nirūpyam na tu jāti ādi lakṣaṇam sva rūpam yat grahaḥ yatra yat ārā upavirodhī sa hi tasya tasmāt bhedaḥ go tva ādi ca gṛhyamāṇam svasmin su a āśraye ca aśva tva ādi āropam nirūṇaddhi iti svasya sva āśrayasya ca svayam eva tasmāt bhedaḥ api ca pratiyogi sāpekṣa tva nirapekṣa tva lakṣaṇa viruddha dharma adhyāsena bhedāt svarūpa bheda grahaṇa aikyām na saṃbhavati iti vadan bheda duṣaṇa artham eva bhedam sādhayati iti sva vacana virodhaḥ iti 
NP_1.2.15^1	 śābda aparokṣa nirāsaḥ śabda janyam api pratyakṣam asti iti te eva varṇayanti tat api ayuktam vyāghātāt na hi parokṣa janana svabhāva tayā siddhā sāmagrī viśeṣa abhāve kvacid svabhāvam atipatet na ca eka jātīya sāmagrītaḥ prasūtam kāryam vicitram syāt ekayā evava sāmagryā sarva jātīya utpatti prasaṅgāt ekasya kāryasya viruddha jāti yoga prasaṅgāt ca daśamaḥ tvam asi ityādi dṛṣṭānte api tvam artha mātram pratyakṣam adaśamaḥ aham a iti pratyayaḥ hi na indriya svātantryeṇa udeti kintu puruṣa vacana anurodhena tad mūle api ced pratyakṣatā evam adharmavān= tvam asi a iti kārtāntika upadeśa ādau atādṛśaḥ aham asmia iti bodhe dharma ādeḥ api pratyakṣa tva prasaṅgaḥ tatas ca apratyakṣam iti jagati kiñcid na syāt pratyakṣa bhūtam yat kiñcid uddiśya viśeṣaṇa tayā eva sarvasya pratyakṣa tvā upapatteḥ pūrva avagata daśama bhāvam tu puruṣam pratyupadeśe bhāṣarāśi praviṣṭa maṣī nyāyena pūrva apara aparokṣaṇī nairantaryeṇa madhya varti śabda janya dhiyaḥ aparokṣa tva vyavahāraḥ kasyacid syāt vā na vā 
NP_1.2.15^2	 atas eva tattvam asya ādi śabdaḥ sva viṣaya gocara pratyakṣa jñāna janakaḥ svatas aparokṣa artha gocara tvāt daśamaḥ tvam asi saṃvid sva prakāśāḥ ityādi vākya vat iti ādi anumānāni nirastāni daśama tva svaprakāśa tva ādi viśiṣṭa ākāreṇa dṛṣṭānteṣu aparokṣa jñāna janana asiddheḥ tathā vigītaḥ śabdaḥ na sva vācya gocara pratyakṣadhī janakaḥ śabda tvāt saṃpratipanna vat iti ādi apipratiprayoktavyam upalambha virodha śābda pratyakṣa lakṣaṇa saṃkara ādi prasaṅgaḥ atra vipakṣe bādhakaḥ na evam pūrvasya śabda janya pratyakṣam antareṇa api yoga ja adṛṣṭa janita sākṣātkārāt praṇidhāna viśeṣa prasādita paramātma saṃkalpāt vā niḥśreyasa siddheḥ iti pratyakṣam cit acit mayam jagat idam yasya iti anuśrūyate yaḥ ca ananya dhiyām ananta vibhavaḥ pratyakṣatām aśnute yaḥ ca ekaḥ yugapad sadā svatas idam viśvam darī dṛśyate prājñam tam pratipanna mokṣaṇa vidhāt akṣam didṛkṣemahi 
NP_3.1.1	 atha anumodayam smṛtyā hetu tvena api saṃsthitm madhye tayoḥ ihetadānīm mānam śabdam pracakṣmahe anāpta anukta vākya janitam tad artha vijñānam tat pramāṇam kāraṇa doṣa bādhaka adarśanāt naca an āpta ukta vākyam pramāṇam kāraṇa doṣa bādhaka darśanāt na ca vākya tva ādibhiḥ bādhaḥ sva vacana virodhāt yadi bādhaka upanyāsa vākyam ayathārtham tadā katham bādhaḥ atha yathārtham tasya api pakṣīkāre tad bādhaḥ bahiṣkāre tena eva anaikāntyam na ca atiprasaṅgaḥ bhrānta ādi vākyānām doṣa mūla tvasya durapahnava tvāt atra tu tad abhāvāt utsvapnāyita ghuṇa kṣata akṣara ādīnām tu viśiṣṭa tātparya viraheṇa bodhaka tvepi anāśvasanīya tvāt vyabhicāra darśanāt ca nityepi vede nityeśvara śāsana ātmani tad tad artha tātparyāna pāyāt tasya ca atra abhāvāt kvācid ka doṣa darśanasya ca pratyakṣa ādau= api asamatvāt svatas paratas vā prāmāṇye ca tatas viśeṣa abhāvāt 
NP_3.1.2^1	 tat ca vedya aṃśe pratyakṣa atiriktam asākṣātkāri tvāt anumāna vat anumāna atiriktam pakṣa liṅga parāmarśa ādi adṛṣṭeḥ pada vākya tad saṃbandha ādīnām ca viśiṣṭa vākya artham pratyasiddha vyāptika tvena āliṅga tvāt dṛṣṭānta abhyupagame sarvatra aviśeṣāt vyutpattau ca svatantra tayā eva bodhaka tva siddheḥ atas eva vaktṛ jñāna anumāna abhyupagamepi śabda prāmāṇyam siddham āgamika buddhiḥ anumā pratyakṣa itara pramiti tvāt saṃpratipanna vat iti ced na ukta uttara tvāt anyathā śabda rasa gandha ādi buddhiḥ anumā acākṣuṣa pramiti tvāt saṃpratipanna vat iti api prasaṅgāt pratyakṣam anumānam ca śāstram ca vividha āgamam dṛṣṭa anumāna āgama jam iti manu ādi mahā ṛṣi saṃmateḥ ca śabda anumānayoḥ bheda udṛśyate na ca atra go balī vardanayaḥ antarbhāva adarśanāt āgāmonumānam saṃbandha grahaṇe sati eva bodhaka tvāt iti ced na bodhya bodhaka bhāva atirikta saṃbandha grahaṇa apekṣiṇī anumāna tva niyamāt 
NP_3.1.2^2	 na ca atra tad atiriktaḥ saṃbandhaḥ yat grahaṇam niyamena apekṣyeta anyathā saṃbandha sāpekṣa tayā tayoḥ pratyakṣa tvasya api su sādha tvāt iti na ca smṛtiḥ apūrva viṣaya tvāt pada saṃdoha viśeṣaḥ vākyam prāmāṇika pada vyavahāra viṣayaḥ padam tasya suptiṅanta tva ādi kalpanayā api vyaktiḥ kriyate atas eva hi anyathā anyathā prakṛti pratyaya ādikam vyākaraṇa antareṣu kalpyate tat ca na sāṃketikam saṃketayitṛ puruṣa asaṃbhavāt atas eva na bhāṣā antara vat tad klaptiḥ nitya veda gata tvāt ca yāni vaidikāni padāni tāni eva laukikanī iti veda śabdebhyaḥ eva ādau ityādi vacanāt api siddham bhāṣāt chandasoḥ tu katipaya śabdānām lakṣaṇa bhedaḥ tad tad ānupūrvī pratiniyama apekṣaḥ bhāṣā prayuktaḥ sarva upi vede kvāpi prayogavān veda eka niyataḥ śabdaḥ na anyatra iti vyavasthitiḥ uktam ca etat veda artha saṃgrahepi vaidikāḥ eva sarve vācakāḥ śabdāḥ ca ityādinā 
NP_3.1.3–3.1.4^1	 vākyam dvidhā pauruṣeya apauruṣeya bhedāt puruṣa svātantrya adhīna racanā viśeṣa viśiṣṭam pauruṣeyam tat dvidhā anvita artham ananvita artham ca ādyam yathā agniḥ uṣṇaḥ āpaḥ dravāḥ iti dvitīyam yathā agniḥ anuṣṇaḥ āpaḥ kaṭhināḥ iti atra eka deśinaḥ vadanti ananvaya āgrahāt anvita vyavahāraḥ kvacid jāyate iti atas eva laukika vākye dṛṣṭa vyabhicārasya na jhaṭati vākyāt vākya artha adhyavasāyaḥ yogya tā vimarśa sa ākāṅkṣa tvāt sāmānya yogya tā grahaṇepi vyakti yogyatāyāḥ vaktṛ jñāna anumāna m anteraṇa asiddheḥ iti prameya saṃgraha ādiṣu samarthitam tathā sat mātra grāhi pratyakṣa nirākaraṇāya śāstrasya anuvādaka tva prasaṅge vivaraṇa kāraiḥ uktam abuddha bodhana svarasasya śabdasya ātathātvam doṣaḥ iti abhisandhiḥ athavā anuvādaka tvam eva syāt na hi māna antara pratīterthe śabdaḥ pramāṇam 
NP_3.1.4^2	 tathā eva hi tasya vyutpattiḥ iti uktvā nanu anuvādaka tayā eva vyutpattiḥ puṃvākyeṣu ityādinā vaktṛ jñāna anumānam upapādya satyam daivāt tad anuvādaka tvam iti na abuddha bodhana svārasya bhaṅga prasaṅgaḥ yathā smṛti anumita vedasya anuvādaka tva ipi arthāt iti na mānatā bhaṅgaḥ ityādi uktam ca prajñā paritrāṇe pauruṣeya giraḥ śaṅkā grastāḥ na sahasā mitim janayanti na yāvat tad mūla mānānavagrahaḥ anumāya ca vaktuḥ tad mūla yogya pramā antaram tad ukta vākya liṅgena vākya artham anujānate anvita artha abhidhānāya yogyam vākyam idam sadā 
NP_3.1.4^3	 asau ca na anṛtam vakti saṃjñātva artham tat abravīt vaktṛ jñāna anumānena jñāta ajñāta sva vākyataḥ anvita artha abhidhāyi tva yogya tā mātra dhīrgirām parāmarśaḥ iti prāptaḥ na artha saṃsarga gocaraḥ māna antara avirodhi tvam yogyatā iti abhidhīyate nanu evam laukikam vākyam liṅgam ced liṅga vat tatas śabdaḥ gṛhīta saṃbandhāt tadvat asya api liṅgatā vyutpatti kāle vyutpitsoḥ liṅga dhīḥ na asti asaṃśayāt yathāvyutpatti śabdāḥ tu bodhakāḥ iti ced atas svatas eva artha bodhaḥ syāt iti na eva asya liṅgatā ityādi 
NP_3.1.4^4	 bhagavat yāmuna munibhiḥ tu āgama pramāṇye vaktṛ jñāna anumānam dūṣitam nigamitam ca tasmāt asti nadī tīre phalam iti evamādiṣu yā siddha viṣayā buddhiḥ sā śabdī na anumānukī iti ayam eva pakṣonusṛtaḥ vara da viṣṇu miśraiḥ tattva ratna ākarepya āgama prāmāṇya grantha upādāna pūrvakam prapañcitam etat apauruṣeyam tu sarvam anvita artham eva ākintu ādityaḥ yūpaḥ iti ādiṣu upacārataḥ nirvāhaḥ ākāṅkṣā satti vogya tāvanti hi padāni anvitam abhidadhati anvaye vā viśrāmyanti āditya yūpa padayoḥ pratyakṣa siddha sva artha bhedayoḥ ayogya tayā mukhya vṛtti parityāgaḥ 
NP_3.1.5^1	 vṛttiḥ dvidhā abhidhā upacāra bhedāt vyutpatti siddhārthaḥ eva vṛttiḥ abhidhā yathā siṃha śabdaspaya mṛgendre sā jāti guṇa ādi viṣaya bhedāt yoga rūḍhi tat samuccaya bhedāt ca bahuvidhāḥ mukhya artha bādhe sati tad āsanne vṛttiḥ upacāraḥ āsattiḥ ca dvividhāḥ mukhya artha saṃbandhaḥ tad guṇa saṃbandhaḥ ca iti tatra pūrveṇa pravṛttiḥ lakṣaṇā yathā gaṅgāyām ghoṣaḥ prativasati iti atra gaṅga śabdasya pravāha viśeṣa rūpa vācya saṃbandhini tīre evam lakṣita lakṣaṇā grāhyā dvitīyena pravṛttiḥ gauṇī yathā siṃhaḥ devadattaḥ iti atra siṃhma śabdasya śaurya ādi gūṇaṇyogini devadatte tattva ratna ākare tu evam uktam abhidhāna abhidheya tvam atas śabda arthayoḥ sthitam 
NP_3.1.5^2	 saṃbandhotra abhidhāḥ dvedhā bodhyā mukhya jaghanyatas abhidhārtha a= agatya ātmā śabdam vyāpārayiṣyataḥ śabda śakti nimittā sā sva arthe mukhya abhidhīyate sva artha abhidhāna dvārā syāt jaghanya artha antare matā iti tad vistaraḥ tatra eva dgaṣṭavyaḥ na ca gauṇala akṣaṇika prayogayoḥ avācya viṣaya tvāt avācya tvam saṃbandha sādṛśya mātra pravṛttepi ana ādi tvāt tatas eva vivakṣita sthale yathā aucityam prayoga upapatteḥ etāḥ sarvāḥ api vṛttayaḥ anvita abhidhāna vṛtti antarbhūtāḥ pṛthak padānām smāraka tvam eva abhihita anvaye hi padānām padārthe padārthānām vāvaya arthe padānām ca tatra iti śakti traya kalpanāgāra evam syāt vākya arthasya āśābda tva prasaṅgaḥ vā 
NP_3.1.5^3	 padārthe lakṣaṇa samāpteḥ pramāṇa prasaṅgaḥ ca naca anvitā abhidhānenyonya āśrayaṇam mithas smaraṇa mātra upajīvanāt yathā āhuḥ pada jātam śrutam sarvam smāritān anvita arthakam nyāya saṃpādita vyakti paścāt vākya artha bodhakam iti na api paunarukti ādi doṣaḥ tad tad aṃśa pratiniyata śakti tvāt na api vākya bhedaḥ eka pradhāna tayā sva artha abhidhānāt padārthaḥ eva vākya arthaḥ saṃsṛṣṭaḥ hi abhidhīyate iti uktam tathā nānā śabda ādi bhedāt iti ādhikaraṇe yadi api avedaḥ a aupāsīta a ityādayaḥ śabdāḥ pratyaya āvṛtti abhidhāyinaḥ pratyayāḥ ca brahma eka viṣayāḥ tathā api tad tad prakaraṇa udita jagat eka kāraṇa tva apahata pāpma tva ādi viśeṣaṇa viśiṣṭa brahma viṣaya pratyaya āvṛtti avabodhinaḥ pratyaya avṛtti rūpāḥ vidyāḥ bhindanti iti 
NP_3.1.5^4	 veda artha saṃgrahepi śodhakeṣu api asatyam jñānam anantam brahma a aānandaḥ brahma a ityādiṣu sāmānādhikaraṇya vyutpatti siddha an eka guṇa viśiṣṭhā eka artha abhidhānam aviruddham iti sarva viśiṣṭam brahma eva abhidhīyate iti atra eva pūrva bhāge samabhivyāhṛta pada antara vācyā anvaya yogyam eva itara pada pratipādyam iti anvita abhidhāyi pada saṃghāta rūpa vākya śravaṇa samanantaram eva pratīyate tat ca svarga sādhana tva rūpam atas kriyāvat ananyārtha tā virodhāt eva parityaktāḥ iti eṣām svārasyam anvita abhidhāne na ca atra para abhyupagamena uktam iti jñāpakam asti 
NP_3.1.5^5	 vara da viṣṇu miśraiḥ api satya jñāna ādi padānām akhaṇḍa eka rasa artha tve anvita abhidhāna anupapatteḥ ca ityādiṣu bahuṣu pradeśeṣu anvita abhidhānam eva māyā vādinam pratyuktam uktam ca āgama prāmāṇye anya anvitā abhidhāna ipi vyavahāra upapattitaḥ avaśya āśrayaṇīyā iyam anvita artha abhidhāyitā iti ārabhya tasmāt ākāṅkṣita āsanna yogya artha antara saṅgate sva arthe padānām vyutpattiḥ āstheyā sarva vādibhiḥ iti tattva ratnākarepi avaśya āśrayaṇīyā iyam anvita artha abhidhāyitā iti āhuḥ yāmunā ācāryāḥ padaiḥ eva anvita abhidhām iti ārabhya prapañcena upapādya upasaṃhṛtam ṣaḍbhiḥ pratīti pramukha upapattibhiḥ nirdhūta codyābhiḥ iha anvitā abhidhā 
NP_3.1.5^6	 siddhā padaiḥ na abhihita anvaya sthitiḥ viparyayāt iti akhilam samañjasam iti prajñā paritrāṇa nyāya su darśanayoḥ ca bahuśas uktam anvita artha abhidhāyi tvam śabda śakti nibandhanam vyutpatti avagatam pundhī doṣa tosya viparyayaḥ ityādinā nanu abhihita anvaya t yotakāni api vākyāni vidyante veda artha saṃgrahe tāvat evam bodhakānām pada saṃghātānām saṃsarga viśeṣa bodhanena vākya śabda abhidheyānām uccāraṇa kramaḥ yatra puruṣa buddhi pūrvakaḥ ityādi uktam tathā tatra eva prakṛti pratyaya rūpeṇa padasya eva aneka viśeṣaṇa garbha tvāt aneka padārtha saṃsarga bodhaka tvāt ca vākyasya iti bhāṣyepi śabdasya tu viśeṣeṇa sa viśeṣaḥ eva vastuni abhidhāna sāmarthyam pada vākya rūpeṇa pravṛtteḥ 
NP_3.1.5^7	 prakṛti pratyaya yogena hi padatvam prakṛti pratyayoḥ artha bhedena padasya eva viśiṣṭa artha pratipādanam avarjanīyam pada bhedaḥ ca artha bheda nibandhanaḥ pada saṃghāta rūpasya vākyasya aneka padārtha saṃsarga aviśeṣa abhidhāyi tvena ityādi uktam evam vyutpatti nirūpaṇe veda artha saṃgrahe siddha vastuṣu śabdasya bodhaka tva śakti grahaṇam atyanta sukaram iti upakramya apavarake daṇḍaḥ sthitaḥ iti vākye yādṛcchika vyutpatti prakāram upapādya tathā bālaḥ atā toyam anbaiṣā a ityādinā buddhi pūrva vyutpādanena tad tad padānām tad tad padārtheṣu eva bodhaka tva śakti grahaṇam upapādya punar api asya śabdasya ayam arthaḥ iti pūrva vṛddhaiḥ śikṣitaḥ ityādi ca uktvā evam eva sarva padānām sva artha abhidhāyi tvam saṃghāta viśeṣāṇām ca yathā avasthita saṃsarga viśeṣa vāci tvam ca jānāti ityādi uktam 
NP_3.1.5^8	 bhāṣyepi prathama sūtra pūrva pakṣa nirākaraṇe evam kila laukikāḥ śabda artha saṃbandham avadhārayanti mātā pitṛ prabhṛtibhiḥ ambā tāta mātula ādīn ityādinā pada vyutpattiḥ pūrvam upapāditā tatra ca teṣu teṣu artheṣu teṣām śabdānām prayogaḥ bodhaka tva nibandhanaḥ iti niścinvanti ityādi uktam punar ca vyutpanna itara śabdeṣu asya śabdasya ayam arthaḥ iti pūrva vṛddhaiḥ śikṣitāḥ ityādi yadi nāma anvita abhidhānam abhimatam tadā katham iva pada mātre vyutpattiḥ syāt yadi ca sā syāt katham anvitam abhidheyam vyutpatti vaiparītya prasaṅgāt tasmāt na anvitā abhidhānam eva siddhānte iti nirṇetum śakyam iti kecid 
NP_3.1.6	 anye tu bodhakānām ityādi vākyam anvite saṃsarga viśeṣa siddheḥ upapadyate pada vākya bheda abhidhānam api tad tad viśeṣa vaiśiṣṭya pradarśana mātra artham para abhyupagamat yotana artham vā pratyeka pada vyutpatti abhidhānam api anvita artha bodhana upayukta asādhāraṇa dvāra prakāśana mātram padārtham smārayitvā eva hi padāni vakya artham bodhayanti iti uktan smṛteḥ ca sva anubhūti mūla tvāt na śakti antara kptiḥ vyākhyātam ca bhāṣya ādikam anvita para tayā vivaraṇe śrī rāma miśraiḥ tathā ṣaṣ artha saṃkṣepepi śabdaḥ ca svatas śakyam anvita tayā bodhayati asaṃbhghavertha antaram iti hi vyutpattiḥ ityādi uktam atas nvita abhidhānam siddhāntaḥ iti evam anvita abhidhāna sāmarthyāt viśiṣṭa pratipatti anyathā anupapatteḥ ca padānām api viśiṣṭa abhidhāyi tvam siddham 
NP_3.1.7^1	 atas eva viśiṣṭa artha abhidhāyi tvepi viśeṣaṇam atre śaktiḥ iti api nirastam abhidhāyitvā atirikta śakti antara abhāvāt aparyavasāna vacanam api viśiṣṭa bodhana śaktasya viśeṣaṇa mātre sthātum aśakta tvāt viśiṣṭa anupraviṣṭam hi viśeṣaṇam pareparañjaka veṣam eva iti tādṛś ākāraḥ viśeṣya grahaṇam antareṇa durgrahaḥ tāvatā ca tad artham viśeṣya grahaṇam iti vyartham vacaḥ yathāprati iti vyavasthāpanasya eva yukta tvāt kim ca gavā ādi śabda abhihita go tva ādi artha svabhāvataḥ vyakti dhīrya di tadvat syāt niṣkarṣaka padeṣu api gavā ādi śabdāḥ jāti ādīn paratantrān pracakṣate tena āśraya pratītiḥ ced tat naḥ siddhaḥ samīhitam param katham avijñāpya pāratantryasya bodhanam vijñāpya yadi śabdasya tatra śaktiḥ na kim bhavet 
NP_3.1.7^2	 parasya paratantreṇa tathā buddhena bodhanam tad buddhyā paratantrasya bodhanenyonya saṃśrayaḥ para dhīnirapekṣam ced pāratantryam pratīyate na tena para buddhiḥ syāt niṣkṛṣṭa pratipatti vat pāratantryam svarūpam ced tulyam niṣkarṣakepi tat adhikam dharmi niṣṭha tvāt anyat na upalabhāmahe pada antara parāmarśa nirapekṣa pratītike nirūḍha lakṣaṇauvādāḥ paryāya avṛtti gocarāḥ vyakteḥ gauritya niṣkarṣāt niṣkarṣe tu ādi apekṣaṇāt niṣkarṣakeṣu adṛṣṭeḥ ca na jātyā vyakti lakṣaṇā ākṛtau= eva yaḥ śaktim śabdānām abhimanyate sattāyām eva kim tena sarveṣām na abhyupeyate atas gavā ādi śabdebhyaḥ viśiṣṭa viṣayā matiḥ śabda śakti prasūtā iti balāt abhyupagamyatām 
NP_3.1.8	 yat tu na loka vyutpatti haniḥ tatra eva śakteḥ iti ṣaṣ artha saṃkṣepe śrī rāma miśraiḥ uktam tat api tatra śakti abhāva pratikṣepa param asamāpta dhīḥ tu vedānta aśruteḥ bhramaḥ āpāta vyutpattyā śruteḥ tad pūrtiḥ iti anantaram abhidhānāt yat ca ātma siddhau yathā gavā ādi pada śaktiḥ ekabuddhi siddhepi sāmānya viśeṣa ātmake vastuni sāmānya aṃśena saṃbadhyate iti tat api para abhyupagata udāharaṇam anya artham yathā iti para saṃpratipanna nidarśanāt guṇa vācini api pade jāti śabda ukta nītitaḥ apṛthak siddha vāci tvāt na yuktā guṇi lakṣaṇāḥ svara liṅga viśeṣa uttha mantra lope na saṃskriyāḥ viśiṣṭa vācaka tvam tu tat āthattam na manmahe 
NP_3.1.9^1	 atas niṣkarṣaka śabda atiriktānām apṛthak siddha viśeṣaṇa vācinām viśeṣya paryavasāna vyutpatteḥ śarīra vācinām deva ādi śabdānām api yathāprayogam śarīri paryavasānam siddham atas eva ca ātma pṛthivī ādi śabdānām īśvara paryanta tā tena sarvaṃsvatu idam brahma jyotīṃṣi viṣṇuḥ ayam ātmā abrahya tat tvam asi iti ādi sāmānādhikaraṇyam tad tad prakāraka brahma param nāma rūpa vyākaraṇam ca tad anupraveśāt atas eva ca tasya sarva śabda vācya tvam api śrūyateth tat eva ca vyajyate tad anupraviśya sat ca tyat ca abhavat iti smaryate ca sarvam samāpnoṣi tatosi sarvaḥ iti sūtritam ca carācara vyapāśrayaḥ tu syāt tad vyapadeśaḥ bhāktaḥ tad bhāva bhāvi tvāt iti 
NP_3.1.9^2	 uktam ca vara da viṣṇu miśraiḥ svarga kāma śabdena kāmyamāna svargaḥ puruṣobhidhīyate na hi īśvara uvāpta samasta kāmaḥ svargam kāmayate tasya ati alpa sukha tvāt atas vācya eka deśe jīve lakṣaṇā gaṅgā śabdasya tīraḥ iva iti yat vā svarga kāma ādi śabdānām api jīva ādi mātrepi mukhya tvam eva pravṛtti nimitta aparityāgāt atas eva hi bhākta padasya bhaktyā vyapadeśa artha tvam api bhāṣya kāraiḥ uktam viśiṣṭa veṣasya śakti viṣaya tvāt tad tyoge katham na lakṣaṇa iti ced aparityakta pravṛtti nimittasya vyutpatti anupraviṣṭa mātra bodhanam mukhya tā tad abhāva kṛtaḥ upacāraḥ iti vyavasthānāt 
NP_3.1.10	 nanu tat tvam asi iti atra tvam iti śvetaketu mātra nirdeśe tat asi iti sāmānādhikaraṇyā yogaḥ śvetaketu śarīrakeśvara nirdeśe tad ā abhimukhyena upadeśa ayogaḥ tad uddeśena tvam artha vidhānam ca asi śabdān anvaya ādinā dūra nirastam prāpta artha tayā nigamana rūpa tvepipava viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhedaḥ niṣkarṣaṇīyaḥ evam aham brahma asmi ityādi vyapadeśa upi durnirvahaḥ jīvena ātmanā iti atra api ātma śabdena jīva ātma ādi abhidhānam ṣāṣya kāra vacana viruddham jīvena mayā ityādi vyapadeśāt paramātmā abhidhāne tu tṛtīya anupapattiḥ vyākaravāṇi iti abhihita tvāt kriyā bhedepi kṛtvā ādeḥ uttara kriyā eka rasyāt kartṛ antara āyuktiḥ samāna kartṛka tva virodhāt karaṇa tva vivakṣayā kartari tṛtīyāyām mukhya tva hāniḥ atas cāreṇa anupraviśya para balam saṃkalayānīti vat jīvasya vai praviśati kartṛ tvam paraḥ tu vyākaraṇa mātra kartā tāvatā tu śabdānām na tad paryanta tva siddhiḥ iti 
NP_3.1.11^1	 atra ucyate saṃbuddhiḥ tāvat atra ātma vidyā upadeśena śvetaketu mātra paryavasitā iti na asaṃbodhya saṃbodhanam vacana vyaktiḥ ca tat asi iti eva tatra kārya kāraṇa bhāvena śarīra ātma bhāvena vā sāmānādhikaraṇya nirvāhaḥ ubhayatra tvaṃśabdasya api tad śabda abhihita dravya paryavasānam siddham dharma antara viśeṣyasya dharma antara viśeṣyataḥ svasmāt abhedaḥ tādātmyam syāt upādāna dehinoḥ atas tvad śarīrakam brahma iti vivakṣāyām satyām tvam tat iti nirdeśa mātram upapannam madhyama puruṣaḥ ca tvaṃśabda prayoga nibandhanaḥ yuṣmadi upapade samāna adhikaraṇe sthānini api madhyamaḥ iti vidhānāt 
NP_3.1.11^2	 atas sa upi tvaṃśabda paryavasāna viṣaya paryavasitaḥ yat vā tat tvam asi iti eva anvayoḥ tu na ca uddeśya anuguṇā tiṅvibhaktiḥ iti niyamaḥ upādeya anuguṇa liṅga vacana ādi nirdeśa vat atra api virodha abhāvāt prayuñjate ca patañjali prabhṛtayaḥ upādeya anuguṇām api tiṅvibhaktim sa punarāvṛttaḥ suvarṇa piṇḍaḥ khadira aṅgāra savarṇe kuṇḍale bhavataḥ ityādiṣu etena aham brahmā asmi iti ādikam api nirvyūḍham jīvena ātmānāḥ iti atra api anena nyāyena sva śabda paryāyeṇa ātma śabdena jīva śabdasya sāmānādhikaraṇyam tāvat siddham 
NP_3.1.11^3	 tṛtīyā anupapattiḥ tu svarūpa tādātmya pakṣe pṛthaktva pakṣe ca samānāḥ atha aṃśa bheda ādinā vibhajya karaṇa tva ādi vivakṣayā kathañcid nirvāhaḥ tathā viśiṣṭa ākāra ādi bheda vivakṣayā vibhajya atra api nirvāham anumanyethāḥ atas śruti ādi vākyeṣu viruddha artha anubandhinaḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyasya na svarūpa aikya niṣṭhatā kārya tvāt apṛthak siddheḥ āviśāt anukārataḥ asti sṛṣṭi upakāra ādeḥ sāmānādhikaraṇya dhīḥ na ca tvad dṛṣṭaḥ puruṣaḥ sthāṇuḥ iti vat puruṣaḥ eva idam sarvam tat tvam asi ityādau bādha artham sāmānādhikaraṇyam iti vācyam mukhya vṛtti saṃbhave tad ayogāt prapañca satya tva ādeḥ ca ābādhita pratyakṣa ādi bala siddha tvāt cit aṃśa sāmānādhikaraṇyam tu na bādha saham tvayā api tad satya tva abhyupagamāt svarūpa aikya vidhāne ca viruddha dharma pratirodhāt tad parityāge padayoḥ anatirikta artha tayā paryāya pada sā mānādhikaraṇya prasaṅgāt dvāra abhāvena mukhya vṛtti bādha āpatteḥ gati antare ca saṃbhavati tad ayogāt sva rūpa mātra nirdeśe ca pada antara vaiyarthyāt svarūpa bhedasya ca bahu pramāṇa siddha tvāt 
NP_3.1.12	 satyam jñānam ityādi lakṣaṇa vākyam api satya tva ādi viśiṣṭa eka viṣayam tathā eva sāmānādhikaraṇya vyutpatteḥ na ca atra viśeṣaṇa bhedāt viviśeṣya bheda aprasaṅgaḥ viruddha viśeṣaṇa abhāvāt na hi ghaṭa paṭa ādiṣu iva virodhaḥ yathā ca pratyakṣe nīla tva utpala tva āt eḥ avirodhaḥ darśana balāt tathā atra api na ca satya tva jñāna tva ādeḥ vaiyadhikaraṇya niyamaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ yena virodhaḥ syāt viśeṣya ekya pare tu sāmānādhikaraṇye viśeṣaṇānām viśeṣaṇa viśeṣyayoḥ ca mithas bhedaḥ guṇaḥ eva na ca viśeṣī a aikya vat viśeṣaṇa viśeṣī a aikya prasaktiḥ viśeṣaṇānām aikya prasaktiḥ vā lakṣaṇa avirodha ādi doṣāt atatha avyutpatteḥ ca na api viśiṣṭe viśiṣṭa antara vidhānāt viśeṣaṇānām mithas samavāya ādi doṣaḥ yugapad aneka viśiṣṭa eka abhidhānāt anūdya vidhāneṣu api yathā vyutpatti dharma pradhāna tvāt ca
