NP_3.1.13	 na ca viśeṣaṇam sarvam viśeṣaṇa antara asaham virodhi mātra virodhi tvāt anyathā pratyakṣa virodhāt sādhya sādhaka dharma ādi viśiṣṭa viṣaya anumāna ādi anudaya prasaṅgāt evantvāt idam viśiṣṭa bodhakam na bhavati ityādi vyavahārasya api vilopaḥ syāt na ca śabdane pratipādane tathā aviśeṣāt pratyakṣa ādi vat śabdena api yathāvastu bodhanīya tvāt viśeṣaṇa mātra paratvam tu na abhyupagatam eva yena viśiṣṭa aikya asiddhiḥ syāt yasya tu viśeṣya mātra paratvam tasya paryāya tulya tvāt pada antara vaiyarthya lakṣaṇa bhaṅga lakṣaṇa ādi doṣaḥ pravṛtti nimittānām viśeṣaṇānām tyāgāt viśeṣya mātrasya ca dvāra rahitasya alakṣya tvāt itara vyāvṛttīnām tu upalakṣaṇa tve svarūpa tve ca pada antara vaiyarthya ādi doṣaḥ saḥ eva 
NP_3.1.14^1	 evam tāsām viśeṣaṇa tve pakṣa antara vat viśiṣṭa bheda ādi doṣaḥ tvad uktaḥ āpatet na ced na anyatra api tyakta pravṛtti nimittasya tad virodhi vyāvṛtti abhilāṣaḥ tu ālokam apahāya timira nirākaraṇa vāñchā vipratipannam vākyam akhaṇḍa param samāna adhikaraṇa vākya tvāt soyam devadattaḥ iti vākya vat yat vā lakṣaṇa vākya tvāt prakṛṣṭa prakāśaḥ candraḥ ityādi vat iti ced na dṛṣṭānta asiddheḥ tat tedantā viśiṣṭasya eva devadattasya soyam iti pratīteḥ yugapad tayoḥ vyāghātaḥ iti ced na yaugapadyasya anabhidhānāt anākṣepāt ca 
NP_3.1.14^2	 yugapad pratipattiḥ tu na doṣaḥ anyathā pratyabhijñā bhaṅge kṣaṇa bhaṅga nairātmya apalāpa ādi vādāḥ vijayeran tathā api atīta tva vartamāna tve katham ekasya iti ced sva pradhvaṃsa kāle hi svayam atītaḥ syāt na ca asau pradhvastaḥ vartamāna tva upalaṃbhāt atīta upādhi viśeṣa saṃbandhi tayā hi tattvam na tu atīta tayā katham ekam pūrvam aparam ca iti ced na pratibandhyupādhi bhedena ubhaya upapatteḥ anyathā kṣaṇasya api pūrva apara madhya vartinaḥ kṣoda prasaṅgāt na hi tasya pūrvasmāt api pūrva tvam eva uttarasmāt api uttara tvam eva vā kṣudyatām kṣaṇa upī iti ced na sarva apahnava prasaṅgāt iti 
NP_3.1.14^3	 tiṣṭhat tu etat dvitīyopi dṛṣṭāntaḥ viśiṣṭa paraḥ eva anyathā vyāvṛtta prati iti anudaya prasaṅgāt prakṛṣṭa tva ādi viśeṣaṇa vaiyarthyāt ca evam śruti bādhopi anumānayoḥ vaktavyaḥ paryāya tulya tva ādi prasaṅga lakṣaṇa pratikūla tarkaḥ ca tathā vipratipannam vākyam viśiṣṭa param ākāṅkṣā yukta vākya tvāt vyadhikaraṇa vākya vat iti bādhakam anumānam api pratipatti anurodhāt dṛṣṭānta siddheḥ ca asya balīyaḥ tvam bhinna pravṛtti nimittānām śabdānām ekasmin= arthe vṛttiḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyam iti śābdaiḥ eva uktam tatra bhinna pravṛtti nimittānām iti paryāya vyāvṛttiḥ 
NP_3.1.14^4	 ekasmin= iti vyadhikaraṇānām ghaṭaḥ paṭa etya ādi an anvitānām ca vyavaccheda artham śabdānām arthe iti ca vyakti artham eva arthe iti viśeṣyasya pradhāna tayā vācya tva sūcana artham vā tena vyadhikaraṇa vākyeṣu eka pradhāna arthe vṛtti saṃbhavepiva tasya viśeṣyatava bhāvāt vyavacchedyatā viśeṣya bodhana vyāpāraḥ vṛttiḥ pravṛttiḥ iti ca sāmānyatas viśeṣataḥ ca atra ucyate prakṛṣṭā hi vṛttiḥ pravṛttiḥ prakarṣaḥ ca atra viśeṣya viṣaya tayā tatra yat upādhikā viśeṣye śabda vṛttiḥ tat pravṛtti nimittam bhinna viśeṣaṇa dvāreṇa eka viśeṣya abhidhānam sāmānādhikaraṇyam iti uktam bhavati 
NP_3.1.15^1	 nanu pauruṣeyam sarvam anvita artham iti pratipāditam tat na upapadyate guṇavat vaktṛ praṇītasya eva vākyasya tathā tva darśanāt iti ced na svatas prāmāṇyāt svarasataḥ hi sarvam jñāna sabādhita vyavahāra janakam dṛśyate bheda agraha ādi viśeṣa upādhikam hi kvacid bādhya vyavahāra hetu tvam tatas svābhāvikam api prāmāṇyam pratibandhakena doṣeṇa kvacid apahnutam yathā agneḥ auṣṇyam tatra tad aṃśa apekṣayā prāmāṇyam eva guṇāḥ tu saṃbhāvita doṣa sthale doṣa nirākaraṇa aupayikāḥ pramāṇyasya taiḥ vyāpti abhāvāt nitya sarvajña vādinām pramāṇa bhūte tad jñāne vyabhicārāt aprāmāṇyasya tu doṣa adhīna tvam avyabhicarita anvaya vyatireka siddham avastunā uprāmāṇyasya katham hetu sādhya tvam iti ced na saṃśaya tva viparyaya tva ādi rūpasya tasya avastu tva abhāvāt bhāva antara atiriktasya ca abhāvasya asmābhiḥ anabhyupagamāt abhyupagamepi pradhvaṃsasya mudgara ādi sādhya tva dṛṣṭeḥ 
NP_3.1.15^2	 tadvat pramā api samyak mithyā bodha sādhāraṇāt atirikta sahitā jāyate kāryatve sati tad viśeṣa tvāt apramāvat prāmāṇyam paratas jñāyate anabhyāsa daśāyām sāṃśayika tvāt aprāmāṇya vat iti ced tatra prathame kṛtsna pramā pakṣīkāre hetoḥ sva mate bhāga asiddhirḥ iśvara pramāyā nitya tva abhyupagamāt anīśvara pramā pakṣīkāre yāvat īśvara siddhi vyartham viśeṣaṇam riśvara anumāna samanantaram prayogaḥ iti ced na tasya śāstra yoni adhikaraṇa nyāyena anumātum aśakyatvāt tarhi viśeṣaṇam na prayokṣyāmahe iti ced na sva abhimateśvara pramayānaikāntyāt anabhyupagata īśvaraiḥ saugata ādibhiḥ evam prayoge kaḥ parihāraḥ iti ced na śruti siddha nitya pramā sam arthanena bādhasya anaikāntikasya vā vaktum śakya tvāt śruti siddha nitya pramāvi a vacchedena kāryatva viśeṣaṇam saphalam syāt hi ced tarhi śrutyā tad siddhiḥ śruti prāmāṇī anirṇayam antareṇa katham syāt  
NP_3.1.15^3	 tad prāmāṇyam ca nitya nirdeṣa tayā abhyupagamyate ced katham tatra paratas prāmāṇyet pattiḥ vaktṛ guṇa adhīnam vākyānām prāmāṇyam iti hi vaḥ siddhāntaḥ nirdeṣa tā eva guṇaḥ iti tad adhīna tayā tatra paratas prāmāṇyam iti ced na pratibandhaka abhāvasya paraiḥ kāraṇa tva anabhyupagamāt abhyupagame ca tāvat mātṛ a dhīna tvepi veda apauruṣeya tva nitya tva ādeḥ avirodhāt veda pauruṣeya tva ādi siddhi artham hi vaḥ paratas prāmāṇya samarthana ārambhaḥ tad apauruṣeya tva ādi siddhi artham eva ca asmābhiḥ svatas prāmāṇyam pratipādyate atha āpta ukta tayā veda prāmāṇyāt īśvara siddhau tat pramāvya vat chedāya viśeṣaṇam iti iṣyate tat api na paratas prāmāṇye nirṇīte vadesya āpta mūla prāmāṇya siddhiḥ tad siddhau ca īśvara siddhiḥ tad pramāvya vat chedāya viśeṣaṇam sa viśeṣaṇa śvāsau hetuḥ paratas prāmāṇyam sādhayet iti cakraka āśraya prasaṅga ārt iśvara anumānān yathā siddhi parihārāya paratas prāmāṇyam nyāya kusuma añjalau samarthyate 
NP_3.1.15^4	 tatra eva ca kāryatva viśeṣaṇam prayujyate na ca asiddhi vyavacchedāya viśeṣaṇam yuktam siddha tve tu paratas prāmāṇya samarthanasya na tad artha tā iti dustaratā tathā api śabda prāmāṇyam vaktṛ guṇa adhīnam iti ced na viśeṣaka abhāvāt doṣa saṃbhāvanā sthale ca tad apekṣaṇāt vedasya ca nirdeṣa tvāt doṣa abhāva adhīna tve paratas prāmāṇyam siddham iti ced na tad adhīna tva abhāvāt tasya virodha nivṛtti mātra rūpa tvāt astu vā tad adhīna tvam tathā api vede tu na doṣaḥ guṇam antareṇa doṣa abhāvaḥ na ghaṭataḥ iti ced anuṣṇa aśīta sparśa vat ubhaya nivṛtteḥ api darśanāt upapatteḥ ca bhāva antara abhāva vādinaḥ doṣa abhāva upi guṇaḥ eva iti ced na svābhāva antareṇa tat nirvāhāt na hi tasya api śīta abhāvaḥ uṣṇaḥ eva anuṣṇa aśīte tad asiddheḥ ubhaya saṃgrahaṇena hi śīta abhāva tvam tadvat atra api sa guṇeṣu āpta vākyeṣu vaktṛ guṇa rahiteṣu veda vākyeṣu ca doṣa abhāvaḥ samānaḥ 
NP_3.1.16	 nanu śabdānām svatas prāmāṇye buddha ādi vākyam api svatas pramāṇam syāt na syāt svatas tvasya utsarga rūpa tvāt virodhi viśeṣe ca tasya ananupraveśāt uktam ca āgama prāmāṇye na eva śabde svatas doṣāḥ prāmāṇya paripanthinaḥ santi kintu svatas tasya pramāṇa tvam iti sthitiḥ vaktuḥ āśaya doṣeṇa keṣu cittadapa udyate aṅgulī agre hi mātaṅga yūtham iti evamādiṣu iti kiñca nitye hetu guṇa apekṣā vede nāsti īśa buddhi vat hetu abhāvāt na doṣaḥ cedū vaktra bhāvāt iha api naḥ akāraṇam yathā jñānam pramātvam adhigacchati akāraṇam tathā vākyam svatas pramiti kāraṇam yadi hetu guṇa abhāvāt aprāmāṇyam prasajyate tadā īśvara pramāyām api anivāryam idam tava 
NP_3.1.17^1	 atha eva brūṣe kāraṇa guṇa doṣayoḥ abhāve tad prayojyayoḥ prāmāṇya aprāmāṇyayoḥ dvayoḥ api asaṃbhavāt raśī antarā yogāt ca niḥsvabhāva tvam veda śabda janya jñānānām syāt iti idam api tulyam īśvara jñāne hetu nivṛttiḥ tat kāryam prāmāṇyam nivartayet na tu nityam iti ced aprāmāṇya hetu nivṛttiḥ api tathā eva atas viruddha svabhāva yogaḥ ubhaya parityāgāt niḥsvabhāva etava vā syāt evam anīśvara vādinām saugata ādīnām śuddha saṃvid santāna ādiṣu adhipati saha kārya ādi kāraṇa tad guṇa ādeḥ a saṃbhavāt svārasikasva ātma gocara prāmāṇyasya ca abhyupagamāt samāḥ carcāḥ yadi api pūrva pratyayasya kāraṇa tvam iṣṭam tathā api tasya apavarga daśā sthasya guṇa doṣa ādi rūpa samasta saṃskāra pratyarthitayā na tad janyasya guṇa hetu tā iti yat ca prāmāṇyam paratas jñāyate iti prayuktam tatra jñāna antareṇa jñāna antara svabhāva vedanābhyupagamāt siddha sādhana tā paratas eva iti vivakṣāyām īdṛśam jñānam pramā iti lakṣaṇataḥ sarva pramāsaṅgrāhiṇi jñāne pārameśvare ca vijñāne tad asaṃbhavaḥ na hi tābhyām sva pramātvam na gṛhītam lakṣaṇa avyāpti kiñcijjña tva ādi prasaṅgāt 
NP_3.1.17^2	 atonyatra paratas eva iti niyamaḥ iti ced tat api na tat dṛṣṭāntena eva pratiprayoktum śakya tvāt vigītam prāmāṇyam sva ādhāreṇa jñāyate prāmāṇya rūpa tvāt riśvara jñāna ādi prāmāṇya vat iti katham tarhi idam pramāṇam apramāṇam vā iti saṃśaya avakāśaḥ iti ced na viśeṣataḥ gṛhyamāṇeṣu api saṃśaya utpatti darśanāt bhavati muhur śuktikā ra jata mohāt andhīkṛta dhiyaḥ kaladhautepi tathā upalabhyamāne yathā upalambham idam rajatam eva vā pūrvavat śukti rajatam vā iti puratas tathā atra api gṛhyamāṇepi prāmāṇye kim idam pramāṇam eva sat pramāṇa tayā upalambhate 
NP_3.1.17^3	 uta bādhāt pūrva bhrama vat apramāṇam sat iti saṃśayaḥ yuktaḥ tathā api sandeha sahena kim svatas grahaṇena niścayaḥ tu para adhīnaḥ eva iti ced kim asmad apekṣayā grahaṇam agrahaṇam vā niyantum śakyam siddhaḥ hi grahaṇa prakāraḥ parīkṣakaiḥ anusaraṇīyaḥ siddhiḥ eva svatas katham iti ced ittham jñānam sva ālambanam prakāśayat svayam api jñāna antara nirapekṣam prakāśate iti tāvat sarva vedānti saṃmatam asvayaṃprakāśa vādepi sva grāhiṇa anuvyavasāyena prakāśamānaḥ vyavasāyaḥ tāvat asaṃśaya ātmā eva dṛśyate 
NP_3.1.18	 smṛtya prāmāṇya vāda īpya pūrva artha gocara tayā smṛti vilakṣaṇaḥ ca aviparyaya ātmā ca ābādha ātmā ca vādha ādeḥ pūrvam tad prasaṅga abhāvāt tatas ca yat viṣaya tayā ayam vyavasāyaḥ prathamam pratibhātaḥ tad viṣaya tayā eva paraspara parikṣodāt paścāt api atas yat tad viṣaya tva lakṣaṇam prāmāṇyam paścāt tena eva vyavasthāpyate tad ādau= eva gṛhītam iti svatas prāmāṇya grahaḥ 
NP_3.1.19	 nanu evam saṃśaya tva ādi lakṣaṇam aprāmāṇyam api svayaṃprakāśena anuvyavasāyena vā prathamamave grahītum śakyam tathā api viparyaya tva lakṣaṇam na tathā gṛhyamāṇa vaiparītyasya svena sva grāhiṇā vā prathamam agrahaṇāt tasmin= aṃśe ca vaidikānām avivādāt tatra imam aṃśam ādāya eva ca antataḥ pasvataḥ prāmāṇya samarthana pravṛtteḥ tatra doṣa abhāva at eva ādau= aprāmāṇya anutpatteḥ tatas eva ca aprāmāṇya pramiti asaṃbhavāt svatas eva ca prāmāṇya pramiteḥ abādhāt ca iti ucyate iti 
NP_3.2.20^1	 atha pauruṣeya apauruṣeya vibhāgaḥ eva anupapannaḥ sarvasya api vākyasya pauruṣeya tve vākya tva ādi liṅga sadbhāvāt sarvajña praṇītāḥ vedāḥ veda tvāt iti vyatireki saṃbhavāt mantra kṛdbhyaḥ tasya ha vai etasya mahataḥ bhūtasya niśvasitam etat yadṛgvedaḥ ṛcaḥ sāmāni jajñire chandāṃsi jajñire tasmāt yajuḥ tasmāt ajāyate ityādi śravaṇāt pratimanvantaram ca eṣā śrutiḥ anyā vidhīyate ityādi smṛteḥ ca adhikṛtya kṛte granthe iti pāṇinismṛti siddhārtha kāṭhaka kālāpaka ādi samākhyā viśeṣa yogāt kādācid ka kathā viśeṣa saṃdṛṣṭeḥ anitya yogāt tad pūrva uttara kālayoḥ tat ananvaya āpatteḥ śabdasya bhūta guṇasya naśvara tvāt iti ced tat na vākya tva anumānasya vipakṣe bādhaka abhāvāt 
NP_3.2.20^2	 akāraṇa kārya utpatti prasaṅgaḥ iti ced na kāryatvasya eva sādhyamāna tvāt akāraṇa tva mātrasya āpādyamānaḥ sya iṣṭa tvāt krama viśeṣeṇa anuccāryamāṇānām varṇānām katham padatvam vākya tvam vā iti ced na para kṛta prabandha pāṭha vat akartṛbhiḥ uccāraṇepi tad siddheḥ ādimam uccāraṇam kartṛ abhāve katham syāt iti ced na ādimattvasya eva asiddheḥ darśana anuguṇyena adyatva vat eva sarvadā paratantra uccāraṇasya eva abhyupagantum ucita tvāt tatas ca sarvadā uccārayitṛ puruṣa apekṣa tvepi pūrva pūrva adhīta prakārasya anusaraṇāt anādi tva siddheḥ 
NP_3.2.20^3	 apauruṣeya tve ghuṇa kṣata akṣara vadū bodhaka tvepi abhiprāya virahāt artha para tvam na syāt iti ced na pratipanne nirbādhe ca arthe pradhāne bodhaka tvasya eva tātparya rūpa tvāt prādhānya ādeḥ laukika vākya vat ākhyāta ādi svabhāvāt eva siddheḥ asmat iṣṭe ca sa īśvaramī māṃsā pakṣe nitya īśvara abhiprāya saṃbhavāt svayam eva hi āha śrutiḥ smṛtiḥ mama eva ājñāḥ iti tathā bhāṣyam sva śāsanau= abodhi śāstram iti nityam śrutyā eva niyuṅkte paraḥ iti nityā api sā tad ājñā gīta ādiḥ api śruti artha upadeśa rūpa tayā pravartate sākṣāt tu śrutiḥ tad ādośaḥ tad anuvidhānāt ca smṛtiḥ api 
NP_3.2.20^4	 ajñāta kartṛka tve gandharva bhāṣita ādi vat āpta kartṛka tva niścaya abhāvāt aprāmāṇyaśaṅkā syāt iti ced na doṣa abhāva niścayāt eva tad nivṛtteḥ anāpta kartṛka tva śaṅkāyām katham doṣa abhāva niścayaḥ iti ced na mahā jana parigrahāt eva anāpta kartṛkaśaṅkā unmūlanāt bāhya āgama parigraha vat kim nasyāt iti ced na bahu jana parigraha ādi mātrasya mahājana parigraha tvena avivakṣita tvāt tad pariprahaviśeṣasya eva vivakṣita tvāt ca tayoḥ kaḥ vā viśeṣaḥ iti ced na hetu darśana adarśanābhyām viśeṣāt ananya gatikaiḥ svaira rasikaiḥ sukha jīvika arthibhiḥ kuhaka vañcitaiḥ vā tad parigrahaḥ iha tu na tathā tad vaiparītyasya su prasiddha tvāt iti 
NP_3.2.21	 api ca bāhya āgama pratibandiḥ kim vadeprāmāṇyam āpta prāmāṇya nibandhanam iti icchadbhiḥ vaiśeṣika ādibhiḥ ucyate uta saugata ādi āgama prāmāṇyam icchadbhiḥ atha vā parityakta aśeṣa pāralaukika āgamaiḥ lokāyatikaiḥ iti na ādyaḥ riśvara kṛta tvepi vedasya evaṃvidha parigraha viśeṣam antareṇa ādyatana rebāhya āgamebhyaḥ vivekasya aśakya tvāt sarvajña praṇīta tva ādi abhimānasya tad anumāna prakriyāyāḥ ca sarvatra durvāra tvāt na dvitīyaḥ abhyupagata prāmāṇye svāgama ipi prasaṅgāt dṛṣṭa phala saṃvādasya visaṃvādān yatha asiddheḥ ca sarvatra sama carca tvāt asmat uktasya nirupādhika parigrahasya sva mate durvaca tvāt atas eva na tṛtīyaḥ prāmāṇyasya parokṣa prāmāṇyasya vākya prāmāṇyasya ca sthāpita tvena vaidika vākye hi autsargike prāmāṇye prāpte nirupādhika prekṣā vat ananta puruṣa parigrahāt eva anāpta kartṛka tva śaṅkā unmūlane ca vaktṛ doṣa śaṅkā anutthānāt vacasi casvataḥ kāca ādi vat doṣa adarśanāt āpta kartṛka tva abhāvepya autsargikam prāmāṇyam anapoditam iti 
NP_3.2.22^1	 atas eva hi prekṣāvantaraḥ coditeṣu bahu vitta vyaya āyāsa sādhyeṣu niśaṅkam pravartante pratiṣiddheṣu ca sukhatareṣu api viṣa saṃsṛṣṭa anna bhojanāt ivat nivartante prayogaḥ ca pāralaukikī mahā jana pravṛttiḥ saphalāḥ prekṣāvat pravṛtti tvāt kṛṣi ādi pravṛtti vat na hi anantaiḥ prekṣā avadbhiḥ avi saṃvādena aphalam anuṣṭhīyate iti śaṅkitum śakyam duḥkha rūphala darśanena siddha sādhana tā iti ced na anabhipreta upālambhāt pravṛtti duḥkhāt adhika puruṣa artha paryavasānasya siṣā dhayiṣita tvāt 
NP_3.2.22^2	 tathā api lābha pūjā khyāti rūpa dṛṣṭa prayojanena eva sārtha tā iti ced tat api asat atad uddeśena teṣām pravṛtti darśanāt tad uddeśena pravṛtteḥ ca ḍāmbhika tvena śāstraiḥ tad niṣṭhaiḥ ca vigarhaṇāt ye ca tad uddeśena pravartante tepya tad uddeśena pravṛttānām anukurvāṇāḥ eva khyāti ādi prāpnuvanti anyathā khyāti lābha pūjā ādeḥ niḥ nimitta tva prasaṅgāt na hi yat kiñcid anena kṛtam iti matvā kaścid kṛcchra saṃpāditān dhana ādīn dadāti pūjayati guṇān vā āropya stauti api tu kutaścid pramāṇāt siddham praśasta ācaraṇam abhimatya eva samara sāmarthya ādi mūla lābha jādikam api antatortha śāstra ādi mūla praśasta pravṛtti prasūtam 
NP_3.2.22^3	 atas sat maryādā pravṛttān dāna māna ādibhiḥ abhyarcayanta uṣpadṛṣṭa buddhyā eva pravartante jana rañjana artham eva dāna ādi janaḥ dātari mānayitari ca rajyate jana anurāga prabhavāḥ ca saṃpadaḥ iti prasiddheḥ iti ced na pratyupakāra ādi anarha pravrajita tapasvi jaḍa andha badhira dīna anātha ādiṣu dāna māna ādibhiḥ anurañjiteṣu api tad mūla dṛṣṭa saṃpad prasaṅga abhāvāt atas eva hi nīti narma saciveṣu eva tad artha dāna ādi vyavasthāpanam pratāraṇa paṭubhiḥ vaindikaiḥ pratāritāḥ tān pūjayanti iti ced na kim te sva ātmānam api pratārayanti 
NP_3.2.22^4	 ye nāma samasta bhoga avimukhāḥ yāvat jīvam ātmānam parikleśayanti yaiḥ ca paṭu prajñāḥ sarve lokāḥ pratāritāḥ te katham loka uttara prajñena tvayā pratārakāḥ iti unnītāḥ andha paramparā kalpa starhi ayam anuṣṭhāna pravāhaḥ iti ced na pramāṇa svarūpa phalayoḥ abādhasya ca pratyakṣa tvāt dharma buddhyā eva ca nirupādhika parigrahasya tvad uktyā eva siddhaḥ anādinidhanesmin= āmnāya mūle anuṣṭhāne pravahati prakriyā antaram āśritya pratārakaiḥ īśvaraiḥ arvācīnaiḥ ca praticchanda pravartanā śruti smṛti siddhā yuktimatī ca iti eṣā diś 
NP_3.2.23^1	 veda anitya tva anumānānām pratiprayogāḥ ca parva apara kalpāḥ etat veda sandarbha pāṭhavantaḥ kalpa tvāt adyatana kalpa vat aiśvaram veda pravartanam apracyuta prācīnasandarbham āpta kartṛka veda pravartana rūpa tvāt adyatana nipuṇa upādhyāya veda pravartana vat na ca āśraya ādi asiddhiḥ pauruṣeya tvepi prāmāṇyam icchataḥ tatas eva tad siddheḥ aprāmāṇyam icchatopi mahā jana parigrahān yatha anupapattyā eva prāmāṇyam prasādhya tatas eva tad sādhanāt na ca asti veda pravartanasya sārasvata pāṭhena anaikāntyam tathā eva tat pravāhasya tad tad śākhā praṇayana vadana ādi tvāt mantra brāhmaṇa ādi vākya svarūpa vaiyākulī virahāt ca iti evaṃvipakṣe bādhaka abhāvāt eva kevala vyatireki api nirastaḥ anumāna adhyāye tasya sāmānyatas dūṣita tvāt ca 
NP_3.2.23^2	 tvad mata īpya āyurveda ādi sapakṣa sadbhāvena tasya asādha araṇyam na hi tebhyaḥ vyāvṛttam apauruṣeya tva ādi lakṣaṇam veda tvam tvayā abhyupagamyate veda śabda prayoga viṣaya tā mātreṇa teṣām api pakṣīkāre sva icchā gṛhīta rūpasya īśvarasya tad tad avatāra saṃvyavahārāḥ veda vyatiriktāḥ santi sa pakṣāḥ na ca te tvayā api na iṣyante veda tayā vā svīkriyante gīta ādiṣu bhagavat ukti aṃśānām śrī viṣṇu smṛti prabhṛtīnām ca veda tva anabhyupagamāt dharma śāstra tayā eva hi vaiṣṇava smṛti ādi prasiddhiḥ avaktṛka sandarbhāḥ vedāḥ veda tvāt yaḥ sa kartṛ kasandarbhaḥ na asau vedaḥ iti pratihetuḥ ca siddhaḥ aprasiddha viśeṣaṇa tva ādi codyam tu iha na tvayā smartavyam 
NP_3.2.23^3	 sandarbhaḥ katham avavatṛkaḥ syāt iti ced na varṇa krama niyama mātra viśeṣasya sandarbha śabdena grahaṇāt tasya ca prāk ukta nayena yathāpūrva pravartana mātreṇa api vyavasthānāt mābhūt avīta hetuḥ vītaḥ tu syāt vigītam vākyam sarvajña praṇītam pramāṇa tve satya laukika artha viṣaya vākya tvāt na tu eva aham jātu nāsam ityādi vākya vat iti ced na veda artha viṣayaiḥ kalpasūtra kāra ādi vākyaiḥ asmad ādi vākyaiḥ eva vānaikāntyāt atīva kartṛka tve satī iti viśeṣayiṣyāmaḥ iti ced na tathā api yathāpūrva praṇayana mātreṇa api tad praṇīta tva siddhau siddha sādhanāt yathāpūrvam eva hi viśvam īśvaraḥ sṛjati yathā adhīmahe sūryācandramasau dhātā yathāpūrvam akalpayat iti 
NP_3.2.23^4	 evam tarhi tulya yogakṣema tayā veda vat jagatā upya kartṛka tvam prasaktam iti ced na yathāpūrvam ghaṭa ādi nirmāṇe kulāla kuvinda ādeḥ kartṛ tva siddheḥ hanta ! vedasya evam syāt iti ced hanta ! syāt eva na hi kalpa antara varṇa vyakti samudāyam eva idānīntana veda rāśim brūmaḥ api tu tādṛk kramayogitā mātram sarvatra vākyeṣu yatheṣṭa krama kalpane puruṣasya svātantrya uktiḥ na punar yathāpura uccāraṇe iti kāvya ādiṣu api prasiddham yadi tvayā ayathā pura praṇīta tvam sādhyeta tatra yathāpura praṇayane kam iva doṣām ālakṣya evam viśeṣayasi mantra ādiṣu krama bhaṅga anupapattiḥ ca kalpa antarepi tad śakti anapāyāt eva tathā tvepi vā yathāpūrva uccāraṇā ipi tad anapāyāt anyathā kalpanā gauravāt iti 
NP_3.2.24^1	 tathā api sarga pralaya saṃbhavāt saṃpradāya vicchede sarva veda ucchedāt paścāt īśvaraḥ tad sraṣṭā syāt na syāt tathā api prācīna vedasā akṣāt kāriṇaḥ tasya tad pravartana mātra aucityāt śaktasya api tad jātīya veda antara kalpane gauravāt śaktau= api siddha upajīvanasya asmad ādiṣu dṛṣṭeḥ eṣām eva ca mantrāṇām kalpa antarepi mantra tva avirodhāt evam mantra nitya tve ca tulya nyāyatayā brāhmaṇa nitya tvasya api dustyaja tvāt tad dṛṣṭāntena vā tad nitya tva sādhanāt sārasvata pāṭhā ādau= api mantra ādi svarūpa bheda abhāvasya ukta tvāt yā brahmāṇam vidadhāti pūrvam yaḥ vai vedān= ca prahiṇoti tasmai vācā avirūpa nityayā apūrve pūrvebhyaḥ vacaḥ etat ūcuḥ ajān ha vai praśnīn= tapasyamānāt brahma svayam bhyabhyānar ṣat te ṛṣayaḥ bhavan tad ṛṣīṇām ṛṣi tvam anādi nidhanā hi eṣā vāc utsṛṣṭā svayaṃbhuvā vyasya vedam sanātanam ityādibhiḥ īśvarasya api anīśvara vat veda pravartana mātra siddheḥ kutas ca sarga pralaya siddhiḥ 
NP_3.2.24^2	 viśvasantatiḥ atyantam ucchidyate santati tvāt pradīpa santati vat viśvasantānoyam dṛśya santāna hīnaiḥ samavāyibhiḥ ārabdhaḥ santāna tvāt āraṇeya agni santāna vat vartamāna brahmāṇḍa paramāṇavaḥ pūrvam utpādita sajātīya santāna antarāḥ nitya tve sati tad ārambhaka tvāt pradīpa paramāṇu vat parvatāḥ api cūrṇībhaviṣyanti avayavi tvāt ghaṭa vat samudrāḥ api śoṣam upayāsyanti jalāśaya tvāt palvala vat iti ādi anumānataḥ iti ced na keṣām cit nitya saṃsāra pakṣe prathamasya hetoḥ tathā tad pratipādakaiḥ āgamaiḥ aṃśataḥ bādhaḥ tat vahiṣkāre ca anaikāntaḥ sarveṣām ca śruti śata siddhaiḥ niti avibhūti niṣṭhaiḥ īśvara nitya vigraha ādibhiḥ taiḥ taiḥ anekāntar na ca tad pakṣīkāraḥ bādhā siddhyoḥ anyatara āpātāt pratiprayogāḥ ca gaṇita viśeṣa ādi siddha dvi pāra ardha saṃkhyā pūrva uttara kālaḥ na loka śūnyaḥ kāla tvāt adyatana kāla vat ityādayaḥ svayam ūhyāḥ 
NP_3.2.25	 vipakṣe bādhakam na samyak dṛśyate yat ca āgama anugrahaḥ eṣām balam iti abhimatam tad āgama pramāṇa tva upajīvanam tathā ca āgamataḥ eva pralaya ādi siddhiḥ tatas ca āgamāt eva āgama nitya tvam siddham uktam ca prajñā paritrāṇe vedatas pauruṣeya tva śaṅkā vede na śāmyati hetu antara samudbhūtā hetu antara nivāritā iti sarga ādau veda parigraha prakāraḥ ca evam upapāditaḥ vyavahāri jana abhāvāt girām vyutpatti asaṃbhavāt veda arthaḥ na eva śakyeta boddhum tasya iti ced na tat bahavaḥ saṃbhavanti eva śabda artha vyavahāriṇaḥ mukta ādyāḥ riśituḥ yat vā bahu rūpa parigrahāt prācya vijñāna saṃskāra anuvṛttyā vā asya vedhasaḥ sarva śabda artha vijñānam supta utthita vat udbhavet na garbha vāsaḥ teṣām na vayaḥ vasthādayopi ca sarva vijñāna saṃpannāḥ sṛṣṭāḥ te iti veda dhīḥ ayaḥ brahmaṇaḥ am iti śratyā sṛṣṭvā brahmāṇam īśvaraḥ asmai vedān adattā iti pratītiḥ naḥ udeti hi śabda artha vedine veda pradānam sārthakam bhavet anyathā vyartham iti artha āpattyā śabda artha veditā iti 
NP_3.2.26^1	 sūtra kāṇḍa mantra kṛt tva janma ādi vākyānām api prathama draṣṭṛ tva smartṛ tva saṃpradāya pravartana ādibhiḥ eva nirvāhaḥ idam api āgama anurodhāt eva siddham svayaṃbhu abhyānarṣat ityādi hi śrūyate prajāpati niyogāt ca tat āhita mahimānaḥ mahā ṛṣa yonadhītān eva veda bhāgān paśyanti tant niyogaḥ ca tad tad ṛṣika tvena anusandhāna ādeḥ karma aupayika tvāt teṣām api pravāha an ādi tva anna anitya saṃyoga ādi doṣaḥ yat vai kiñca manuḥ avadat iti ādau pravāha anādi tvam paraiḥ uktam tad upākhyāna antara ādiṣu api tulyam uktam ca bhagavatā vyāsena yugāntentarhitān vedān sa itihāsān mahā ṛṣayaḥ lebhire tapasā pūrvam anujñātāḥ svayaṃbhuvā iti itihāsotra tad tad vṛttāntaḥ uktam ca tena eva dharma śāstra ipi dharma mūlam vedam āhuḥ grantha rāśim akṛtrimam tad vidām smṛti śīle ca sādhu ācāram manaḥ priyam 
NP_3.2.26^2	 iti śākhā praṇayanam ca dvāpara ante bhāvi puruṣa śakti parikṣayāt veda vṛkṣa eka deśa uddharaṇam etena samākhyā nirvyūḍhāḥ pravacana viṣaya tvāt idam ca sarvam prasādhitam prajñā paritrāṇe yādṛś prabhāvāḥ śrūyante ṛṣi ādyāḥ veda rāśiṣu tādṛśāḥ eva sṛjyante vedān dṛṣṭvā svayaṃbhuvā atas tebhyaḥ purā veda sattvāt vedasya nitya tā anadhītya eva vedānām āvirbhāvayitṛ tvataḥ tapasā prāppaya saṃskārāt tad sūkta tva ādi saṃbhavaḥ tapaḥ prabhāvāt matrāṇām ṛṣi darśana saṃskṛteḥ śaktiḥ ādhīyate kācid yathā asmākam adhītitaḥ artha avabodhaka tvam tu śabda śaktyā anya śabda vat ṛṣi darśana todhīta īparapi śakti antara udbhavaḥ apūrva kārya niṣpattau= upakuryāt idam tatas kāṭhaka ādi samākhyāyāḥ nimittam ca idam eva vā prakṛṣṭam vā pravacanam tad siddhā veda nitya tā iti 
NP_3.2.27	 varṇa anitya tvam krama anitya tā vā na abhimata veda nitya tva virodhi na ca varṇa nitya tvam veda nitya tva hetuḥ kāvya ādiṣu api tulya tvāt śabda adhikaraṇam ca anupayukta varṇa anitya tva param na anumanyāmahe śārīraka devatā nadhikaraṇe ca śabdaḥ iti ced na atas prabhavāt pratyakṣa anumānābhyām atas eva ca nitya tvam samāna nāma rūpa tvāt ca āvṛttau= api avirodhaḥ darśanāt smṛteḥ ca iti sūtraiḥ idam sarvam samarthitam 
NP_3.2.28^1	 veda artha saṅgahe tu vedāḥ pramāṇam ced vidhi artha vāda mantra āgatam sarvam apūrvam artha jātam yathā avasthitam eva bodhayanti prāmāṇyam ca vedānām aautpattikaḥ tu śabdasya ārtthena saṃbandhaḥa iti uktam iti mantra artha vādayoḥ api yāthārthyam prakramya śabda śakterasa aṅketika tvam tatas eva śabda anumāna vivekaḥ pauruṣeya apauruṣeya ādi vibhāga ādikam ca vyaktam pradarśitam tathā hi yathā agni jala ādīnām auṣṇya ādi śakti yogaḥ svābhāvikaḥ yathā cakṣuḥ ādīnām indriyāṇām buddhi janaka tva śaktiḥ svābhāvikī tathā śabdasya api bodhaka tva śaktiḥ svābhāvikī 
NP_3.2.28^2	 na ca hasta ceṣṭā ādi vat saṅketa mūlam śabdasya bodhaka tvam iti vaktum yuktam avana ādi anusandhāna avicchedepi saṅketayitṛ puruṣa ajñānāt yāni saṅketa mūlāni tāni sarvāṇi sākṣāt vā paramparayā vā vijñāyante na ca devadatta ādi śabda vat kalpayitum yuktam teṣu sākṣāt vā paramparayām vā saṃketaḥ jñāyate gavā ādi śabdānām tu anādyam u sandhāna avicchedepi saṃketa ajñānāt eva bodhaka tva śaktiḥ svābhāvikī agni ādīnām auṣṇya ādi śakti vat indriyāṇām bodhaka tva śakti vat ca śabdasya api bodhaka tva śaktiḥ avaśya āśrayaṇīyāḥ 
NP_3.2.29^1	 nanu ca indriya vat śabdasya api bodhaka tvam svābhāvikam ced saṃbandha graham bodhaka tvāya kim iti apekṣate  liṅga vat iti ucyate yathā jñāta saṃbandha niyamam dhūma ādi agni ādi buddhi janakam tathā jñāta saṃbandha niyamaḥ śabda upyartha viśeṣa buddhi janakaḥ evam tarhi śabda upyartha viśeṣasya liṅgam iti anumānam eva syāt mā evam śabda arthayoḥ saṃbandhaḥ bodhya bodhaka bhāvaḥ eva dhūma ādīnām tu saṃbandha antaram iti tasya saṃbandhasya jñāpana dvāreṇa buddhi janaka tvam iti viśeṣaḥ evam gṛhīta saṃbandhasya bodhaka tva darśanāt anādi anusaṃdhāna avicchedepi saṃṅketa ajñānāt bodhaka tvavam śaktiḥ eva iti niścīyate 
NP_3.2.29^2	 evam bodhakānām pada saṃghātānām saṃsarga viśeṣa bodhaka tvena vākya śabda abhidheyānām uccāraṇa kramaḥ yatra puruṣa buddhi pūrvakaḥ te pauruṣeyāḥ śabdāḥ iti ucyante yatra tu uccāraṇa kramaḥ pūrva pūrva uccāraṇa krama janita saṃskāra pūrvakaḥ sarvadā apauruṣeyāḥ te vedāḥ iti ucyante etat eva vedānām apauruṣeya tvam nitya tvam ca yat pūrva uccāraṇa krama janita saṃskāreṇa krama viśeṣam smṛtvā tena eva krameṇa uccārya tvam tena ānupūrvī viśeṣeṇa tam eva saṃsthitāḥ akṣara rāśayaḥ vedāḥ ṛc yajuḥ sāma atharva bhedena bhinnāḥ ananta śākhāḥ vartante iti 
NP_3.2.30^1	 atra āṅgirasa anukti ratharvā anupraveśa vivakṣayā evam tri vedī vyapadeśa īpi vivakṣā bhedaḥ grāhyaḥ sarva upyasau punar mantra artha vāda ādi rūpeṇa trividhaḥ tatra prāmāṇika mantra vyavahāra viṣayaḥ mantraḥ sa ca anuṣṭheya artha prakāśana ādinā upakāroti na ca idam eva tad lakṣaṇam vasantāya iti evamādi avyāpteḥ vasantāya kapiñjalān ālabhante iti ādayaḥ tu mantrāḥ api vidhi parāḥ eva mīmāṃsitāḥ sakila mantraḥ kriyamāṇa anuvādi stotra śastra japya ādi bheda bhinnaḥ paiśāca māgadha ādi tad tad bhāṣā mantrāṇām phala pradatve tad tad bīja jāti ādikam nidānam śraddheya devatā nāma aṅka mātram tu na tad akṣara śakti pratibandhakam kṣipra kṣudra phala prakāśanena vipralambha artham tathā eva īśvara ādibhiḥ sṛṣṭam 
NP_3.2.30^2	 garuḍa ādi nāma aṅka bhāṣā mantreṣu tu tat tad devatā smṛti upakāraka tvam api asti etena mantra vyākaraṇam nirvyūḍham ye tu sapta koṭayaḥ mahā mantrāḥ iti āpta śāstra pratiṣṭhitāḥ te tu praṇava yoga ayoga ādibhiḥ vaidikāḥ tāntrikāḥ iti vibhajyante tatra śūdra adhikāra tva sidhi artham tāntrika paribhāṣā na punar avaidikatayā śrauta smārta ādi bheda vyapadeśa vat pramāṇa siddha tva aviśeṣāt sarveṣām ca mantrāṇām sa dvārakam advārakam ca paramātmā eva pratipādyaḥ phala pradaḥ ca sa dvārakeṣu tāvat viniyoga bhedāt bahudhā brahmaṇi paryavasānam tat tad deva śarīra tvāt tad tad aṃśa tayā sthiteḥ aindṣa ādinya āyataḥ ca eṣām sarveṣām īśvare sthitiḥ 
NP_3.2.31–3.2.32	 vidhi adhīna pravṛtti uttambhaka vākya viśeṣaḥ hi artha vādaḥ saḥ api pratyakṣa ādi aviruddhe sva arthe pramāṇam svatas prāmāṇyasya anapāyāt yatra virodha dhīḥ tatra api aviruddha artha upacāreṇa tad prāmāṇyam sa ca kvācid vidhi eka vākya tayā pramāṇībhavati iti artha vāda adhikaraṇa ādiṣu sthāpitam svatas prayojana bhūta artha viśeṣa viṣayaḥ tu svatantra tayā api prāmāṇyam prāpnoti iti samanvaya sūtra siddham tad prāpti abhilāṣe tu tad upāya vākya pravṛttiḥ sa caturdhā nindā praśaṃsā para kṛti purākalpa bhedāt niṣedha ādi śeṣa bhūtaḥ niṣedhya ādi doṣa vāda utra nindā vidhi ādi śeṣa bhūtaḥ vidheya ādi guṇa vādaḥ praśaṃsā eka anubandhī kathā viśeṣaḥ para kṛtiḥ aneka anubandhī tu purākalpaḥ hita anuśāsana rūpam vākyam iha vidhiḥ sa ca bahuvidhaḥ nitya naimittika kāmya saṃvalita vidhi niṣedha ādi bhedāt niyama parisaṃkhye api vidhi bhedau= eva tatra evam vivekaḥ aprāptasya vidhau prāptiḥ niyame prāpta pūraṇam bādhaḥ tu parisaṃkhyāyām prāptasya eva eka deśataḥ 
NP_3.2.33^1	 atha atra kaḥ nāma liṅā ādi pratyaya arthaḥ na tāvat apūrvam tasmin pramāṇa antara agocare vyutpatti ayogāt tad gocara tve tu apūrva tva vyāghātāt liṅā ādi bodhite vyutpattau= itaretara āśraya prasaṅgāt vimarśataḥ siddhiḥ syāt iti ced na vimarśasya smṛti anubhava atiriktasya anami upagamāt kriyā kāryevī utpannasya ca anvayā yogya tāyām api lakṣaṇa ādibhiḥ eva nirbāhya tvāt abhidhānāni atha akaraṇa ayogāt prathama vyutpatteḥ api sarvatra kāryaḥ eva iti niyama abhāvāt tathā gāmānaya ityādi prayojaka vṛddha vākya śravaṇa samanantaram gavānayane pravṛttam puruṣam ālokya pārśva sthaḥ vyutpitsuḥ cetana pravṛtteḥ kārya tā buddhi pūrvaka tvāt prayojya vṛddha kārya tā buddheḥ ca kāraṇa antara adarśanāt yat anantaram yat dṛśyate tat tasya kāraṇam iti prayojaka vṛddha vākyam eva prayojya vṛddha kārya tā buddheḥ kāraṇam iti adhyavasyati 
NP_3.2.33^2	 tathā kasyacid aputraḥ te jātaḥa iti kenacid ukte pratipanna putra utpatteḥ tasya priya tvam ca jñāyate vyutpitsuḥ putra janma vākya śrāviṇaḥ puruṣasya mukha vikāsam ālokya tasya priya artha pratipratti nimitta tva anumānāt tad pratīteḥ ca kāraṇa antara adarśanāt putra janam avākyam eva kāraṇam kalpayati na ca putra janmanaḥ priya tvam bālena ajñātam iti vācyam prajñāta putra janmanaḥ tasya prauḍhasya bhāṣā antara vat prathama vyutpattau= evam saṃbhavāt na udāharaṇam ādaraṇīyam iti ca nyāya vidaḥ 
NP_3.2.34^1	 tatas ca ye bālānām priya tvena saṃpratipannāḥ bhakṣya bhojya ādayaḥ tad darśī vyutpitsuḥ tad saṃpatti śrāviṇaḥ puruṣasya mukha vikāsa darśana ādi prakriyayā vyutpadyate iti kim na upapadyate priya antara smṛti ādibhiḥ api mukhe vikāsaḥ saṃbhavati iti ced tathā eva svayam tad adhīna prayojana antara smaraṇa ādinā api gavānayana kartavya tā bodhaḥ saṃbhavet āsatti viśeṣa vaśāt aneka prayoga anugateḥ ca vyavasthā iti ced tulyam tathā api tad tad priya anubandhi sulagna janma sukha prasava svādu vāc tvā ādi harṣa hetu artha antara saṃbhāvanayā viśeṣaḥ durniścayaḥ iti ced na gavānayanepi vatsa saṃyojana kṣīra saṃpādana ādi kartavyatā bodhakepi vākye tad artha gavānayana saṃbhavāt gāmānam etyādi vākyam gavān ayana kartavyatā eka bodhakam iti katham niścinuyāt anvaya vyatireka mahima vaśāt dṛṣṭa anugrahāt ca iti ced tulyam 
NP_3.2.34^2	 tat evam putra janma vākya udāharaṇa samīkārasya manda matīnām durāroha tvāt tad upekṣaṇena spaṣṭatara vyutpatti prakāraḥ yādṛcchikaḥ buddhi pūrvaḥ ca bhāṣya kāraiḥ darśitaḥ tat atra likhyate evam kila bālāḥ śabda artha saṃbandham avadhārayanti mātā pitṛ prabhṛtibhiḥ amba atāta mātula ādīn śaśi paśu nara mṛga pakṣi sarīsṛpa ādīn= ca enam avehi imam ca avadhāraya iti abhiprāyeṇa aṅgulyāḥ nirdiśya nirdiśya taiḥ taiḥ śabdaiḥ teṣu teṣu bahuśas śikṣitāḥ śanais śanais taiḥ eva śabdaiḥ teṣu teṣu artheṣu sva ātmanām budhdi utpattim dṛṣṭvā śabda arthayoḥ saṃbandha antara adarśanāt saṅketayitṛ puruṣa ajñānāt ca teṣu artheṣu teṣām śabdānām prayogaḥ bodhaka tva nibandhanaḥ iti niścinvanti punar ca vyutpanna itara śabdeṣu asya śabdasya ayam arthaḥ iti pūrva vṛddhaiḥ śikṣitāḥ sarva śabdānām artham avagamya para pratyāyanāya tad tad artha avabodhi vākya jātam prayuñjate 
NP_3.2.34^3	 prakāra antareṇa api śabda artha saṃbandha avadhāraṇam suśakam kenacid puruṣeṇa hasta ceṣṭā ādinā apitā te sukham āste iti devadattāya jñāpaya a iti preṣitaḥ kaścid tad jñāpane pravaṛttaḥ apitā te sukham āste a iti śabdam prayuṅkte pārśva sthonyaḥ vyutpitsuḥ mūka vat ceṣṭā viśeṣa jñaḥ tad jñāpane pravṛttam imam jñātvā anugataḥ tat jñāpanāya prayuktam imam śabdam śrutvā ayam śabdaḥ tad artha buddhi hetuḥ iti niścinoti iti kārya arthaḥ eva vyutpattiḥ iti nirbandhaḥ nirnibandhanaḥ iti nyā paḥ śaḥ atra pitā te sukham āste iti vākyasya sthāne apavarake daṇḍaḥ sthitaḥ iti udāharaṇa antara mātram anyatra uktam atas siddhāsiddhepya ādi a vyutpattiḥ bhavatu vā prathama vyutpattiḥ kāryaḥ eva tathā api prayoga anvaya vyatireka vaśāt eva śabda śaktiḥ vivecanīyāḥ prayujyante ca siddha parāḥ eva avivakṣita kartavyaiḥ śabdāḥ yathā kosau rājā kauravaḥ kautuka mātrāt eva hi atra praśnaḥ prativacanam ca tad anuvidhāyi a iva 
NP_3.2.34^4	 atas yathā padānām prātisvikī śaktiḥ siddhe kāryā ipi iti yathāsaṃbhavam niṣkṛṣyate tathā tātparyam api yathāyogam eva vyutpatti upāya tvepi ca kāryasya sarva śabda tātparya viṣaya tva ayukteḥ kārya vākyepi pravartaka tva ādi lakṣaṇam ca prādhānyam apūrvasya mṛgyam sukha duḥkha abhāvābhyām atiriktasya svatas svasmin pravartaka tva ayogāt vyutpatti daśāyām api asukha rūpasya ānayana ādeḥ anyaśeṣa tayā eva pravṛtti śeṣa tva avagamāt atas sukhe duḥkha nivṛttau vā sākṣāt kāryatva bodhaḥ tad artha tayā tad sādhane apekṣita tvena ca sādhana vat sādhana sādhanepi kārya tā bodha upapattiḥ na ca sukha ādi tvam apūrvasya na ca tad sādhana tayā tat pravartaka tvam abhyupagatam abhyupagamepi laukika sevya prītyā iva devatā prītyā eva śruti ādi siddhayā kāla antara bhāvi phala siddhauliṅvācyatayā svarūpeṇa vā tad kalpanā yogāt rātri satra ādinayāt ca pratiṣṭhā deśa viśeṣa śata yātanā sā dhana tva ghṛta añjana= chāga ādi parigraha vat vidhi apekṣitam pratītam ca devatā prīti ātmakam eva apūrvam liṅvācyatayā svarūpeṇa vā dvāram upakalpyatām kim anyena  
NP_3.2.36	 yat ca jalpanti ardha lokāyatikāḥ vigrahaḥ haviḥ ādānam yugapad karma sannidhiḥ prītiḥ phala pradānam ca devatānām na vidyate iti tat api jaimini hṛdaya anabhijña tā nibandhanam na hi svatas pramāṇa āmnāya smṛti purāṇa ādi siddhāḥ sādhaka bādhaka pramāṇa agocarāḥ devatā vigraha ādayaḥ hātum yuktāḥ na ca ayogyeṣu anupalambha mātreṇa bādhaḥ śaṅakyaḥ atiprasaṅgi tvāt sākṣāt lokāyatikavāda prasaṅgāt stutyāḥ vidhi śeṣa bhūteṣu api artha vādeṣu tad artha tayā eva sva artham abhidadhāneṣu na vākya bheda ādi doṣaḥ stuti ādi paratvepi na mukhya artha bādhaḥ sva artha bādhaka abhāvaḥ sva artha prahāṇa ayogāt na ca sarvā stutiḥ ayathārthāḥ na ca asatā guṇena kathitena stuti siddhiḥ yatra tu mukhya artha bādhaḥ tatra api aipacārikam kiñcid ālambanam abhipretam anyathā viḍambana mātram eva syāt na ca upacchandana mātra tā tad jñāne puṃsaḥ pravṛtti anupakārāt nirūpakasya ca tad ajñāna ayogāt anyathā bhrānti mūla pravṛtti tva prasaṅgāt samanvaya adhikaraṇa nayāt ca siddha eka parāḥ santi bhāgāḥ tad anudhāvinaḥ ca itihāsa purāṇa ādayaḥ 
NP_3.2.37^1	 nanu artha vāda adhikaraṇe vidhinā tu eka vākya tvāt stuti arthena vidhīnām syuḥ iti sarveṣām artha vādānām vidhi eka vākya tvam uktam samanvaya sūtre tu katham tat viruddha uktiḥ mā evam arthavāda aprāmāṇya pūrva pakṣa pratikṣepāya vidhi eka vākya tayā prāmāṇyam saṃbhavati iti etāvat mātram arthavāda adhikaraṇe sthāpitam vidhi eka vākya tve brahma svarūpa tātparya abhāva pūrvapakṣaḥ tu apavaraka nidhi sadbhāva ādi vākya vat svatas prayojana bhūta artha viṣaya vākyānām bhinna vākya tayā api prāmāṇyam upapādya samanvaya sūtre pratikṣipyate iti virodha abhāvāt 
NP_3.2.37^2	 api ca autsargiṅkam āpavādi kañca tam tam artham pratipādayatsu vākyeṣu viṣaya vyavasthayā virodha śamanam vyākaraṇa ādiṣu api dṛṣṭam iti atas eva brāhmaṇa śeṣāḥ artha vādāḥ iti ārṣam api vākyam autsargika viṣayam avagantavyam yā tu śabda bhāvanā eva liṅā ādi arthaḥ iti kaumārila kusṛtiḥ sā tu pratīti viṃsavāda ādi pratihatā na hi vidhi vākya śrāvī puruṣaḥ liṅā ādi sva vyāpāram abhidhatte atas mayā pravartitavyam iti manyate na ca yāga ādi svarūpe liṅa ādi vyāpāre ca kenacid vākyena samuccitya pratipāditepi kaścid pravartamānaḥ dṛśyate 
NP_3.2.37^3	 liṅā ādeḥ ca jñāyamāna tva lakṣaṇa vyāpāra mātrāt śakti lakṣaṇa vyāpārāt vā pravartaka tve vyutpatteḥ prāk api tatas pravṛtti prasaṅgaḥ vyutpatteḥ api sahakāri tve tad sāpekṣāyāḥ nirviṣayāyāḥ tasyāḥ asaṃbhavāt tad viṣayaḥ vācyaḥ na ca sva vyāpāre liṅā ādiḥ kvacid vyutpannaḥ sarveṣām api śabdānām sva vyāpāra atiriktaḥ eva hi arthe vyutpatti ye ca abhidha ādayaḥ śabdāḥ tepi na śṛṅga grāhikayā sva vyāpāram abhidadhati api tu śabda mātra vyāpāre tad pravṛtteḥ sāmānya upādhi kroḍīkāreṇa sva vyāpārasya api niveśaḥ atas eva abhidha ādi śabda abhidheyasya nimittasya ca sāmānyatas pratipanna tvāt vyutpatti upapattiḥ 
NP_3.2.37^4	 liṅā ādeḥ tu sva vyāpāre pratīte tatra vyutpattiḥ syāt tad pratītiḥ vyutpannena ced anyonya āśrayaḥ avyutpannena ced atiprasaṅgaḥ iti na ca iṣṭa sā adhana tva mātram liṅā ādi bodhyam ataveṣṭa sādhanam idam ateḥ kuru a iti saha prayoga darśanāt na ca ādara ādi nibandhanā punar uktiḥ iyam pratīteḥ atathātvāt hetu sādhya nirdeśa ayogāt ca akartavyam idam atas kuru iti api dṛśyate iti ced na brāhmaṇasya kartavyam idam atas tava api kartavyam iti vat sāmanya viśeṣa ādi vivakṣāyāḥ avirodhāt atyanta eka artha vivakṣāyām tu tatra api prayoga ayogāt 
NP_3.2.37^5	 atas eva āptasya vaktuḥ icchā mātram liṅā ādi arthaḥ iti pratyuktam āptasya iṣṭam idam atā mama idam kāryam iti pravartamāna puruṣa abhilāpa viśeṣa darśanāt na ca liṅā artha tvāt eva nimantraṇa ādi vat vidhiḥ api vaktṛ abhiprāya mātram iti vācyam saṃbhāvanā ādibhiḥ viśeṣa vihitaiḥ ca anaikāntyāt eka śabda vācya tā mātreṇa eka tve ca aneka artha śabda bhaṅga prasaṅge dṛṣṭānta upi na sidhyet yadi api para mate hi udayana uktā niṣedha anupapattiḥ tathā api na sā asmat pakṣam avagāhate kartavyatāyāḥ vidhi artha tve na kartavyaḥ iti nañanvaya avirodhāt kartṛvyā pāra sādhya tvam eva ca kartavya tvam tathā hi veda artha saṅgahe liṅa ādeḥ koyam arthaḥ parigṛhītaḥ a iti praśna pūrvakam pratyuktam yaja deva pūjāyām iti devatā ārādhana bhūta yāga ādeḥ prakṛti arthasya kartṛ vyāpāra sādhyatām vyutpatti siddhām liṅādayobhidadhati iti na kiñcid anupapannam kartṛ vācinām pratyayānām prakṛti arthasya kartṛ vyāpāra saṃbandha prakāraḥ hi vācyaḥ bhūta vartamānatā ādi manye vadanti liṅā ādayaḥ tu kartṛ vyāpāra sādhya tām vadanti iti 
NP_3.2.37^6	 bhāṣye ca ādya sūtre atas vidhi vākyeṣu api dhātu arthasya kartṛ vyā pāra sādhya tā mātram śabda anuśāsana siddham eva liṅā ādeḥ vācyam iti adhyavasīyate dhātu arthasya ca yāga ādeḥ agni ādi devatā antaryāmi parama puruṣa samārādhana rūpa tā samārādhitāt parama puruṣāt phala siddhiḥ ca iti aphalam atas upapatteḥ a iti pratipādayiṣyate iti atra kartṛ vyā pāra sādhya tā mātram iti niṣkṛṣṭa artha pradarśanāya uktam pratipatti prakāraḥ tu yajeta ityādau sva vyāpāra sādhya yāga ādi viśiṣṭaḥ iti kartṛ prādhānyena eva yathā uktam dīpe kartṛ adhi karaṇaiḥ yajeta upāsīta iti hi kartari lakāraḥ atas kartāram eva bodhayati śāstram iti 
NP_3.2.37^7	 uktam ca veda artha saṃgrahepi svarga kāmaḥ yajeta iti evamādiṣu lakāra vācya kartṛ viśeṣa samarpakāṇām svarga kāma ādi padānām niyojya viśeṣa samarpaka tvam śabda anuśāsanā viruddham iti yadi api dīpa granthaḥ puṃsaḥ kartṛ tvam śruti siddham iti atra eva tad paraḥ tathā api dhātu artha sādhya tā paraliṅā ādiṣu api karta pradhāna tayā vṛttim pradarśya sāṃravyān pratikṣipati iti tādarthyāt tatra api tat paratvam eva grāhyam pacati ityādau pākam karoti ityādi nipuṇa vyākriyāḥ ca kṛti karma tayā eva dhātu arthasya anvayam vyañjayanti 
NP_3.2.38^1	 śrī gīta ābhāṣye ca etat vyañjitam ayudhyasva a iti atra ayuddha ākhyam karma ārabhasva a iti vyākhyānāt vyākaraṇāt karaṇa tayā ca dhātu arthasya anvaye katham kriyā viśeṣaṇasya karma vibhakti anta tā na hi viśeṣyeṇa viśeṣaṇam bhāvayet iti anveti phalasya apūrvasya vā bhavadbhiḥ bhāvya tva abhyupagamāt vartamāna vyapadeśa ādiṣu ca sādhya antara abhāvepi na viśeṣaṇa mātram sādhyam na ca prathama antam kiyā viśeṣaṇam karaṇa pakṣepi dhātu arthena ananvaya prasaṅgāt ananvita viśeṣaṇa tā ādi anupapatteḥ 
NP_3.2.38^2	 na ca akarma vibhakti antena dhātunā karma vibhakti antasya katham sāmānādhikaraṇyam iti vācyam karaṇa vibhakti antena api asāmāna ādhikaraṇya prasaṅgāt na ca prapavatīyamāne karma tvena anvaye kaścid doṣaḥ dṛśyate priyaṅgu kāmaḥ kṛṣim kuryāt itivat svarga kāmaḥ yāgam kuryāt iti vākya arthepi virodha abhāvāt tadvat eva arthataḥ tasya tad upāya tva siddheḥ kena iti karaṇa ākāṅkṣāyāḥ api śamanāt nāmadheya gata tṛtīya anvayopi na avaśyam sāmānādhikaraṇyena tad tad nāmakaiḥ karma viśeṣaiḥ devatā pūjām kuryāt iti evaṃpara tvepi svarasa anvayāt sāmānya viśeṣa rūpeṇa vyadhikaraṇa nirdeśa upapatteḥ 
NP_3.2.38^3	 cāṭu vādena rājānam prīṇayet itivāt yāgam kuruṣva ityādau na kṛñarthasya api sādhya tva prasaṅgaḥ tasya eva kartṛ vyāpāra rūpa tve tad sādhya tva ayogāt prakṛti pratyayoḥ anyatarasya kṛtau= udāsīna tvāt ekaḥ dvau bahavaḥ ityādi vat tatra api yadā karma tām vivakṣati tadā api kartṛ vyāpāra antaram abhipretya vā bheda upacāreṇa vā nirvāhaḥ yathā udaka āharaṇa kriyām karoti ityādau na ca tāvatā anavasthā prati iti anāroheṇa vyavahārasya paryavasita tvāt agnihotram juhoti iti ādi prayogaḥ ca asmad pakṣa anukūlaḥ atas kim kena katham iti bhavat prokta vat kimartham kim kena katham iti ākāṅkṣā catuṣṭaye svarga ādinā kim artham iti ākāṅkṣā pūraṇam devatām prīṇayet iti kim iti ākāṅkṣāna śāntiḥ jyotiṣṭomena ityādi nāmadheya ādibhiḥ kena iti ākāṅkṣā pūryate katham iti ākāṅkṣā pūraṇam tu bhavatām asmākam ca tulyam eva iti śābdoyam panthāḥ atas tat tad adhikāriṇaḥ sva sādhya dhātu artha viśiṣṭa tā bodhini yajeta iti ādau tad tad dhātu artha anuṣṭhāne phalam ananuṣṭhāne pratyavāyaḥ ca sarva praśāsituḥ saṅkalpāt bhavati iti api vākyāt avagatam 
NP_3.2.38^4	 avāntara devatā buddhi vṛtti viśeṣaḥ tu sa dvāraka yajate śrāddha bhoji puruṣa prīti ādi vat ānuṣaṅgikaḥ anyathā kalpa antara ādiṣu pralīna prācīna devatā gaṇeṣu pūrva kalpa anuṣṭhita karma phala anutpatti prasaṅgāt atas eva hi ekasya eva śruti rājñā anyeṣām ca āra adhaka tva vat ārādhya tvam api tat ā āyattam iti nārāyaṇa āryaiḥ tu evam uktam āptasya hita kāmasya niyogam kecid ūcire bhāṣya kāra upi bhagavān etat eva anvamanyata iti atra ca sva śāsanau= abodhi śāstram ca pradiśya iti bhāṣyam abhisaṃhitam idam ca vidhi niṣedha anuvartana ati vartana prayukta nigraha anugraha vacana balāt siddham 
NP_3.2.38^5	 śrutiḥ smṛtiḥ mama eva ājñāḥ yaḥ tām ullaṅghya vartate ājñācchedī mama drohī mad bhakta upi na vaiṣṇavaḥ iti avidhiḥ preraṇam a iti ca vyākāri vaiyākaraṇaiḥ preraṇam ca śāsanam eva tattva ratna ākara kāraiḥ ca evam uktam kriyā tad śaktiḥ vā kim api tad apūrvam pitṛ sura prasādaḥ vā kartuḥ phala daḥ iti raṅga īśa kudṛśaḥ tvad arceṣṭā pūrte phalam api bhavat prīti jam iti trayī vṛddhāḥ tat tad vidhiḥ api bhavat preraṇam iti nitya naimittika ādi vidhi bhedeṣu ca praśāsituḥ abhiprāya viśeṣāḥ vyañjitāḥ ājñā te sa nimitta nitya vidhayaḥ svarga ādi kāmyat vidhiḥ sonujñā śaṭha citta śāstra vaśatā upāya ubhicāra śrutiḥ 
NP_3.2.38^6	 sarvāḥ yasya samasta śāsituḥ aho śrīraṅga rājasya te rakṣā ākūta nivedinī śrutiḥ api tvad nitya śāstiḥ tatas iti api ca veda artha saṅga hepi upāttam draviḍa bhāṣyam sva śāsana anuvartinaḥ jñātvā kāruṇyāt svabhāvāt śraddhayait vidvān karma dakṣaḥ iti anantaram ca ayam eva arthaḥ bhagavat gītāyām api darśitaḥ ye me matam idam nityam anutiṣṭhanti mānavāḥ śraddhāvantonasūyantaḥ mucyante tepi karmabhiḥ ye tu etat abhyasūyantaḥ na anutiṣṭhanti me matam sarva jñāna vimūḍhān= tān viddhi naṣṭān acetasaḥ 
NP_3.2.38^7–3.2.39	 iti sva ājñā anuvartinaḥ praśasya viparītān vinindan punar api sva jña anupālanam akurvatām āsura prakṛti antarbhāvam abhidhāya adhamā gatiḥ ca uktetiḥ idṛśaḥ eva vidhi śabda arthaḥ vedāntibhiḥ svīkṛtaḥ iti parepi kecid anvavādiṣuḥ atas mūla skandhīkṛta niyogam dhātu arthasya kartṛ vyā pāra sādhya tvam vā nirviṣaya preraṇa asaṃbhavāt tad sādhya tva paryantam preṣaṇam eva vā liṅā ādi asādhāraṇa arthaḥ iti sthite vidhi ni mantraṇā mantraṇa adhīṣṭa saṃpraśna prārthaneṣu lij iti samabhivyāhṛta nimantraṇa ādi samāna yogakṣema tayā vidhi śabda artha tayā vyākṛtasya preṣaṇasya eva liṅā ādi śabda vācya tvam yuktam iti anyathā api preṣaṇam antargatam eva iti apare idam ca vidhi vākyānām īśvara śāsana ātmaka tvam jaimininā api sūcitam eva codanā lakṣaṇa ūrthaḥ dharmaḥ iti codanā śabdaḥ hi ca udakam kañcid puruṣam sūcayati ahṛdayāt api śābara udāharaṇāt idam vyajyate ācārya coditaḥ karomi iti hi dṛśyate iti 
NP_3.2.40	 evam codanā śabda sūcitaḥ ca puruṣaḥ sva vākyena prāk eva viśeṣataḥ darśitaḥ apicaḥ autpattika sūtre tasya jñānam upadeśaḥ iti asūtrayat upadeśa upi hi upadeṣṭāram ākṣipati tad pramāṇam bādarāyaṇasya iti sūtra khaṇḍe ca svasya su ācārya bhūta bādarāyaṇa samāna abhiprāya tvam vyañjitam sa ca bādarāyaṇaḥ jaiminim sva śiṣyam abhyupagata īśvara ādi tattvam sākṣāt api avirodham jaiminiḥ ityādiṣu bahuṣu sūtreṣu adarśayat pratikṣepaḥ tu kvācid kaḥ anya para uktyāpāta pratīta artha mandam ati moha nirāsa arthaḥ vā kṣudra pramāda mātrasya api uddhāra arthaḥ vā iti na pradhāna virodha kalpana liṅgam arthavāda adhikaraṇe ca vidhinā tu eka vākya tvāt stuti arthena vidhīnām syuḥ iti preraṇa rūpa vidhi pratipāda kaliṅā ādi avayava dvārā samudāya bhūtam vidhi uddeśa vākyam lakṣayitvā tad eka vākya tvam artha vādānām vadan kṛtsnasya vedasya īśvarājñā rūpa vidhi pratipādaka tvam tat vākya kaṇṭha uktam asūcayat evam anyatra api bhāvyam 
NP_3.2.41^1	 evam śrutiḥ tāvat īśva rājñā tad anuvidhānāt smṛtiḥ api brāhmaṇa mantra artha vāda mayāḥ hi anantāḥ vedāḥ saṅkīrṇāḥ vikīrṇāḥ kvacid kadācid utsannāḥ ca tatra kṛtsna vedinaḥ manu ādayaḥ tad tad deśa kāla viśeṣeṣu akṛtsna vedinām tattva anuṣṭhāna viplava praśamanāya sva anubhūtān veda arthān yathāvat nibadhnanti atas tad mūla una ādi vācām artha nirṇayaḥ śruti smṛti virodhe tu smṛtyā mūla antara anumānāt anuṣṭhāna vikalpam kecid āhuḥ sarveṣām guṇatrayavatām āptatama tvepi kvācid ka bhrama saṃbhavāt śrutyā smṛti bādhaḥ iti apare tattva viṣa naye tu virodhe bādhaḥ eva ānya paryaṃvā vastuni vikalpa asaṃbhavāt smṛti dvaya virodhe tu parigraha tāratamya ādibhiḥ vyavasthā na ca kvacid smṛtīnām aprāmāṇye sarvatra anāśvāsaḥ bādhakā darśanāt kāraṇa doṣa kpteḥ ca niyata liṅga abhāvāt saṃvāda bhūyaḥ tu a ādibhiḥ parigrahāni atha anupapattyā ca śruteḥ eva mūla tva kalpana upapatteḥ anyathā pauruṣeya vākyasya sarvasya aprāmāṇya prasaṅge vilīnam āgamena 
NP_3.2.41^2	 na ca etat na aniṣṭam iti vaktum śakyam pitṛ ādi āpta vākyam pramāṇīkṛtya ca avārkasya pravṛtti darśanāt na ca kvācitka saṃvāda mātreṇa bāhya āgameṣu api visrambha avakāśaḥ pratyakṣa śruti virodha bhūyaḥ tvena vaidika parigraha abhāvena veda bāhya tva prasiddhyā veda pratikṣepāt ca veda ākhya mūla kalpanasya aśakya tvāt na ca alaukikam pratyakṣa ādi mūla tva saṃbhavaḥ yoga ja sā akṣātkāra mūla tva kptiḥ api veda aviruddha sthale syāt na ca tatra api niścayaḥ viparīta upalambhasya api saṃbhavāt iti tatas ca veda mūlāḥ smṛtayasnividhāḥ dharmaśāstra itihāsa purāṇa bhedāt tatra ādyayoḥ adūra viprakarṣāt eka vidyā sthāna niveśaḥ atra ca adhikṛta anadhikṛta vibhāgena bala abala niyatiḥ ābhāsa āhnike darśitāḥ purāṇeṣu api sāttvika rāja sādi vibhāgaḥ ca 
NP_3.2.42^1	 yānipunar sāṃkhya yoga pāśupatapañca rātrāṇi tāni api dharma śāstra bhedāḥ eva pariśuddha ātma cintana rūpa jñāna yoga pradarśana adhikṛtam śāstram sāṃkhyam samādhi paryanta karma yoga niṣṭham śāstram yogaḥ pratibuddha itara viṣaya paśupati bhajana pratipādakam pāśupatam pratibuddha viṣaya bhagavat ananya bhajana upadeśa pravṛttam tu śāstram pañca rātram etāni ca kvacid kvacid aṃśe paraspara upajīvīni paraspara virodhe tu veda anusāreṇa bala abala vyavasthā veda viruddhe tu aṃśe bādhaḥ pramādasya anīśvareṣu sarveṣu saṃbhavāt vipralambhasya tu asura ādi vyāmohana udyate sākṣāt īśvare api yathā uktam bhagavatā eva tvam hi rudrapa mahā bāho moha śāstrāṇi kāraya 
NP_3.2.42^2	 alpa āyāsam darśayitvā phalam śīghram pradarśaya aham moham kariṣyāmi yaḥ manam mohayiṣyati iti atas yat sāṃkhyar iśvarān adhiṣṭhita pradhāna ādi pratipādanam yat ca īśvaram abhyupagamya kevala nimitta kāraṇa tva pratiphalana kalpa aiśvarya varṇanam yoge yat ca pāśupate parāvara tattva vyatyaya veda viruddha ācāra ādi kalpanam tat sarvam vyapohya śiṣṭe ḥṃśe prāmāṇyam grāhyam na ca etat tuṣa taṇḍula vibhāga vat alpa jñaiḥ śakyam atas hi śārīrake trayāṇām nirāsaḥ pañca rātram tu kṛtsnam śruti vat smṛti vat vā pramāṇam pratyakṣa śruti ādi virodha abhāvāt 
NP_3.2.42^3	 mahābhārate ca āptatama mānava dharma śāstrasya api tad mūla tva ukteḥ atyādareṇa vyāsa diparigraha viśeṣāt īśvara dayā mūla tvena ca kāraṇa doṣa prasaṅga abhāvāt vedānteṣu yathāsāram saṃgṛhya bhagavān hariḥ bhakta anukampayā vidvān saṃcikṣepa yathāsukham iti ca tatra eva vyakteḥ veda prāmāṇya aṅgīkāratad artha ukti bhūyaḥ tvatad vaiśadya hetu tva vacana sādhu paritrāṇa artha tva sattva uttara nārada ādi śrotṛka tva ādi nibandhana spaṣṭa prāmāṇya tvāt na ca vipralambha artham tathā nibandhaḥ anyatra api prasaṅgāt adhītāḥ bhagavan vedāḥ iti ādeḥ durgraha tva mātra tātparyeṇa veda nindā ādi rūpa tva abhāvāt 
NP_3.2.42^4	 nindā rūpa tva īpi udita homa nindā vannindita itara praśaṃsana pravṛtteḥ saṅkarṣaṇaḥ nāma jīvaḥ jāyate iti ādeḥ tu avatāra ādi gocara tvasya tatra eva siddheḥ śarīrake ca utpatti asaṃbhavātna ca kartuḥ karaṇam iti sūtra dvayena pūrva pakṣam kṛtvā vijñāna ādi bhāve vā tat apratiṣedhaḥ vipratiṣedhāt ca iti tad prāmāṇya pratiṣedhaḥ parihṛtaḥ tathā nirmūla tva asat parigraha sat parigraha abhāva vaudika saṃskāra varjana avaidika saṃskāra vidhāna vidyā sthāna parigaṇana abhāva kṣudra vidyā bāhulya ādi manda śaṅkānām bhagavat yāmuna munibhiḥ parihāraḥ prapañcitaḥ iti na iha pratanyate 
NP_3.2.43	 evam sākṣāt īśvara dayā mūla tvāt manu ādi nibandhanebhyosyā atirekaḥ teṣām śruti virodhe sati bādhya tvam api saṃbhavet guṇatraya vaśya tayā kādācid ka bhrama ādi saṃbhavāt smṛti ādīnām hi śruti mūla tayā eva prāmāṇyam iti bhāṣyepi uktam tad upari api iti adhikaraṇe saṅkīrṇa brāhmaṇa mantra artha vāda mūleṣu dharmaṃśāḥ tra itihāsa purāṇeṣu iti 
NP_3.2.44^1	 tatas eva ca eṣām viprakīrṇa śākhā mūla tvam siddhāntaḥ iti api sūcitam kvacid kadācid keṣāñcid śākhā viśeṣāṇām ucchedaḥ te ca punar vyāsa ādibhiḥ kvacid kadācid pravartyante iti etāvatā ucchinna śākhā mūla tvam astu uktam ca bhagavatā āpastambena teṣām utsannāḥ pāṭhāḥ prayogāt anumīyante iti manu ādi vacana prāmāṇyam nyāyam antareṇa api śrutyā eva siddham yat vai kiñca manuḥ avadat tad bheṣajam ityādibhiḥ evam śiṣṭa ācārasya api yathā te tatra varteran tathā tratra vartarthoḥ yāni asmākam su caritāni tāni tvayā upāsyāni ityādibhiḥ smṛtiḥ ca smṛti śīle ca tad vidām ācāraḥ ca eva sādhūnām ityādi śrutyā eva dharma nirṇaye saṃbhavati kim dharma śāstreṇa iti āśaṅkya āha marīciḥ durbodhāḥ vaudikāḥ śabdāḥ prakīrṇa tvāt ca ye khilāḥ tad jñaiḥ te eva spaṣṭa arthāḥ smṛti tantre pratiṣṭhitāḥ iti sati api dharmaśāstre gṛhya apekṣām darśayati devalaḥ manu ādayaḥ prayoktāraḥ dharma śāstrasya kīrtitāḥ 
NP_3.2.44^2	 tad prayukta prayoktāraḥ gṛhya kārāḥ sva mantrataḥ iti atas dharma śāstra gṛhya ādi sāpekṣa tvam veda artha nirṇayasya virodhe ca yathāyogam bala abala vyavasthā siddhāḥ bhagavat dharma śāstrasya tu pañca rātrasya śruti ādi virodhe ṣoḍaśi grahaṇa ādeḥ iva deśa kāla adhikārī avasthā viśeṣa viṣaya tayā vikalpaḥ eva śruteḥ iva asya api doṣa saṃbhāvanā viraha ādi siddheḥ āhuḥ ca evam abhiyuktāḥ vede kartṛ ādi abhāvāt iti ārabhya tasmāt sāṃkhyam sa yogam sa paśupati matam kutracid pañca rātram sarvatra eva pramāṇam tat idam avagatam pañcamāt eva vedāt iti anyatra ca upaniṣadi tu bahvyām vyāvaghoṣya āma doṣa pratihata guṇa rāśiḥ ghuṣyate tārkṣyaketuḥ śrutiḥ api tad upajñaiḥ pañca rātraiḥ vikalpam na labhate iti sūktam bhāṣya kṛt yā muna āryaiḥ iti tat etat yāmunā ācāryaiḥ āgama prāmāṇye saṃbhāvita samasta pūrva pakṣa yukti nirākaraṇena prapañcitam tad anusāreṇa eva bhāṣya kāraiḥ śrī pāñcarātra adhikaraṇam vyākhyātam śruti mūlam idam tantram pramāṇam kalpa sūtra vat 
NP_3.2.44^3	 ityādi vacanam tu trayī anta mūla tayā ekāyana śruti mūla tayā ca yojyam na ca atra veda tve sandegdhavyam yam vākeṣu anuvākeṣu niṣad su upaniṣatsu ca mahataḥ veda vṛkṣasya mūla bhūtaḥ mahān ayam skandha bhūtāḥ ṛc a ādyāḥ te śākhābhūtāḥ tathā mune ityādi vacanāt tathā ṛgveda pāṭhe paṭhitam vratam etat su duścaram iti saṃvāda pradarśanāt veda śākhā vyāsa daśāyām nirukta śākhāyāḥ api gaṇita tvāt bhagavat śāstra sāra bhūta sāttvata pauṣkara ādiṣu rahasya āmnāya vidhāne ekāyanīya śākhā uktaiḥ mantraiḥ parama pāvanaiḥ ityādibhiḥ tad śrutitpratipādanāt 
NP_3.2.44^4	 atra bhagavat yāmuna munibhiḥ eva uktaḥ granthaḥ likhyate yat api uktam agarbhādhāna ādi dāha anta saṃskāra antara sevanāt bhāgavatā nāma brāhmaṇyam a iti tatra api ajñānam eva aparādhyati na punar āyuṣmataḥ doṣaḥ yatas ete vaṃśa paramparayā vājasaneya śākhām adhīyānāḥ kātyāyana ādi gṛhya ukta mārgeṇa garbhādhāna ādi saṃskārān kurvate ye punar sāvitrī anuvacana prabhṛti trayī dharmā tyāgena ekāyana śruti vihitān eva catvāriṃśat saṃskārān kurvate tepi sva śākhā gṛhya ukta dharmam yathāvat anutiṣṭhamānā na śākhā antarīya karma ananuṣṭhānāt brāhmaṇyāt pracyavante anyeṣām api paraspara śākhā vihita karma ananuṣṭhāna nimitta abra āhmaṇya prasaṅgāt sarvatra hi jāti caraṇa gotra adhikāra ādi vyavasthitāḥ eva samaya ācārāḥ upalabhyante 
NP_3.2.44^5	 yadi api sarva śākhā pratyayam ekam karma tathā api na paraspara vilakṣaṇa adhikāri sambaddhāḥ dharmāḥ kvacid samuccīyante vilakṣaṇāḥ trayī vihita svarga putra ādi viṣaya upabhoga sādhana aindra āgneya ādi karma adhikāribhyaḥ dvijebhyaḥ trayī anta ekāyana śruti vihita vijñāna abhigamana upādāna ijyā prabhṛti bhagavat prāpti eka upāya karma adhikāriṇaḥ mumukṣavaḥ brāhmaṇāḥ iti na ubhayeṣām api anyonya śākhā vihita karma ananuṣṭhānam abrāhmaṇyam āpādayati yathā ca ekāyana śākhāyāḥ apauruṣeya tvam tathā kāśmīrāgama prāmaṇyam eva prapañcitam iti na iha prastūyate prakṛtānām tu bhāgavatānām sāvitrī anuvacana ādi trayī sambandhasya sphuṭataramu palabdhiḥ na tad tyāga nimitta vrātya tva ādi sandeham sahate iti 
NP_3.2.45^1	 caturvidham ca idam pañca rātram āgama siddhāntaḥ divya siddhāntaḥ tantra siddhāntaḥ tatra antara siddhāntaḥ ca iti caturvidham ca idam veda mūla bhūta aṃśasya upabṛṃhaṇam tad abhiprāyeṇa hi uktam mahābhārate mahataḥ veda vṛkṣasya mūla bhūtaḥ mahān ayam ityādi caturṇām ca eṣām lakṣaṇa ādikam śrī pauṣkara ādiṣu bhagavatā eva darśitam yat ca teṣu caturṣu sādhāraṇya asādha araṇya arca upasaṃhārya anupasaṃhārya ādikam vaktavyam tat sarvam śrī pāñcarātra rakṣā siddhānta vyavasthāyām sarva parāmarśena sādhitam asmābhiḥ iti tatra eva tad vistaraḥ sāttvata dharma goptuḥ ananyaiḥ anusandheyaḥ iti na atra prabrūmaḥ 
NP_3.2.45^2	 evam sthite kecid bāhlīka prāyāḥ āgama bāhyāḥ śrīmat vaikhānasa prāmāṇye viśerate tatra tāvat kalpasūtram na apramāṇam itara vat eva kalpasūtra tvāt tad kartuḥ ca kalpasūtra kāra tva prasiddheḥ veda aviruddha tvāt vaidika mantraiḥ eva sakala dharma vidhānāt sūtra antarāṇām api kuṇḍa sanniveśa lakṣaṇa ādiṣu kvacid kvacid tad upajīvanāt varṇa āśrama dharmāṇām anukūlam nārāyaṇa paratva pratipādana ādeḥ api sattva mūla tvena prāmāṇya eka hetu tvāt harim eva smaret nityam karma pūrvā pareṣu api 
NP_3.2.45^3	 dhyāyet nārāyaṇam devam snāna ādiṣu ca karmasu ityādinā śaunaka ādibhiḥ api tathā eva vidhānāt vaṃśa paramparayā ca vaikhānasaiḥ adhīyamāna tayā viplavasya api anavakāśa tvāt astu kim api tat idam tat iti kim niyākamam iti ced itara anupalamaḥ tad upalambhaḥ ca anyathā sarvatra śruti smṛti ādīnām tathā tathā saṃśaya prasaṅgāt astu idam eva tat pramāṇam ca tathā api bhārgava ādi catuṣkasya katham prāmāṇyam iti ced na ukta uttara tvāt mahā ṛṣi praṇīta tva veda aviruddha tva ādeḥ sama tvāt pañca rātra virodha usti iti ced na tattve tad abhāvāt kartavya kriyā ādi bhedasya api pratiniyata adhikāri viṣaya tvena eva upapatteḥ kalpasūtra prakriyā bheda vat āgama divya tantra tantra antara rūpa pañcarātra avāntara catuṣka kriyā ādi vibhāga vat ca āśvamodhike śrī vaiṣṇava dharma śāstre dvitayam api sama prāmāṇyatayā upāttam dvayoḥ api paraspara prāmāṇyam viṣṇoḥ tantram dvidhā proktam ityādiṣu vyañjitam paraspara ākṣepa vacanāni tu ikṣu bhakṣa kṛti cikīrṣubhiḥ asa hiṣṇubhiḥ upakṣiptāni vā sva śāstra praśaṃsā artha vāda rūpāṇi vā iti na tatas virodhaḥ 
NP_3.2.46^1	 nanu bhārgava ādīni na tāvat kalpasūtrāṇi tathā anabhyupagamāt aprasiddheḥ ayukteḥ ca  na smṛti antarāṇi manu ādiṣu apāṭhāt tadvat tad prasiddhi abhāvāt ca ana ca svatantra tantra antarāṇi sāṃkhya yoga ādi saha pāṭhā darśanāt vaikhānasa anuvartanāt ca tat katamām vidhāma valambyā amīṣām prāmāṇyam ucyate  manu atri bhārgava ādi vat nāradīya ādi vat ca dharma śāstra tayā eva teṣām api prāmāṇyam aṣṭādaśa ādi parigaṇanasya upalakṣaṇa tāyāḥ prāmāṇikaiḥ abhyupagamāt smṛti antareṣu deva utsava ādi prapañcanam na asti iti ced mā bhūt prapañcanam svarūpam tāvat anujñātam tad prapañca parāṇām tathā api jīvānām anta tonyonya vaiṣamya mātrasya ca sārvatrika tvāt nikṛṣṭa ādhikārikāṇi tāni iti ced na teṣu anyeṣu ca brāhmaṇya eka pradhāna tva vacatāt tathā upalabdheḥ ca katham teṣām brāhmaṇyam iti ced śāntam pāpam śravasī pidadhīmahi tathā api vaktavyam 
NP_3.2.46^2	 dṛśyante hi ete vaṃśa paramparayā vedam adhīyānāḥ vekhānasa sūtra ukta vaidika sakala saṃskāra śālinaḥ varṇa āśrama dharma karmaṭhāḥ bhagavat ekāntāḥ brāhmaṇāḥ nūnam amīṣām brāhmaṇya eka kāraṇena bhāgavata tvena eva viparītam bambhrami iti brāhmaṇa gardabhaḥ anyathā vaikhānasa kalpasya api niradhikāri tvena aprāmāṇya prasaṅgaḥ astu tad prāmāṇyam santu ca deśa antare kāla antare vā tad adhikāriṇaḥ amī tu katame iti ced deśa antara ādau= api evam vaktum śakya tvāt viparītam vā kasmāt na syāt  evam ca sati sūtra antara ādiṣu api kaḥ samāśvāsaḥ  vaikhānasānām nikṛṣṭa jāti tva vacana vivādābhyām sandeha viṣaya tvam iti ced āpta grantha stha tā dṛśa vacana abhāvāt bhāvepyeteṣām nikṛṣṭa jāti tve pramāṇa abhāvāt āgama prāmāṇya ukta sātvata ādi samākhyā nirvāha sama tvāt na hi aneka arthaḥ śabdaḥ na asti na ca śabda aikyāt artha aikyam śabda bhedena artha bhedaḥ vā anyathā vilīnam tṛtīya āśrameṇa api vivādasya tubhavādṛśa jihvā spanda mātra adhīnasya sūtra gotra ādau= api suśaka tvāt 
NP_3.2.46^3	 itas pūrvam tāvat na asti iti ced na asya api vivādasya anādi tvā yogāt tatas pūrvam abhāvātaḥ tathā ca bhavataḥ bhaviṣyataḥ vā vivādasya vivāda tva aviśeṣāt tatas param teṣām anāśvāsa prasaṅgāt asmākam tāvat teṣu saṃśayaḥ na asti iti ced asmākam vā kim asti amīṣu  kva tarhi nikṛṣṭa jāti antaram  kim asmāsu tat nyāsīkṛtam  yena asmābhiḥ pradarśanīyam na ca asmābhiḥ anantāḥ deśāḥ draṣṭum śākyāḥ sambhavati ca ucchedaḥ idānīm kṣatriya vaiśya māhiṣya ādi vat teṣām keṣām cit nāma sāmya mātrāt atra anupraveśaḥ saṃbhavati iti ced na kasyāḥ api śaṅkāyāḥ sarvatra sulabha tvāt asti ca varṇitu abhikṣu tvā ādīnām sāmyam anyatra api yaḥ ca evam atiśaṅkayā dūyate sa tu sva mātā pitṛ carita an avadhāraṇena sva brāhmaṇyam api yathārham atiśaṅketa iti jitam lokāyatena uktam ca bhagavatā ajñaḥ ca aśraddhadhānaḥ ca saṃśaya ātmā vinaśyati 
NP_3.2.46^4	 na ayam lokosti na paraḥ na sukha saṃśaya ātmanaḥ iti tat siddham viśiṣṭa ādhikārikam veda aviruddham vaikhānasa ādi smaraṇam pramāṇam iti yat ca dharma śāstra ādiṣu aṣṭādaśa ādi parisaṃkhyānam na tad adhika saṃkhyā vyavaccheda param anyeṣām api śiṣṭa parigraha ādeḥ aviśiṣṭa tvāt anukta aṃśa darśana ādinā upajīvya tvāt ca iti evam sa parikaraḥ vedaḥ pramāṇam iti siddham chandaḥ pādau śabda śāstram na vaktram kalpaḥ pāṇī jyautiṣam cakṣuṣī ca śikṣā ghrāṇam śrotram uktam niruktam vedasya aṅgāni āhuḥ etāni ṣaṣ ca evam sa parikara veda artha tattva nirṇaya viṣayāḥ atha atas dharma jijñāsā iti ārabhya anāvṛttiḥ śabdāt anāvṛttiḥ śabdāt iti evam antā viṃśati lakṣaṇī mīmāṃsā tatra ca saṃhitam etat śarīrakam jaiminīyena ṣoḍaśa lakṣaṇena iti śāstra ekatva siddhiḥ iti bhāṣya upāttaḥ vṛtti granthaḥ 
NP_3.2.47^1	 tattva ratna ākare tu evam uktam karma devatā brahma gocarā sā tridhā udbhabhau sūtrakārataḥ jaimineḥ muneḥ kāśa kṛt snataḥ bādārayaṇāt ityataḥ kramāt iti anayoḥ devatā kāṇḍasya jaiminīya tvakāśa kṛt snīyatva uktī tādadhīni ādi vivakṣaya samāna arthe gamayitavye tatra karma kāṇḍa artham evam saṃjagṛhuḥ dharma dhīḥ mānabheda aṅga prayukti krama kartṛbhiḥ sa ati deśa viśeṣaḥ ha bādha tantra prasaktibhiḥ iti veda arthe nyāya cintye prathamam avasitam karma tat devatā ca atha atas śārīraka aṃśe niravadhika phala brahma cintā tu asūtri 
NP_3.2.47^2	 tatra adhyāye parasmin svayam upaniṣadām anvayosya avirodhaḥ mokṣa upāyotha muktiḥ viṣaya viṣayiṇau siddha sādhyau dvikā arthau tatra adya iti anta gūḍhā viśada viśada ta= chāyajīva ādi vācaḥ paścāt smṛti ādikaiḥ akṣati rahita hatiḥ kārya tā abhra indriya ādeḥ doṣa adoṣau tṛtīyepya vara para gatau bhaktiḥ aṅgāni ca atha upāsa anuṣṭhā prabhāva utkrama saraṇi phalāni antime cintitāni vicārāt pūrvam eva atra prāptam adhyayanam vidheḥ atas nadhīta vedasya vicāraḥ śāstra bādhitaḥ kramaḥ viṃśati lakṣaṇyāḥ na vā edhaḥ kintu yauktikaḥ atas vyutkrama cintāyām anaucityam praśiṣyate 
NP_3.2.48^1	 evam viṃśati lakṣaṇī śravaṇa mananābhyām su pratiṣṭhita samasta śāstra arthasya mokṣa sādhana tayā vidheyam nididhi āsanam na vākya artha jñāna mātram tasya rāga prāpta śravaṇa ādi siddha tvāt atas eva ca tasmin viśeṣe vedanā ādi sāmānya śabda paryavasānam na ca nididhi āsana ādikam niṣiddham varaṇīya tvam eva vihitam iti vācyam svatantra anya kartṛka varaṇa karmībhāvasya āpuruṣa tantretu enā vidheya tvāt atas tat hetunā prīti rūpa tvena upāsanam eva viśiṣyate tathā sati bhaktyā tu ananyayā iti smṛti avirodhaḥ ca tat eva ca nididhi āsanam prīti rūpam prakaraṇa viśeṣāt samādhiḥ 
NP_3.2.48^2	 ca ca aṣṭa aṅgaḥ śāstreṣu śiṣyate tāvati ca pātañjala prāmāṇyam api āgama śīlanam ca āphalāt mātrayā anuvartanīyam smaranti ca svādhyāyāt yogam āsīta yogāt svādhyāyam āviśet svādhyāya yoga saṃpattyā paramātmā prakāśate iti yat punar śrūyate grantham abhyasya medhāvī jñāna vijñāna tatparaḥ palālam ima dhānya arthī tyajet grantham aśeṣatas iti tat kośa tyāga abhiprāyam na ca sa ādara paṭu saṃskāra pracaya saṃsiddha medhā saṃpadaḥ puruṣasya kośena kiñcid sāddhyam medhāvī iti ca viśeṣvate 
NP_3.2.48^3	 dhīḥ dhāraṇāvatī medhāḥ iti ca naighaṇṭukāḥ adhīmahe ca medhā manīṣe mā viśatām samīcīna bhūtasya bhavyasya avaruddhyai iti yaddhā mukta prāya atyanta niṣpanna yoga puruṣa viṣayam etat na hi tasya śāstreṇa jñātavyam tadānīm asti sākṣātkṛta samasta tattva artha tvāt yat tu smaryate śāstra jñānam bahu kleśam buddheḥ calana kāraṇam upadeśāt harim buddhvā viramet sarva karmasu iti idam tu tīvra saṃvegināmalasāstikānām ca grāhmam buddhi calana hetūnām asat śāstrāṇām tyāga artham vā tadā viśeṣaṇa sāphalyam dharma vidyā sthāneṣu api hi bahis daleṣu ati saṃrambhaḥ mumukṣoḥ apa udyate na śabda śāstra abhiratasya mokṣaḥ na ca eva ramya āvasatha priyasya 
NP_3.2.48^4	 na bhojana ācchādana tatparasya na loka citta grahaṇe ratasya iti tat śābdam prameya tattvam adhijigamiṣatām pramāṇeṣu sāram tad abhāve puṃsaḥ paśubhiḥ samatva prasaṅgāt iti yasya ājñā nigama eka harmī a valabhī vāstavya pārāvatī yat bhrū lāsi avaśaṃvadā vidhi śiva sva sthāna su sthāsikā yaḥ sarvatra yathāpuram vitanute nāmāni viśva ākṛtiḥ nityam naḥ pratibhātu sarva vacasām niṣṭhā sa nārāyaṇaḥ 
NP_4.1.1^1	 atha smṛtiḥ nirūpyate saṃskāra mātra jam jñānam smṛtiḥ iti tad lakṣaṇam nanu smṛtiḥ na pramāṇam avidyamāna viṣaya tvāt ananubhūti tvāt bhrama sambhava ucca iti ced na smṛti mātrā prāmāṇyasya prathama ahnikre pratikṣipta tvāt avādhita bāhya artha darśanāt atīta anāgata viṣaya anumāna ādi bādha prasaṅgāt sarva loka virodhāt ananubhūte artha antarepi smṛti prasaṅgāt smṛteḥ api sva prakāśa tvepi vedya ākāre saṃskāra ādi sāpekṣa tvāt na ca pūrva anubhava puraskāreṇa eva grahaṇāt aprāmāṇyam iti ced na smṛti pramoṣe tad abhāvāt pramāṇa tayā saṃmatāyām pratyabhijñāyām bhāvāt ca 
NP_4.1.1^2	 paratantra tvāt apramāṇyam iti ced na sva hetu pāratantrya mātrasya sārvatrika tvāt anubhava mūla tvasya pramāṇa mūla tvasya ca sa vikalpaka ādibhiḥ anaikāntika tvāt saṃskāra mātra janya tvasya asādhāraṇa tvāt sva viṣaya prakāśa vyavahārayoḥ tu smṛteḥ api svatantra tvāt icchā ādi vat viṣaya niyamepi pāratantryam asti iti ced na tadvat eva ajñāna tva prasaṅgāt jñānam eva hi svatas viṣaya pravaṇam icchasi atas eva hi nityayoḥ api riśvara cikīrṣā prayatnayoḥ viṣaya niyamāya jñāna apekṣām brūṣe icchā ādīnām api svatas viṣaya prāvaṇyam jñāna tvam ca asmābhiḥ svīkṛtam nanu saṃskāra vat iti ced na tasya api sva hetu samāna viṣaya jñāna utpādana śakta svabhāva tvāt atas hetu niyata viṣaya tvam eva phalitam tat ca anubhavepi samam tathā ca samāna viṣaya anubhava janya tva tad abhāvābhyām smṛti anubhavayoḥ pāratantrya svātantrya vyavahāraḥ mandānām 
NP_4.1.1^3	 sva prāmāṇya nirṇaya ādau= api na anubhava apekṣa tva nirbandhaḥ sva viṣaya prakāśana bādha viraha ādibhi satad siddheḥ gṛhīta mātra grāhi tvasya asādhāraṇa tvāt prābhākarāṇām anumāna ādau naiyāyika ādīnām dhārāvāhika ādau yoga siddha sarvajña vādinām dvitīya yoga pratyakṣa ādau keṣāñcid īśvara vādinām anitya īśvara jñāne ca vyabhicārāt ca niṣprayojana tvāt aprāmāṇyam iti ced na tṛṇa ādi viṣaya pratna yakṣa ādinā naikāntyāt asiddheḥ ca smṛtyā eva hi jagatām kṛta akṛta pratyavekṣaṇa ādi siddhiḥ smṛtyā eva hi śabda anumānayoḥ pravṛtiḥ para bhakti ādi niṣpattiḥ ca pūrva anubhuvasya eva tāni prayojana āni iti ced sarva jagat ādi kāraṇasya brahma saṃkalpasya eva kim na syuḥ  evam ca anubhavasya api na tad siddhiḥ tad kāraṇasya iti vaktum śakya tvāt 
NP_4.1.1^4	 yat uktam prajñā paritrāṇe jñāta ātma jñāna rūpa tvāt sva prameya prahāṇataḥ viṣaya avyabhicāri tvepya prāmāṇyam smṛteḥ matam ityādi tat api anena parihṛtam pramāṇa vyavahāra abhāvāt aprāmāṇyam iti ced na pāmara vyavadvāra abhāvasya anaikāntika tvāt evam parīkṣaka vyavahāra bhāvasya api vigīta tvāt ca sarva parīkṣaka vyavahāra abhāvasya ca asiddheḥ māna manohara ādau vāc īśvara ādibhiḥ ta prāmāṇi asya ukta tvāt katipaya parīkṣa kavyahāra abhāvasya ca atiprasañjaka tvāt akṣapāda ādi vyahāra avi avahārayoḥ bṛhaspati ādi vyavahāra vat asmābhiḥ na atīva ādaraṇāt indra pāṇini ādīnām tu sarva saṃpratipatteḥ abādhāt ca ādarāt pārāśarya ādīnām pramāṇa parigaṇana anadhikṛta tvena tad anuktera prayojaka tvāt āgamaḥ pramāṇam iti api vyavahāra abhāvāt 
NP_4.1.1^5	 pratyakṣam ca anumānam ca śāstram ca vividha āgamam ityādiṣu ca pratyakṣa ādi mūla smṛteḥ pratyakṣa ādi samāna carca tvena pṛthak vyavahāra abhāva upapatteḥ pramāṇa hetukā smṛtiḥ pramāṇam eva avisaṃvādāt iti uktam ca nyāya tattve smṛti udāsīna bhedake caturthedhi karaṇe apramāṇa mūla tvam tu ubhayoḥ api na asti vyabhicāra abhāvena anadhigata artham pramāṇam iti viśeṣaṇasya ayukta tvāt pramite pramiti anupapattiḥ kva dṛṣṭā  smṛtau ced pratijñā eva dṛṣṭāntaḥ syāt jñāna antare ced na nujānāmi ityādi tattva ratna ākare ca yathārtha niścayaḥ mānam tat hetuḥ ca iti sūrayaḥ na ativyāptiḥ smṛtau vyāptiḥ yathārthena hi sā pramā 
NP_4.1.1^6	 iti uktvā asya uttara ardha vivaraṇa īpi uktam anubhūta viṣaya asaṃpramoṣaḥ smṛtiḥ yathā sa ghaṭa ati nanu tām api vyāpnoti lakṣaṇamya satyam tad vyāptau na ati vyāptiḥ tasya api lakṣya pakṣe nikṣepāt lakṣya alakṣye anālakṣya kṣipyate lakṣaṇam katham loka dhī vī avahāram hi lakṣya alakṣya avadhi viduḥ ityādi yat tu anubhavaḥ pramāṇam smṛti vyatiriktam jñānam anubhavaḥ ityādinā smṛteḥ aprāmāṇyam uktam iva śrī viṣṇu cittaiḥ tat nūnam para ma tā anvāroheṇa atas eva hi taiḥ svatas prāmāṇya nirṇaya daśāyām anyathā vyavahṛtam tathā hi tasmāt siddham etat pramāṇānām yathārtha tva lakṣaṇam prāmāṇyam guṇa jñāna anapekṣāt sva pramāṇāt eva avasīyate svakīyāt kāraṇāt eva jñāyate iti ca iti 
NP_4.1.1^7	 tathā artha tathā tvam guṇa saṃvāda jñāna anapekṣa jñapti tad abhāvepi jñāyamāna tvāt ityādau na ca hetoḥ asiddha tvam tathā hi rajata jñānasya artha tathā tvam nāma rajata viṣaya tvam tat ca asati bādhake rajata grāhiṇā eva jñānena avagamyate ityādi atas yathā avasthita vastu niścaya ātmaka tvam eva prāmāṇyam pramāṇa jñānānām ātmīyāt kāraṇāt jñāyate na guṇa saṃvāda jñānam apekṣate iti tathā pramāṇānām yathā avasthita vastu niścaya ātmaka tvam eva prāmāṇyam tad ābhāsa yuktayaḥ pūrva pakṣiṇa ucyante siddhāntepi viveka pradarśanam eva iti yadi ca anubhavaḥ eva pramāṇam tat na yuktam upayuktam vā 
NP_4.1.1^8	 na ca sarvam anubhavam pramāṇa tayā vyavaharanti pīta śaṅkha bhrama ādiṣu adarśanāt na api sarvām smṛtim apramāṇa tayā pramāṇa mūla smṛtiṣu tad abhāvāt agṛhīta grahaṇa śaktam pramāṇam iti vara da viṣṇu miśroktiḥ api para ma tā anvāroheṇa netavyāḥ yat tu āgama prāmāṇye proktam pramāṇa antara dṛṣṭa artha viṣaya vyāpiśemuṣī pramāṇam eva tat pūrvam na ced sva artham vigāhate iti idam api anuvāda vākyasya anya para tayā sva artha prāmāṇya vyavaccheda artham anyathā smṛti pramoṣe pramuṣita tad aṃśe pūrva anubhava puraskāreṇa sva artha avagāhana asiddheḥ katham tatra smṛti tva nibandhanam aprāmāṇyam bhaviṣyati  
NP_4.1.2^1	 yat tu bhāṣye sat mātra grāhi pratyakṣa nirākaraṇa daśāyām uktam aśve hastini ca saṃvedanayoḥ eka viṣaya tvena uparitanasya gṛhīta grāhi tvāt viśeṣa abhāvāt ca smṛti vailakṣaṇyam na syāt iti na tatra smṛteḥ aprāmāṇyam sūcitam prakāra antareṇa api vailakṣaṇya siddheḥ tad apekṣayā ca prasaṅga upapatteḥ yat ca aparam bhāṣyam indriya janmanaḥ pratyakṣasya hi eṣa svabhāva niyamaḥ yat sva sama kāla vartinaḥ padārthasya grāhaka tvam na tu sarveṣām jñānānām pramāṇānām ca smaraṇa anumāna āgama yogi pratyakṣa ādiṣu kāla antara vartinā upi grahaṇa darśanāt ityādi tatra api parasya aniṣṭa prasaṅgāya tad abhiprāya anudhāvanena vibhajya udāharaṇam yuktam 
NP_4.1.2^2	 yat ca śāstra yoni adhikaraṇe bhāṣitam bhāvanā prakarṣa paryanta janmanaḥ tasya viśada avabhāsa tvepi pūrva anubhūta viṣaya smṛti mātra tvāt na prāmāṇyam iti kutas pratyakṣatā iti idam api na sākṣāt siddhānta stham na ca yāthārthyam tatra pratikṣiptam evam anyat api bhāvyam smṛtyaprāmāṇya vādinā upi vaiśeṣikāḥ tām yathā arthyāt vidyā koṭau paṭhanti tatas eva ca tad eka deśibhiḥ api tat prāmāṇyam svīkṛtam iti 
NP_4.2.3^1	 evam tāvat vivecitam pramāṇam cārvākāḥ tu pratyakṣam ekam pramāṇam iti āhuḥ teṣu eva kecid anumānasya pratyakṣentarbhāvam icchanti kecid tu aprāmāṇyam pratyakṣam anumānam ca kāṇādāḥ saugatāḥ ca tatra pūrve śabdasya anumāna intarbhāvam āhuḥ pare tu kecid antarbhāvam kecid aprāmāṇyam te ca āgamam ca sāṃkhyāḥ bhūṣaṇa mata anuvartinaḥ ca tatra vedasya anādi tvam pūrve parijagṛhuḥ uttare tu īśvara sṛṣṭa tām tāni ca smṛtim ca vaiśeṣika eka deśina usmad siddhānta eka deśinaḥ ca tāni eva sārtha āpattikāni prābhākarāḥ anupalabdhi ṣaṣṭhāni tāni eva tautātitāḥ tad pralobhana rucayaḥ māyā vādinaḥ ca tāni eva saṃbhavati hi a yuktāni purāṇa śaraṇāḥ adyatana pramāṇa parigraha upalambha prakriyā iyam anante pūrva apara kāle kaḥ kim aṅgīkuryāt kim vā bahiṣkuryāt iti kaḥ jānāti anyatra kalpa sākṣāt kāriṇaḥ tasmāt ekasmāt devāt iha ca nyūna vādinaḥ tad avasare nirastāḥ 
NP_4.2.3^2	 adhika tayā para abhimatānām tu arnta bhāvaḥ vaktavyaḥ tatra yathā pratyabhijñā ādīnām pratyakṣa ādiṣu eva niveśaḥ iṣyate evam anyeṣām api pratyabhijñā tāvat grahaṇa ātmikā eva iti eke tathā hi pratyabhijñāyām api smṛtiḥ anubhavaḥ iti aṃśa bheda usti ced iti āśaṅkya pratyuktam śrī viṣṇu cittaiḥ yadi viṣaya bhedaḥ tadā aṃśa bhedaḥ saṃbhavet aikyam eva hi niraṃśam pratyabhijñā pratyakṣa viṣayaḥ katham saṃskāraḥaparokṣadhī janakaḥ iti ced na cakṣuḥ ādi indriya sahakṛtasya saṃskārasya jñātuḥ aikyāt tat idam iti aparokṣadhī hetutva upapatteḥ aparokṣa artha aikya sādhikāḥ sā pratyabhijñā soyam vai pumān iti evam ātmikāḥ saṃskāra mātra janya tvāt na smṛtiḥ mānam eva tat iti dīpe ca aanusmṛteḥ ca a iti sūtre bhāṣitam pratyabhijñānāt ca na paṭa ādeḥ kṣaṇika tvam tat eva idam iti pratyabhijñāyate pratyabhijñā hi nāma atīta vartamāna kāla varti eka vastu viṣayam ekam pratyakṣa jñānam 
NP_4.2.3^3	 tasya kāla dvaya sambandha aviśiṣṭam ekam eva vastu viṣayaḥ na ca tat iti aṃśaḥ smaraṇam idam aṃśaḥ ca grahaṇam atīta sambandhini indriya saṃprayoga abhāvāt iti vācyam tat idam iti sāmānādhikaraṇyena grahaṇasya ekatva sphuraṇāt pūrva anubhava janita saṃskāra saciva indriya saṃprayoga yuktasya puruṣasya tathā grahaṇam upapadyate eva anvaya vyatireka adhīnam hi sarvatra sāmagrī parikalpanam iti anye tu atra dhī bheda bāddhya parihārau matvā tat idam aṃśayoḥ tad aṃśe saṃskāra anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāna darśanāt parokṣa rūpa tayā idam aṃśe ca pati akṣa rūpa tayā ca ubhaya ātmaka tvam āhuḥ tad mate saṃskāra adhīna prakāśā smṛtiḥ iti lakṣaṇam aparokṣa jñānam pratyakṣam ubhaya lakṣaṇa yogāt pratyabhijñāyām ubhaya ātmaka tvam iti abhyupagantavyam ca asmad siddhāntibhiḥ sarvaiḥ pratyakṣa itara jñānānām parokṣa aparokṣa rūpa tvam svayaṃprakāśa tvāt sarva jñānānām vedya itara aṃśa apekṣayā ca pratyakṣa tvāt 
NP_4.2.3^4	 uktam ca idam śrī viṣṇu cittaiḥ api sva prakāśakam viṣaya prakāśakam ca ekam eva jñānam tatra smṛtriḥ anubhūtiḥ iti kutas bhedaḥ iti paricodya prakāśa māna bhedāt iti brūmaḥ yathā gauḥ ayam iti ekasmin= eva jñāne prakāri prakāra viṣaya bhedena jñāna aṃśa bhedaḥ yathā gauḥ ayam iti ekasmin= eva jñāne prakāri prakāra viṣaya bhedena jñāna aṃśa bhedaḥ yathā ca ghaṭa paṭau= iti ekasmin= eva jñāneṃśa bhedaḥ yathā vā para abhyupagata bhrama jñāneṣu adhiṣṭhāna aṃśe prāmāṇyam itaratra aprāmāṇyam ca iti parihārāt tathā smṛteḥ sva prakāśa aṃśa upi saṃskāra mātrajaḥ eva indriya ādi pratiniyata kāraṇa antara abhāvāt iti paricodya na evam jñānānām prakāśamāna tvasya svābhāvika tvāt iti parihārāt ca tasmāt sarvatra viṣaya apekṣayā eva aparokṣatva anumiti tva smṛti tva ādi vibhāgaḥ jāti saṃkara asaṃkara ādi tu darśana adarśanābhyām vyavasthāpyam aupādhika saṃkara ādi vat ca tat evam ubhaya ātmaka tva upapatteḥ pratyabhijñā api ubhaya ātmikāḥ iti 
NP_4.2.4	 pratyabhijñā api abhijñāvat tridhā ca akṣa ādi bhedataḥ tad tad saṃskāra saṃbheda mūla tva anna vadhā bhavet pratyakṣa toktiḥ dīpa ādau pradarśana pareṣya tām na hi liṅga ādibhiḥ soyam iti jñānam na jāyate śabda jam pratyabhijñānam upajīvya pravartate śākhā antara adhikaraṇa nyāyaḥ ca kratu vidyayoḥ dīpa ādiṣu iva sarvatra bādhaka ādeḥ asaṃbhavāt vigītam pratyabhijñānam pramāṇam sa vikalpa vat karaṇa akaraṇa ādīnām kāla bheda ādi upādhitaḥ avirodhāt na bīja ādau śakyate bheda kalpanam anyathā deśa bhedena karaṇa akaraṇa ādibhiḥ ekam jagati na eva syāt iti syāt sarva śūnyatā tasmāt viruddha saṃspṛṣṭa viṣaya pratyabhijñayā sthira tvam ātmanām siddham bāhyānām api vāstavam 
NP_4.2.5^1	 pratisandhānam api ātma gocaram pratyabhijñā viśeṣaḥ eva yoham adrākṣam saḥ eva spṛśāmi iti evamādi rūpa tvāt pratisandhiḥ artha dvaya viṣaya ekabuddhiḥ iti eke tatra api pṛthak anubhūta aneka artha gocara eka kartṛka ekabuddhiḥ iti pūraṇīyam iti saṃvādaḥ nāma jñāna jāti antaram iti kecid tat ayuktam saṃkhyā antara asaṃbhavāt yat tu vara da viṣṇu miśraiḥ uktam gṛhīta artha viṣayam śabda kāraṇakam jñānam saṃvādaḥ iti tat api śābda avāntara bhede saṃjñā viśeṣa niveśa mātra param na hi gṛhīta artha viṣaya tve śabda śakti prasūta tvam apaiti gṛhīta mātra gocara pramāṇa antarepi tad anyatva prasaṅgāt bhavati hi parva toyam agni mān iti śabda śravaṇa anantaram dhūmam parāmṛśatopi tādṛśī buddhiḥ 
NP_4.2.5^2	 tathā dvitīya yogi pratyakṣa ādau= api draṣṭavyam anapekṣita tva ādikam api śruta viṣaya anumāna ādau samam na ca apekṣā yuktam prāmāṇyam bhedaḥ bhedaḥ vā tṛṇa ādi pratyakṣasya api tathā prasaṅgāt iti uktam kimartham tarhi vedānām vedāntānām ca aprāpta viṣaya tvam samarthyate iti ced atathā prāptau sākṣāt aprāmāṇya prasaṅgāt tathā prāptau= api anapekṣita tayā prekṣāvadbhiḥ nirarthaka prayāsa bhīrubhiḥ tyājya tva āpātena phalatā uprāmāṇya prasaṅgāt iti paśya 
NP_4.2.6^1	 upamānam api yadi gṛhyamāṇa padārtha gata sādṛśya vijñānāt smaryamāṇa padārtha gata sādṛśya vijñānam tadā smṛtiḥ tad tad vastu saṃsthāna viśeṣa ādi atiriktasya sādṛśyasya abhāvāt tasya ca pūrva dṛṣṭa tvāt smaryamāṇa tvāt ca vyavahāropyaḥ tu apūrvaḥ tad tad vyavahāra vat pratisambandha viśeṣa parāmarśa upādhikaḥ yat vā yaḥ yat sadṛśaḥ sa tad gata sādṛśya pratiyogī yathā mithas sva hastau iti vyāpti siddhau gauḥ etat sadṛśaḥ etad gata sādṛśya pratiyogi tvāt iti anumānāt smaryamāṇa gata sādṛśya asiddhiḥ anyathā gṛhyamāṇa gata vaisādṛśya jñānāt smaryamāṇa gata vaisādṛśya pratītiḥ api māna antaram syāt 
NP_4.2.6^2	 sā ced arthāpattiḥ sādṛśya dhīḥ api tathā kim na syāt iti athavā yugapad eva tad sadṛśoyam iti pratyayena eva ubhaya vṛtti sādṛśya sphuraṇāt na tad hetukam anyathā pṛthak anubhūtayoḥ tadānīma pratīta sādṛśyayoḥ parastāt yugapad smaryamāṇayoḥ yugapad eva pratīya māna sa adṛyayoḥkaḥ nirvāhaḥ  tatra api vā pramāṇa antaram kalpyate  yathā gauḥ tathā gavayaḥ go vat dviśaphaḥ na bhavati aśvaḥ dīrghagrīvaḥ pralamba uṣṭhaḥ vikaṭa ākṛtiḥ paśuḥ kramelakaḥ iti tu sādharmya vaidharmya dharmya mātra viṣayam 
NP_4.2.6^3	 trividham api atideśa vākyam āgamaḥ eva yat tu śruta atideśa vākyasyagavaya ādau= ati deśa vākya artha pratyabhijñānam upamānam tat ca vyutpatti phalakam iti tat api anupapananam prāk eva vyutpatti siddheḥ yat tu sādṛśyasya nimittattvāt nimittasya apratītitaḥ samayaḥ durgrahaḥ pūrvam śabdena anumayā api vā iti tatra nimittasya apratītitaḥ iti tu asiddham gavayatva ādeḥ eva jāti viśeṣasya go sādṛśya ākāra upalakṣitasya prathamam eva vākya artha tayā pratītiḥ go sādṛśya ākāra upalakṣitasya prathamam eva vākya artha tayā pratītiḥ go sādṛśya upalakṣitaḥ kaścid vyakti viśeṣaḥ gavayaḥ iti hi pratītiḥ paścāt pratyakṣita gavayasya tat vaiśadya mātram eva uktam ca śrī viṣṇu citteḥ go sadṛśaḥ gavayaḥ iti gosādṛśya eka adhikaraṇam sāmānyam vācyam iti vyutpannam prathamam vākya artha tayā pratīteḥ go sādṛśya upalakṣitasya anirṇaye paścāt api anirṇayaḥ anyathā nirṇaye tathā paścāt api tatas vākya śravaṇa velāyām eva nirṇitam iti evam ca anabhyupagame katham inrdā ādi śabda vyutpattiḥ  na hi atra nimitta bhūta saṃsthāna viśeṣa ādi dṛṣṭiḥ 
NP_4.2.6^4	 na ca nityam tatra avyutpattiḥ tad artha viśiṣṭa vākya artha bodha āpātāt evam nitya atīndriya viṣaya saṃskāra ādi śabdānām api nityam avyutpattiḥ eva syāt tatra ced kathañcid nirvāhaḥ tathā atra api tat siddham na upamānam atiriktam iti arthāpattiḥ tu anumānam eva tathā hi anupapadyamānadarśanāt upapādaka kalpanam nāma vyāpyāt vyāpaka jñānam avyāpyasya tena vinā anupapadyamāna tva abhāvāt avyāpakasya ca tad upapādaka tva ayogāt iti pramāṇa dvaya virodhe sati viṣaya vyavasthāpanam arthāpattiḥ iti api na vācyam pramāṇayoḥ satoḥ virodha abhāvāt viruddhayoḥ api prāmāṇya ayogāt 
NP_4.2.6^5	 nanu devadattasya jīvane kutaścid pramāṇāt pramite jīvatā kvacid sthātavyam iti aviśeṣeṇa deśa sāmānya sambandha avagatau gṛham api āskandantyām satyām pratyakṣe ca gṛhe tad abhāvam pratipādayati spaṣṭaḥ virodhaḥ atas tat śānyai bahis bhāva kalpanam arthāpattiḥ iti mā evam kvacid iti viditasya jīvanasya niyama abhāvāt bahis vidyam āna tā saṃdehe niścaya rūpeṇa gṛha abhāva pratyakṣeṇa pratispardhi tum asāmarthyāt na ca viruddha viṣayayoḥ vāstavam kutra api sama bala tvam samasti ubhayā prāmāṇye tu kathañcid syāt 
NP_4.2.6^6	 ābhimānika bala sāmya īpi tathā eva yadā vaiṣamya grahaḥ tadā tatas eva bala abala siddhau kim artha āpattyā sādhyam  atas kevala niravakāśa virodhi viśeṣa sannidhau sati sa avakāśam sāmānyam saṃkocayitavyam iti vyavasthā syāt sā api ca tathā eva vyāpteḥ iti anumāna phalam eva anyathā virodhi viṣaya tyāgaḥ iva avirodhi viśeṣa paryavasāna ādau= api māna antara kptiḥ kim na syāt  evam anabhyupagame ca dhūma anumāna ādau= api arthāpatti tva prasaṅgaḥ agnim vinā anupapadyamāna tva svaya liṅga pratyakṣa rūpa pramāṇa dvaya virodhasya ca vaktum śakya tvāt dhūmaḥ hi kāraṇa bhūtam vahnim ākṣipati pratikṣipati tu pratyakṣam iti virodhe parvatārvāc bhāge vahniḥ iti vyavasthā kalpanasya arthāpatti tvam syāt vyāpti nirūpaṇam antareṇa gamakatā gamakasya eva dharma antara yogi tayā gamyate ityādi bhedāḥ tu āśā mātra kalpitāḥ iti uktam ca śrī viṣṇut tittaiḥ arthāpattiḥ anumānam ityādi kecid tu kevala vyatirekiṇi arthāpatti saṃjñām niveśayanti tasya prāk eva nirāsāt na pramāṇa varga anupraveśaḥ anupraveśepi vā na pṛthaktvam 
NP_4.2.7^1	 yat tu āgama prāmāṇye anubhavaḥ ca indriya liṅga śabda sadṛśāni atha anupapadyamāna artha pūrvakaḥ ityādiṣu upamāna artha āpatti parigrahaḥ pratibhāti tat api pūrva pakṣa pradeśa gata tvāt na siddhānta tvāya kalpate abhāvaḥ tu asmad mate bhāva antarātmā sa ca akṣa ādibhiḥ yathāsaṃbhavam sidhyati abhāva ātmanā tu grahaṇepi pratiyogi smaraṇa ādi sahakāri sahitāni tāni eva pramāṇani iti na tad atirikta kalpanā avakāśaḥ atas eva hi prāgarta ja abhāva ādi vijñānam api nirvyūḍham dṛṣṭaḥ eva hi deśa kāla ādi saṃsarga ādi viśeṣaḥ paścāt pratiyogi smaraṇa ādimataḥ puruṣasya tad abhāva ātmanā dhiyam adhirohati smartavyasya smaraṇa abhāvāt vā tatra tad abhāva anumānam
