NP_4.2.7^2	 evam atirikta abhāva pakṣepi nirmūlā pramāṇa antara kptiḥ sa ghaṭam bhū talam iti vat aghaṭam bhū talam iti api hi aparokṣā pratītiḥ na ca adhikaraṇa grahaṇa upakṣīṇam indriyam guṇa ādiṣu api prasaṅgāt atireka vat anatiḥ ekepī ajñāta karaṇa tva ādīni anumānāni ca sulabhāni iti saṃbhava upyanumānam eva sahasre śatam saṃbhavati iti ādeḥ pūrva anubhū sahasra gata vyāpti bodhana tvāt saṃbhavati kṣatriye śairyam iti ādeḥ saṃdeha ātmaka tvena apramāṇa tvāt avirodha niścaya rūpa tvepi tad avirodha niścāyaka pramāṇa antare viśramaḥ aitihyam tu pramāṇa mūlam ced āgamaḥ tad ābhāsa mūlam ced tad ābhāsaḥ evam ceṣṭā ālipi akṣara ādikam api abhiprāya varṇa viśeṣa ādi avinābhūtam anumānam eva 
NP_4.2.7^3	 ceṣṭāyām vara da nārāyaṇa bhaṭṭārakaiḥ evam uktam śabdasya vyavahārasya anukāraḥ ceṣṭayā api hi kriyate śābda vijñāna yoginām sva artha bodhikāḥ anādi vyavahāreṣu ceṣṭāḥ vijñāta śaktikāḥ bodhikāḥ syuḥ yathā adhyakṣam iti ced bhavataḥ matam ceṣṭāḥ giraḥ vā svīkāryāḥ para pratyāyanāya hi anādayaḥ girām eva anāditā jyāyasī tadā ceṣṭā sāmayikī śābda vyavahāra anusāriṇī asya evam bodhikā iti evam bharata ādi āgame sthitā dṛśyatena ādiḥ āmnāyosmaryamāṇa praṇetṛkaḥ ityādi tattva ratna ākare tu evam uktam vyutpanna bodhya bodhaka niyamam ced ceṣṭitam śābdam aniyatam api saha dṛṣṭyā smārakam iti na pṛthak eṣṭavyam iti lipi akṣareṣu tu ayam gakāraḥ ayam ghakāraḥ iti varṇa ātmanā jñānam apramāṇam eva 
NP_4.2.7^4	 etena cihnena idam akṣaram jānīhi iti abhiprāyeṇa lipi akṣara saṃbandha grāhakāṇām pravṛttiḥ tatas ca vyāpti siddhiḥ eṣā lipiḥ etad varṇa viśeṣa abhiprāya pūrvikā bhrama ādi rahita varṇa abhiprāya vat puruṣa likhita etat lipi tvāt saṃpratipanna vyutpatti kāla lipivat ityādi rūpaḥ prayogaḥ draṣṭavyaḥ yat tu pratibhāyām uktam tattva ratna ākare nanu ca pratibhā kācid yathārthāḥ mānam iṣyatām bāhya artha naiḥ apekṣyeṇa bāhya jñāna kṣamāḥ tu sā viśiṣṭa kāla puruṣa ādi apekṣā utkarṣa saṃbhavāḥ satyam kāla ādi bhedaḥ tu durviveca usmad ādibhiḥ san= api asau vyavahṛtau na upayogī iti upekṣyate pratibhāyāḥ phalam dṛṣṭam yadā prāmāṇya niścayaḥ 
NP_4.2.7^5	 tad anyatas kṛtārtha tvāt prekṣyate na parīkṣakaiḥ puṇyeṣu puruṣeṣu eṣā bhūyiṣṭham satya darśinī tasmāt patañjaliḥ prāha pratibhā ca iti tām pramām iti tat api prāc ukta yogi pratyakṣa viśeṣa viṣayam eva nanu evam tat api pramāṇa tri tvam catuṣṭvam vā anupapannam pratyakṣa parokṣa rūpeṇa dvi tvasya eva yukta tvāt iti ced na atiprasaṅgāt tathā hi bahuṣu ekaikam uddhṛtya tad anyeṣu aika rāśyataḥ dvaidhakptau ghadādau= api evam eva prasajyate anumāna numāna tva śabdā śabda vibhāgataḥ pramāṇa dvi tvam evam te vada kim vāna rocate pratyakṣasya tad anyābhyām vaijātya grahaṇāt yadi tayoḥ api svetarābhyām vaijātyam sphuṭam eva naḥ 
NP_4.2.7^6	 atokṣaliṅga śabda ākhyāsā dhāraṇa nidānataḥ upalakṣyam pramātri tvam catuṣṭvam vā api saṃsmṛteḥ spaṣṭam aspaṣṭam iti ca jaināḥ yat dvaidham ūcire tad pratyakṣa parokṣa tva vibhāgāt na viśiṣyate atas na tāvati dvaidhe sādhite vivadāmahe parokṣasya eka māna tvam durvacam bheda sādhanāt nanu adhyakṣepi bheda usti bāhya antara vibhāgataḥ divya adivya tayā cakṣuḥ śrotra ādi bhidayā api ca tadvat parokṣasya ekasya pramāṇasya vibhāgataḥ anumāna āgama bhidā katham na abhyupagamyate datta uttaram idam kiñcid dṛṣṭam etat śrutam tu idam etat tu anumitam ca iti lokoktiḥ iha sākṣiṇī yatas kutaścid vaidharmyam sādharmyam api kenacid sarvatra sulabham kāmam iha api parigṛhyate 
NP_4.2.7^7	 atas smṛti anubhūti ākhyā vibhāgāt api na ucitam pramāṇa dvi tvam iti evam prāk uktā eva su paddhatiḥ trividha unubhavaḥ ca eva tad mūlā ca tathā smṛtiḥ iti ṣoḍhā vibhāge tu na vimanyāmahe vayam anubhūti vibhāgena tad mūlāyāḥ smṛteḥ api vibhāgasya gata artha tvāt aikarāśyam udāhṛtam atas hi tasyāḥ tad mūleṣu antarbhāva vivakṣayā pramāṇa vargam tri tvena prāñcaḥ kecid viviñcate evam anyat api cintyam iti nanu anena na kim pramāṇa cintā kleśena avimṛśya api pramāṇa vargam upalambha anvaya vyatireka ādi vaśāt paśu ādīnām iva manuṣya ādīnām api laukikeṣu artheṣu pravṛtti nivṛtti tad prayojana ādikam nirupadravam sidhyati 
NP_4.2.7^8	 alaukikeṣu api tad tad vidhāyakaiḥ tad anugrāhakaiḥ ca kalpa sūtra ādibhiḥ carita artha dhiyām kim anena piṣṭa peṣaṇa ādi kalpena vṛthā vimarśena iti ced mā evam avakāśa uparodhāya tattva upaplavam icchatām aviparyāsa siddhyai ca viśodhyā mānayat hatiḥ pratisaṃdhāya ca phanalam prārambha āhnika darśitam sādhya prameya saṃśuddhyai sa aṅge māne pariśramaḥ pratyakṣita samasta arthaiḥ yogi indra enar api laṅghyate pramāṇa plavam ālambya tattva viplava sāgaraḥ tasmāt ukta rītyā śuddhiḥ kartavyā iti śuddha anyāya niṣevitā śruti śiraḥ śuddhānta siddhāntinī bhadrāṇām pratipādanāya bhajatu pratyakṣa tām akṣatām patyau nitya rase samam karuṇayā pātivratīm bibhratī sarva granthivimocanī bhagavatī sā me samīcī kṛtiḥ 
NP_5.1.1^1	 evam sa parikaram pramāṇam viśodhitam atha prameyam pradarśayāmaḥ tatra yat punar ṣaṣ sapta ādi rūpeṇa padārthān vibhajya vaiśeṣika ādayaḥ cintayanti tat na sākṣāt apavarga aṅgam iti taiḥ eva abhyupetam api ca vidyamāna parityāgāt asatām ca parigrahāt vyāmohanāḥ vimarśāḥ te bahiṣkāryāḥ mumukṣubhiḥ sāvāntara vibhāgeṣu tat tad cintā āśrameṣu iha avistarāya diś mātram doṣāṇām abhidadhmahe yat tatra āhuḥ abhidheyaḥ padārthaḥ 
NP_5.1.1^2	 sa ca bhāva abhāva bhedena dvidhā iti tat tāvat asat vyapadeśāt na iti ced na dharma antareṇa vākya śeṣāt i ukteḥ śabda antarāt ca iti ārambhaṇa adhikaraṇa sūtreṇa abhāvasya para abhyupagata abhāva abhāvasya iva bhāva antara tva samarthanāt pratikṣiptam yat api ca dravya guṇa karma sāmānya viśeṣa samavāya rūpeṇa bhāva rūpāṇām padārthānām ṣoḍhā parisaṃkhyānam tat api vaiśeṣika adhikaraṇe samavāya abhyupagamāt ca sāmyāt anavasthiteḥ iti sūtrakāraiḥ eva samavāya ākhya padārtha antara dūśaṇena parāḥ tam abhāva tad adhikaraṇayoḥ viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāva saṃnidhi viśeṣa ādi śabda vācya saṃbandha antara anumānam api samavāya dūṣaṇa= chāyayā eva dūṣitam eva 
NP_5.1.1^3	 yaḥ ca anyonyam atyanta tulyeṣu mukta ātma ādiṣu mithas vyāvṛtta dhī jananāya dravya tva ādi hetunā viśeṣa ākhyaḥ padārthaḥ kalpyate sā upi tulya nyāyatayā sūtrakāraiḥ dūṣita prāyaḥ eva mahat dīrgha vat vā hva sva parimaṇḍalābhyām iti anupapanna paramāṇu dvi aṇuka ādi prakriyā nidarśanena anyeṣām api tad abhyupagatānāmunapapanna tvasya sūcita tvāt ca api ca anityeṣu dravyeṣu tāvat jāti guṇa pādibhiḥ eva vyāvṛtta dhīḥ sidhyati iti nityeṣu hi viśeṣaḥ nyaḥ kalpyate yathā āhuḥ nitya dravya vṛtta yontyāḥ viśeṣāḥ iti tathā api veda antibhiḥ diś saṃjñaka vibhu padārtha antara anabhyupagamāt ākāśasya ca kāryatva ādi śruteḥ prakṛti vikāra bhūta pṛthivī ādi aṃśa viśeṣa atirikta paramāṇu jāla pratikṣepāt tathāvidha paramāṇūnām ca avasthā pravāhasya anādi anta tvāt na tatra viśeṣa kptiḥ 
NP_5.1.1^4	 tatas kāla ātmānau pariśiṣyete tatra api cetanānām na kāla tattvam ātma tayā bhāti kṣaṇa lava ādi avasthā yogi tva parāktvā acetana tva ādibhiḥ eva tasmāt sveṣām svebhyaḥ ca tasya vyāvṛtta dhī saṃbhavāt anyathā anyena api kalpitena tad asaṃbhava prasaṅgāt atas ātma pariśeṣe tatra api jīveśvarayoḥ aṇu tva vibhu tva niyāmya tva niyantṛ tva ādheya tva ādhāra tva śeṣa tva śeṣi tva śarīra tva śarīr itvābhiḥ anekavidhaiḥ dharma bhedaiḥ vyāvṛtta dhī siddhau kim anyena viśeṣeṇa 
NP_5.1.1^5	 tat atyanta sāmyavatsu mukteṣu nityeṣu api hi tad sāmyasya eva saṃrakṣaṇāya dharmi grāhaka siddhāḥ yāvat ātma bhāvinaḥ te te viśeṣāḥ na parityaktāḥ na ca īśvara dvaitam yena īśvarāṇām mithas vyāvṛtta pratītyai viśeṣam kalpayiṣyāmaḥ ekasya eva sarva deśa kāleṣu ekātapatra tayā sarva śruti siddha tvāt asya eva ca sāmānya śabdaiḥ viśeṣa śabdaiḥ ca rūḍhitaḥ yogataḥ tad tad vasatu viśiṣṭa tva ādinā ca tad tad prakaraṇa anuguṇam śarīrake pratipādya tva sthāpanāt jīveṣu api baddhānām mithas bhedaḥ tad tad sukha duḥkha dhi icchā vaicitryeṇa vyaktaḥ 
NP_5.1.1^6	 baddha muktayoḥ ca kiñcijjña tva sarvajña tva ādibhiḥ muktānām nityānām ca viśuddheḥ ādimat tva anādimattvābhyām eva vibhakta dhī saṃbhavaḥ mukta daśāyām nityebhyaḥ kim vaiṣmyam iti ced kim tena  prāktanena tad tad ātma varti tayā pratyakṣitena guṇa ādi bhedena tad anya vyāvṛtta dhī siddheḥ siddhaiḥ api tad vyavahāre prāktana upādhi bhedaiḥ eva tad tad pramāṇa pramitaiḥ pratisaṃhitaiḥ sarva nirvāhāt etena muktānām mithas vibhakta buddhiḥ api nirvyūḍhāḥ na hi teṣām eka rūpaḥ prāktanaḥ saṃsāraḥ viṣama vipāka samaya anādya saṃkhyāta karma pravāha vaicitrya pratiniyata deśa kāla svarūpa sukha duḥkha tad kāraṇa ādi saṃtateḥ eva mithas vyāvartaka tvāt 
NP_5.1.1^7	 tad atad vibhāgaḥ hi tad kāla vartinā evam dharmeṇa iti na niyamaḥ atad kālavartinā api tad niṣṭhatayā upalabhyamānena tad siddheḥ na hi atītaḥ saṃsāraḥ mukta ātma svarūpam upalabhamānaiḥ na upalabhyate upalabhyamānaḥ vā anya niṣṭhaḥ pratibhāti atha nityeṣu mithas kā vārtrā  sā api kuśala eva teṣām api hi satya saṃkalpānām vicitrāḥ saṃkalpa icchādaya riśvarasya iva aniyata deśa kāla viṣaya aparyanuyojya sāmagrīkāḥ anādi ananta saṃtānavantaḥ santi iti kim anyena viśeṣeṇa  api ca yad darśane yatra yat āropaḥ na bhavati sa hi tasya tatas bhedaḥ saḥ eva ca viśeṣaḥ sa ced sva rūpa bhūtaḥ hantvam ādi rūpeṇa bhātaḥ parāropam pratirundhyāt kaḥ tatonyaḥ tatas viśeṣaḥ tasya  evam anabhyupagame viśeṣa kptau= api kā gatiḥ vaiśeṣikasya sva para nirvāhakāḥ te viśeṣāḥ iti ced kim te eva  api ca pṛthaktve vidyamāne kim taiḥ viśeṣaiḥ  pṛthaktu asya eka jāti saṃgṛhīta tvāt na tata upi vyāvṛtta dhīrī iti ced tarhi tatas na kvacid api syāt viśeṣeṣu api vā viśeṣa tva ākrānteṣu kaḥ te nistāraḥ  viśeṣa tvam nāma jātiḥ na asti iti ced kim tat 
NP_5.1.1^8	 upādhiḥ iti ced kim tatas na saṃgrahaḥ  tathā sati kvacid api tad nibandhana anuvṛtta dhī bhaṅga prasaṅgāt evam anyonya abhāvena api gatārtha tā dustara iti parāstaḥ para abhimata viśeṣaḥ sāmānyam api paroktam sūtrakāraiḥ eva nirasta prāyam tathā hi tad ananya tvam ārambhaṇa śabda ādibhyaḥ ityādibhiḥ sūtraiḥ kārya daśāyām upādānasya avasthā antara āpatti mātram eva na punar para abhimatam avayavi ākhyam dravyam asti iti samarthanāt ghaṭa ādi avayavi abhāve tad āśrita ghaṭa tva ādi sāmānyam avayavi samaveta tayā abhyupagata guṇa ādayaḥ tad ubhaya ārambha prakriyā jālam ca nirmūlitam 
NP_5.1.1^9	 yat ca upādānasya ghaṭa tva ādi rūpam avasthā antaram saṃyoga viśeṣa ādi rūpam tat paraiḥ api kārya tayā abhyupetam upalambha ādibhiḥ ca tathā eva sidhyati iti na tatra api nitya tva kalpanā avakāśaḥ tatas sarveṣām dravyāṇām sva rūpa tona ādi ananta tvāt kārya dravya tva ātma tva ādi mātram eva śiṣyate guṇeṣu nityeṣu avasthā rūpeṣu ca anuvṛtta pratyaya nimittam kim iti cintyam tatra evam bhāṣitam śārīraka ādye saṃsthāna atirekiṇonekeṣu eka ākāra buddhi bodhyasya adarśanāt tāvatā eva go tva ādi jāti vyavahāra upapatteḥ atireka vādepi saṃsthānasya saṃpratipanna tvāt ca saṃsthānam eva jāti 
NP_5.1.1^10	 saṃsthānam nāma svāsa ādhāraṇam rūpam iti yathāvastu saṃsthānam anusaṃdheyam iti etat uktam bhavati kim saṃsthāna atiriktam sāmānyam vivikta sphuṭa pratyakṣa adhyavasāya bhedāt aṅgīkriyate uta upapatti balāt iti na ādyaḥ asiddheḥ na antyaḥ anyathā siddheḥ atirikta sāmānyam abhyupagacchata upi hi tad upalakṣaṇam saṃsthānam iṣṭam dṛṣṭam ca prativyakti niyatam saṃsthānam katham anuvṛtta pratyaya kāraṇam iti ced katham vā tad jātīyasya lakṣaṇam bhavati  anuvṛtta jāti antara saṃgṛhīta upādhi rūpa tayā iti ced tāvatā eva gavā ādi vyavahāra siddhau kim anyena 
NP_5.1.1^11	 tathā api anta tonuvṛttam sāmānyam kvacid abhyupagantavyam yatra ananyathā siddhiḥ anyathā upādhi saṃgrahasya api asaṃbhavāt iti ced tava api vā tatra sāmānyam upalakṣaṇena saṃgṛhyate na vā pūrvatra anyathā siddhiḥ anavasthitiḥ ca uttaratra niyāmaka adarśanāt jāteḥ āśraya vyavasthā na syāt vyāvṛttānām api svabhāvataḥ eva kāsāṃcid vyaktīnām tad vyañjaka tva niyatiḥ iti ced saḥ eva svabhāvaḥ kim na vyavahāram niyachet nirviṣayaḥ katham vyavahāraḥ syāt iti ced tāsām eva vyaktīnām viṣaya tvāt 
NP_5.1.1^12	 vyāvṛttānām anuvṛtta vyavahāra viṣaya tve sarvatra viṣaya vyavasthā bhajyeta iti ced vyāvṛttānām anuvṛtta vyañjaka tve sarvatra tad vyaktiḥ kim na syāt  saṃbandhā saṃbandhābhyām niyamāt iti ced na saṃbandhasya api samavāya nāmnaḥ sārvatrika tva abhyupagamāt tatra api abhivyakti pratiniyamasya mṛgya tvāt nānā samavāya vādepi vyakti svabhāva niyamasya dustyaja tvāt tathā api dṛṣṭa eka go vyakteḥ vyakti antare soyam iti pratyabhijñānam katham syāt ayam gauḥ iti eka vyaktau vyutpāditaḥ ca katham vyakti atyantarepi tat śabda vācya tām pratīyāt iti ced tava api vā katham 
NP_5.1.1^13	 eka dharma samavāyāt iti ced tena eva dharmeṇa svatas militasya samavāyasya eva nityam sarvatra vṛtti abhyupagamena sarvatra sarva vyavahāra saṃkara prasaṅgāt kāsāṃcid eva vyaktīnām tad vyañjaka tva svābhāvyāt vyavasthā uktā iti ced tarhi tāsām eva vyaktīnām pratisaṃdhāna vyavahārayoḥ viṣaya tvam astu tathā sati bhrānta tvam tayoḥ syāt iti ced na tad vyakti tvena pratisaṃdhāna ādeḥ abhāvāt api tarhi tathātvena vyakti svarūpa atiriktam tathātvam nāma antareṇa jātiḥ eva syāt iti ced tad jāti vyañjakam tad tad eka vyakti svarūpa atiriktam kim na jāti antaram syāt 
NP_5.1.1^14	 upādhi viśeṣaḥ eva ayam pratiniyata āśrayaḥ iti ced evam tarhi pratiniyata pratiyogikam svabhāva niyatam paraspara smāraka tvam upajīvya tad jātīya tayā pratisaṃdhāna vyavahāra upapattau kim anya kalpanena  tasmāraka taditara vibhāgaḥ kutastyaḥ iti ced tad vyañjaka taditara vibhāgaḥ te kutastyaḥ  darśana adarśana āyatte iti ced tulyam saṃbandha sādṛśyayoḥ abhāve katham smāraka tvam iti ced tayoḥ vā katham  sadṛśa saha anubhūta darśanasya saṃskāra udbodhaka tvāt iti ced tat api kutas  
NP_5.1.1^15	 kārya darśanāt kalpyate iti ced tulyam anyathā saṃbandham sādṛśyam vā ekam upādāya tad anyasya katham smāraka tvam iti ca udyasya durvāra tvāt na ca atra sādṛśyam na aṅgīkurmaḥ sausādṛśya rūpa tva abhyupagamāt sāmānyasya nāma antareṇa para abhimata jāti svīkāraḥ iti ced vyāvṛttānām saṃniveśa ādīnām eva pratiniyata pratiyogi smāraka svabhāva tayā sādṛśya rūpa tvāt gavaya ādeḥ api tarhi gojātīya tva ādi prasaṅgaḥ iti ced na sādṛśya sausādṛśya vibhāga svaya sāṃpratyayikasya sarva saṃmata tvāt iti evam sāmānya ādiṣu sūtrakāra ādibhiḥ nirasteṣu pariśiṣṭāḥ dravya guṇa karma rūpāḥ trayaḥ padārthāḥ iti kecid ācāryāḥ 
NP_5.1.2^1	 anye tu manyante yathā tad pratīteḥ anyathā siddha tayā te padārthāḥ bhāṣya kāra ādibhiḥ nirasyante tathā karma api iti ye tāvat iha sarvatra sūrya parispanda ādi vat apratyakṣam karma phala anumeyam icchanti tatra yayā sāmagryā karmaṇaḥ siddhiḥ abhimatā tayā eva dṛṣṭam karma phalam sādhyatām kim antarā kalpitena karmaṇā  tathā api ced kptiḥ anyatra api kāla viprakarṣā darśanepi sāmagrī kāryayoḥ madhye anyasya kpti prasaṅgaḥ tathā eva ca tratrāpi iti anavasthā syāt ye ca pratyakṣam karma iti āhuḥ taiḥ api nūnam karma phala tvena abhyupagama saṃyoga vibhāga atiriktam nipuṇa nirīkṣaṇa ipi na upalabhyate iti manyāmahe 
NP_5.1.2^2	 calati pratyayopi hi tāvatā eva caritārthaḥ na ca vācyam yāvat saṃyogam calati pratyaya prasaṅgaḥ iti pūrva deśa vibhāga pūrvaka deśa antara saṃyoga prathama kṣaṇa viṣaya tvāt tad pratyayasya tatas eva hi uttara kāle saṃyoge vartamānepya calat iti bhūta anusaṃdhānam upapannam nanu pravāha madhya sthite sthāṇau pūrva salila skandha viyogaḥ uttara salila skandha yogaḥ ca dṛśyate na ca tatra cala tvam icchāmaḥ vyoma ādayaḥ eva sthira deśa tvena vivakṣitāḥ iti ced na pravāhasya tatas viśeṣa adarśanāt laulyam viśeṣaḥ iti ced tarhi saṃyoga vibhāga atiriktam laulya rūpam karma pratyakṣam iti katham tad apahnavaḥ 
NP_5.1.2^3	 iti tatra āhuḥ yā nāma karma sāmagrī tvayā iṣyate sā tad tad karma phala tayā abhimatam saṃyoga viśeṣam utpādayantī niyata svabhāvam eva tam utpādayati atas eva eva saṃyogoneka niṣṭhopi san kvacid calati pratyaṃyam kvacid saṃyoga mātra pratyayam ca janayati yathā ekaḥ eva samavāyaḥ guṇa guṇibhyām aviśeṣeṇa svatas militopi san kvacid āśraya pratyayam kvacid āśrita pratyayam ca janayati na hi āśraya bhāvaḥ āśrita bhāvaḥ vā samavāya svarūpa atiriktaḥ tadvat iha api iti vayam tu brūmaḥ apratyakṣa karma vādaḥ tāvat prāc ukta dūṣaṇāt ayuktaḥ pratyakṣam tu karma svarūpataḥ durapahnavam tatra bhāṣya ādiṣu atireka vidhi niṣedha adarśanāt artha antara virodha abhāvāt ca udāsitavyam iti idam tu manyāmahe atirekepi guṇa vargāt na rāśi antaram karma vibhājaka abhāvāt sva icchā kalpita vibhājakasya sarvatra sulabha tvena yathā abhimatam ekam guṇam ubhayam vā aṅgīkṛtya rāśi antara kalpana prasaṅgāt guṇa avāntara vaicitryasya guṇa tva virodha abhāvāt atas dravyam adravyam iti eva vibhāgaḥ iti 
NP_5.1.3	 tatra ca ātma guṇa tayā abhimateṣu sukha duḥkha icchā dveṣa prayatnāḥ pañca tad tad utpādaka tayā abhimata buddhi viśeṣān atiriktāḥ veda artha saṃgrahe samarthitāḥ dharma adharmau vihita niṣiddha kriyā sādhya tayā abhimatau= ājñāvataḥ rājñaḥ iva sarva praśāsituḥ īśvarasya anugraha nigraha ākhya buddhi viśeṣa rūpau bhāṣya ādiṣu bahuṣu pradeśeṣu prapañcitau yaḥ punar saṃskāraḥ sa tāvat buddhi viśeṣa ātmanā uktaḥ na ca tad prayuktaḥ tatas ciranaṣṭa viprakṛṣṭa ākāre vyāpti adarśanāt vāsanā anuvṛtteḥ ca vācanika tvāt 
NP_5.1.4	 yadi api indriyasya indriyasya arthe iti ādi gītāślokeṣu bhāṣya kāraiḥ vāsanāyā icchā dvāreṇa eva pravṛtti hetu tva vacanāt jñāna vāsanā viśeṣa atiriktā karma vāsanā na asti tathā api jñāna vāsanā durapahnavā tatas ca tad āśraya mātram vicāryam tatra dharma bhūta jñānasya dravya tvaṃnyāya tattva ātma siddhi bhāśi ādi siddham anusara tām tad niṣṭha smṛti ākhya vikāra utpādakaḥ saṃskāraḥ api tad niṣṭhaḥ prāptaḥ antaraṅga tvāt abādhāt ca 
NP_5.1.5	 ye tu para paribhāṣam anusarantaḥ tad anuguṇam tasya guṇa tvam gṛhṇanti teṣām ātmani eva saṃskāraḥ iti viśeṣaḥ na ca buddhoḥ nitya tvam saṃkoca vikāsa ādi daśā bhedam ca abhyupagacchadbhiḥ adravya tvam tasyāḥ su vacam avasthā antara yogi tvam eva hi upādana tvam tat eva hi dravya lakṣaṇam tathā api naguṇa tva hāniḥ apṛthak siddha viśeṣaṇa tva atirikta guṇa tva avadarśanāt karma vyatirikta jāti mātra āśraya tva ādi rūpa guṇa lakṣaṇa saṃketasya asmābhiḥ anādaraṇāt na ca dravyasya āśrita svabhāva tva lakṣaṇam apṛthak siddha viśeṣaṇa tvam viruddham avayavini yuṣmābhiḥ api svīkaraṇāt yathā ca dravya tva viśeṣaṇa tva ādibhiḥ na virodhaḥ iṣyate evam atra api upalaṃmbha yukti ādeḥ sāmana carca tvāt atas jñānam dravyam tad avasthā viśeṣāḥ tu adravyāṇi iti saṃskāra ākhya vikāra āsthitiḥ api tatra eva yuktāḥ vega ākhyaḥ tu saṃskāraḥ tad utpādaka tva abhimata karma viśaiṣa atiriktaḥ na dṛśyate na ca yujyate sthita sthāpakau tu karma nivṛttau= api tad avinābhūta saṃyoga viśeṣa tvam vaktum yuktam 
NP_5.1.6^1	 ye ca bhagavataḥ nantāḥ maṅgala guṇāḥ prakīrtyante te sarva ipi ṣāṅguṇya vitati rūpāḥ iti saṃmatam yathā āhuḥ tava ananta guṇasya api ṣaṣ eva prathame guṇāḥ yaiḥ tvayā iva jagat kukṣau= anyepi antar niveśitāḥ iti ṣaṭsu ca guṇeṣu balam dhāraṇa sāmarthyam aiśvaryam niyamana śaktiḥ vikāra hetuṣu api avikṛta tvam vīryam tejaḥ para abhibhavana sāmarthyam anya anapekṣa tā vā iti lakṣitānām caturṇām ati mathane jñāna śakti vitati rūpa tvam vyaktam na ca jñāna śaktyoḥ api evam mithas ntarbhāvaḥ śakyaḥ ajñeṣu api dravyeṣu śakti darśanāt aśakteṣu api jñāna darśanāt atas eva jñāna viśeṣaḥ śaktiḥ iti api nirastam śakti viśeṣaḥ tu jñānam syāt iti ced kosau śakti śabda arthaḥ  
NP_5.1.6^2	 vilakṣaṇaḥ guṇa viśeṣaḥ prabhākara ādi nayena padārtha antaram vā iti ced na tarhi jñānasya tad viśeṣa tā sidhyet atha kārya upayukta viśeṣaṇa mātram śaktiḥ iti sarva prayoga anugatam paśyasi tadā na kevalam jñānasya api tu sarvasya eva śakti tvam prāptam sarvasya api pradhāna kāraṇa tayā abhimate kasmiṃścid viśeṣaṇa tvena avasthānāt nanu evam udayana ādīnām iva svarūpa sahakāri vyatirikta śakti abhāvaḥ prasaktaḥ iti ced ananyathā asiddha yukti vaśāt āgama balāt vā tad siddheḥ tad śabdaḥ tu vivakṣā viśeṣāt syāt iti brūmaḥ śakti samarthana saṃrambhaḥ ca ācāryāṇām nyāya kuliśe nipuṇam anusaṃdheyaḥ śakti mātra kāraṇa ādi vādāḥ ca bāhyānām upalambha yukti āpta āgama ādi virahāt anādaraṇīyāḥ sā ced upādānam sūkṣmandravyam eva asau syāt iti na vivādaḥ 
NP_5.1.7	 atha ācit dravya viśeṣa guṇān paśyāmaḥ tatra śabda ādayaḥ pañca tad tad bhūta vartinaḥ pratyakṣa ādi balāt abhyupagatāḥ sattva rajaḥ tamāṃsi ca śāstra anusāreṇa saṃyogaḥ ca pratyakṣa ādi siddhaḥ nairantarya mātram eva ayam iti ced tat kim dravya svarūpam uta āgantuḥ avasthā viśeṣaḥ  na ādyaḥ nitya tva prasaṅgāt na dvitīyaḥ nāma antareṇa tad abhidhānāt iti vibhāga pṛthaktve tu abhāva ukta nyāyena dūṣaṇīye paratva aparatve api sukha ādi= chāyayā na hi tad tad upādhi avacchinna deśa kāla viśeṣa saṃbandha atirikte paratva aparatve paśyāmaḥ tad kalpane ca prāk tva pratyaktvādayopi hi bahavaḥ guṇāḥ tulya nyāyāḥ kalpyāḥ syuḥ evam sat asat guṇa pradarśana prakriyayā saṃkhyā parimāṇa guru tva drava tva snehānām tattvam avasātavyam iti adravyeṣu eṣā diś 
NP_5.1.8^1	 atha dravyāṇi vimṛśyante tatra tāvat kaumārila abhimata vibhu śabda ākhya dravya vādaḥ śabdasya acit avasthā viśeṣa tvena śruti ādi siddha tvāt nirākāryaḥ ātma siddhau tu śabdasya dharmī ativarti tva gatimat tva vādaḥ tad āśraya bhūta avayava dvāreṇa iti netavyaḥ yat tu tamaḥ khalu calam nīlam para apara vibhāga vat prasiddha dravya vaidharmyāt navabhyaḥ bhettum arhati iti āhuḥ tat etat dravyam tāvat abhyupagacchāmaḥ tathā hi uktam vara da gurubhiḥ tattva sāre tamaḥ nāma dravyam bahula viralam mecakacalam pratīmaḥ kena api kvacid api na bādhaḥ ca dadṛśe 
NP_5.1.8^2	 atas kalpyaḥ hetuḥ pramitiḥ api śābdī vijayate nirālokam cakṣuḥ prathayati hi tat darśana vaśāt iti etena viyati vitatānām sūkṣmāṇām pṛthivī avayavānām kṛṣṇaḥ guṇaḥ tamaḥ iti pakṣopi pratikṣiptaḥ sa āśrayasya eva tasya grahaṇa virodha abhāvāt guṇa mātra tayā ca kasya api anupalambhāt sparśa rūpa rasānām ca śabda gandha vat bhrāntau pramitau vā nirādhāra grahaṇa adarśanāt ca iti evam dravya tve siddhe kṛṣṇa varṇasya dravyasya pṛthivī tvam eva abhyupagantum ucitam yat kṛṣṇam tat annasya iti śruteḥ 
NP_5.1.8^3	 yadi api pṛthivyām pāka viśeṣa vaśāt śukla ādi rūpam na anyatra pākāt api bhavati ākāśa ādiṣu nailya upalambha upi hi pañcīkaraṇa mūla pṛthivī saṃsargāt ākāśe ca aviśeṣāt iti sūtre bhāṣitam aṇḍa antarvartinaḥ ca ākāśasya trivṛt karaṇa upadeśa pradarśinta pañcī karaṇena rūpava tvāt cākṣuṣa tvepya virodhaḥ iti nanu evam ākāśam eva dravya antara saṃsargān nīlam tamaḥ iti upalabhyate iti syāt iti ced na syāt ākāśe tamaḥ iti pṛthak upalambhasvārasyāt dravnaya antara tve tu kalpanā gauravāt antatotrā api pañcīkaraṇena dravya antara saṃsargasya abhyupagata tvāt ca iti 
NP_5.1.8^4	 sparśa anupalambhaḥ tu indranīla āloka durdina ātapa ādeḥ iva anudbhava ādeḥ api syāt na ca pārthiva rūpasya sarvasya āloka sāpekṣa cakṣuḥ grāhya tva niyamaḥ kalpyaḥ karaṇa vaicitryāt iva viṣaya vaicitryāt api vyavasthā upapatteḥ divā bhītānām viśiṣṭa añjana rañjita akṣāṇām ca āloka nirapekṣam eva cakṣuṣā eva padārthāḥ gṛhyante āloka abhāva mātre ca tamasi tamaḥ jyotiṣoḥ nivṛtti vacanam cavyāhanyeta pratiniyata nailya āropakalpanā prayāsaḥ ca atas pṛthivī viśeṣa tvam tamasaḥ yuktam pṛthivī ādīni pañca bhūtāni manaḥ ca triguṇa dravya pariṇati viśeṣa tayā śruti ādi siddha tvāt na pṛthak dravyāṇi 
NP_5.1.8^5	 tatra ca avayavya ākhyam bhautika dravyam tad ananya tvam ārambhaṇa śabda ādibhyaḥ iti ādibhiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ sūtraiḥ buddhi śabda antara ādeḥ anyathā siddhi ādi upapādanena nirastam mahat dīrgha vat vā hva sva parimaṇḍalābhyām ityādibhiḥ ca parāmabhimataḥ paramāṇuḥ atas pariṇāma viśeṣāt upalambha yogya tva ayogya tva ādi daśā viśeṣa yogi prakṛti ādi saṃjñam dravyam vicitra vyavasthita krama samaṣṭi vyaṣṭi rūpam avatiṣṭhate diś tattvam api tad tad upādhi avacchinnāḥ tad tad deśa viśeṣāḥ eva atirikta kalpakānām parāpara pratyaya viśeṣa ādīnām anyathā siddheḥ 
NP_5.1.8^6	 diś utpatti śrutiḥ ca tad upādhika tad nirvāhaka sṛṣṭyā upapannā anyathā dyupṛthivī antarikṣa ādi vat triguṇa pariṇati viśeṣa tā eva syāt na pṛthak dravya tā na ca evam kālepi prasaṅgaḥ nityasya kālasya bhagavat parāśara ādibhiḥ pṛthak prasaṃkhyānāt tasya prakṛti pariṇati viśeṣa tva ādi pakṣāḥ tad pūrva apara kāla avaśyaṃbhāvāt śruti ādi balāt ca pratyastāḥ atas triguṇa kālau= ātmāca iti trīṇi siddhāniḥ iśvarasya tu pṛthak saṃkhyāne catvāri tasya hi cetana tva ādibhiḥ saṃgraha saṃbhavepi avāntara vailakṣaṇya jñāpanāya pṛthak saṃkhyānam prācāmanādi vācām ca anyathā prakriyā antareṇa acetaneṣu api saṃgraha prasaṃgāt 
NP_5.1.8^7	 viviktam ca bhagavatā parāśareṇa parama ātma ātmanoḥ yogaḥ parama arthaḥ iti iṣyate mithyā etat anya dravyam hi na eti tat dravya tām yatas iti evam dharma bhūta jñāna ākhyam api dravyam ajaḍa tva aviśeṣa īpi spuṭatara vaidharmya anatara balāt pṛthak gaṇayanti tasya adravya tva vādaḥ keṣāñcit nātha muni yāmuna muni bhāṣya kāra ādi prabandha virodhāt prāyas para citta rañjana arthaḥ śuddha sattva ākhyasya ca dravya antarasya para vigraha ādi yātha arthya upadeśa pravṛtta nirukta ādi āpta āgama siddha tvāt sūkṣma triguṇa avasthā viśeṣa ādi pakṣāḥ bahiṣkāryāḥ atas ṣaṭ etāni dravyāṇi 
NP_5.1.8^8	 bhoktṛ bhogya niyantṝṇām sat ā ātmanā eka dravya tva ādi pakṣāḥ api nirviśeṣa sanmātra pakṣa vat vyāghāta śruti virodha ādibhiḥ bahuśas bhāṣya ādiṣu nirastāḥ tatra triguṇa śuddha sattve sva niruktyā eva lakṣye kṣaṇa lava ādi ātmā kālaḥ aṇuḥ jñātāḥ jīvaḥ vibhuḥ tu īśvaraḥ jāna ati vyavahārāsādhāraṇa kāraṇam vyavahārya viśeṣaḥ matiḥ evam triguṇa kāla jīva īśvara śuddha sattva m ati rūpeṇa ṣoḍhā dravya vibhāgaḥ evam pramāṇa sārtha ghaṇṭā pathena dravya adravya rūpa prameya grāmam adhijigamiṣatām na kudṛṣṭi bāhya kalpita kūṭa yukti garta nipātaḥ iti 
NP_5.2.9^1	 atra yadi api pramā viṣayaḥ prameyam iti vyutpattyā āropita ākāra vyavaccheda arthayā anāropita rūpam sarvam prameyam tathā api niḥśreyasa antaraṅga tayā tad arthibhiḥ prakarṣeṇa meyam prameyam iha vivakṣim yat viṣayeṇa bhrameṇa saṃsarāmaḥ yat viṣayeṇa ca tattva jñānena apavarjyemahi tat iha naḥ prakarṣeṇa meyam prameyam tat ca dvādaśavidha mukta mākṣapāde ātma śarīra indriya artha buddhi manaḥ pravṛtti doṣa pretya bhāva phala duḥkha apavargāḥ prameyam iti tatra cetanaḥ ātmā sa dvidhāḥ iśvaroni īśvaraḥ iti jagat kartār iśvaraḥ jagat vyāpāra rahitaḥ cetanoni īśvaraḥ yat caitanya samāna adhikaraṇam yat apṛthak siddham yat dravyam tat tasya śarīram tat dvividham karma jam akarma jam ca iti ādyam asmad ādīnām dvitīyam īśvara ādīnām sāttvika ahaṅkāra upādānakam dravyam indriyam tat ekādaśavidham pañca jñāna indriyāṇi pañcakarmenidrayāṇi manaḥ ca iti indriya gocarāḥ iha arthāḥ te ca śabda ādayaḥ guṇāḥ tad viśiṣṭāni ca artha prakāśaḥ buddhiḥ smṛti ādi karaṇam indriyam manaḥ 
NP_5.2.9^2	 manaḥ vāc kāyānām puṇyā puṇya rūpaḥ vyāpāraḥ iha pravṛttiḥ tathāvidha pravṛtti hetavaḥ doṣāḥ te ca saṃgrahāt rāga dveṣa mohāḥ pūrva deham vihāya uttara deha prāptiḥ pretyabhāvaḥ pravṛtti sādhyam phalam tat eva puruṣeṇa pravṛtti phalatayā uddiṣṭam prayojanam pratikūla vedanīyam duḥkham tatra sukha tad sādhana ādikam api viṣa saṃpṛkta madhu vat prabhūta anartha anuṣaṅgi tvāt duḥkham eva mumukṣuṇā bhāvyam iti tasya api pratikūla vedanīya tvam duḥkha antara kāraṇa asamāna adhikaraṇāḥ duḥkha nivṛttiḥ apavargaḥ sa ca svābhāvika ātma svarūpa āvirbhāva pūrvaka samasta vibhūti guṇa viśiṣṭa niratiśaya ānanda brahma anubhava garbhaḥ iti parama puruṣa arthaḥ tad pūrvakaḥ vā tādṛśa brahma anubhava upavargaḥ iti etat eva ca prameyam saṃgrahāt caturdhā vibhajya kecid anusaṃdadhate aheyam tasya nivartakam hānam tasya upāyaḥa iti ye tu kaṇa caraṇa ādayaḥ ṣaṣ sapta ādi rūpeṇa sarvān padārthān vibhajya parīkṣante te sāmānya viśeṣa samavāya ādīnām padārtha antara tva pratikṣepeṇa nirastāḥ 
NP_5.2.9^3	 tatas ca dravya guṇa karmāṇi trīṇi eva avaśiṣyante tatra api karmaṇaḥ saṃpratipanna guṇa atirikta tva pakṣepi saṃskāra ādi guṇa avāntara viśeṣa vat guṇa pakṣa kakṣīkārāt dvau padārthau tatra ca guṇa śabdasya apṛthak siddha viśeṣaṇa mātra vyutpannasya tathāvidheṣu keṣucid dravyeṣu api vṛtteḥ dravya guṇa rūpeṇa vibhāgān aucityāt dravyam adravyam iti eva padārtha vibhāgam ādriyāmaheḥ idṛśasya tu vicārasya apavarge paraṃparayā upayogaḥ mumukṣūṇām pradhānatamam tu prameyam viśiṣṭam brahma ekam eva iti manvānaḥ bhagavān bādarāyaṇaḥ atha atas brahma jijñāsā iti upakramya tat eva sa prakāram nirūpitavān tad prakāra tayā eva anyat prameyam kecid tu deha ātma viveka krama anusāreṇa bhoktā bhogyam preritāram ca matvā iti śruti prakriyayā ca tridhā tattvam vibhajya cintayanti tatra api sa prakāra dravya cintanāda dravya cintā api antar bhavati tad tulya nyāya tayā kāla cintā ca 
NP_5.2.9^4	 tad abhiprāyeṇa kālasya padārtha viśeṣaṇa tayā eva samasta vastu prati iti antar bhāvāt na pṛthak astitva ādayaḥ vaktavyāḥ na ca parihartavyāḥ kālosti na asti iti vyavahāraḥ vyavahartṝṇām jāti ādi astitvanāstitva vyavahāra tulyaḥ iti jaina nirākaraṇa samaye bhāṣya kāraiḥ uktam ātataḥ ca brahma ekam eva tattvam iti vā cit acit īśvara bhedena trīṇi tattvāni iti vā paśyatām na kaśvit viśeṣaḥ svarūpa bhedasya viśiṣṭa aikyasya ca ubhayeṣām abhimata tvāt atas eva pradhāna puruṣa vyakta kālāḥ tu pravibhāgaśaḥ rūpāṇi sthiti sarga anta vyakti sadbhāva hetavaḥ ityādi anusāreṇa caturdhā pañcadhā vā vibhajya cintayatām kārya viśeṣaiḥ saha pañca ṣaṣ saptaviṃśati ādi saṃkhyām niveśayatām ca pūrvā viśeṣaḥ eva śrūyate ca tam ṣaṅviṃśakam iti āhuḥ saptaviṃśam atha apare puruṣam nirguṇam sāṃravyam atharvaśirasaḥ viduḥ iti prāpyam prāptā prāpti upāyaḥ nivartyam phalam ca iti kecid pañcadhā prameyam parisaṃcakṣate saṃbandha viśeṣeṇa saha anye ṣoḍhā iti 
NP_5.2.10^1	 atha ayam aparaḥ pravṛtti arthaḥ saṃgraha ūnuṣṭhāna parihāra antaraṅgaḥ tathā hi hitam ahitam ca prakarṣeṇa meyam tatra laukika hita ahitayoḥ anvaya vyatireka āyurvedanīti śāstra ādikam pramāṇam tat api yoga sādhana bhūta śarīra rakṣaṇa artham mumukṣuṇā api śruti smṛti ādya virodhena anusaraṇīyam alaukika hita ahitayoḥ tu vedāḥ pramāṇam tad upabṛṃhaṇa tayā smṛti itihāsa purāṇāni ca yat ca śruti vihitam tat akhilam api yathā adhikāram hitam yat ca tat niṣiddham tat akhilam api ahitam nanu abhicāra ādi karmaṇām anartha hetūnām kṣudra puruṣa artha sādhanānām ca kāmyānām karmaṇām katham hita tvam  ucyate adhikāri viśeṣam apekṣya hi sarvaḥ vidhiḥ niṣedhaḥ ca yathā uktam traiguṇya viṣayāḥ vedāḥ iti 
NP_5.2.10^2	 yaḥ hi sukham duḥkha nivṛttim ca icchati tasya tad sādhanam apekṣamāṇasya laukikeṣu sādhaneṣu pravṛttasya teṣām niraya ādi hetu bhūtānartha hetu tvena tad parihārāya anartha hetu tva rahitāḥ sukha ādi upāyāḥ pratipādyante evam kāmya karmāṇi pāralaukikāni dṛṣṭa jātīya tad adhika phala artha tayā dṛṣṭa anartha āvaha sukha pravṛtti pratibandha aupayika tvāt hitāni eva rāgiṇām tathā aihalaukikāni api citra ādīni kārīrya ādīni tu jagat hitāni api abhicāra karmaṇā upi hiṃsā ādi yuktasya api svarūpataḥ na anartha hetu tvam tad aṅga paśu hiṃsā ādeḥ agnīṣomīya ādi vat vidhi prāpta tvāt api tu sva sādhyena aprāpta viṣaya vadha ādinā tad apekṣayā ca abhicāraḥ niṣidhyate sā upi hi kvacid avaśya kartavyaḥ eva ṣaṭsu anabhicaran patet ityādi darśanāt 
NP_5.2.10^3	 atas ca mumukṣoḥ api rakṣaka kṣatriya ādi abhāve rākṣasa ādi abhibhave ca ātma rakṣaṇa artham abhicāraḥ kartavyaḥ eva sarvatas eva ātmānam gopāyet iti śāstrāt anyathā aharahar anuṣṭheyasya aprayāṇāt anuvartanīyasya karma ādeḥ uccheda prasaṅgena upāya aniṣpatteḥ mokṣā siddhi prasaṅgāt vṛṣṭi anna ādi dṛṣṭa arthāni ca sarvāṇi upāsana niṣpatti aupayika tayā tat tad apekṣāyām anuṣṭheyāni pāralaukikāni tu tad phala abhisaṃdhi viraheṇa karma yoga anuṣṭhānadaśāyām nitya naimittikaiḥ ekīkṛtya kartavyāni naimittikāni hi sarvāṇi prasakta anartha parihāra artha tayā sarva hitāni eva evam nityāni uttara karma adhikāra artha tvāt akaraṇa nimitta pratyavāya parihāra artha tvāt ca atas śruti vihitam sva varṇa āśrama ucitam sarvam hitam eva atas eva hi smaranti śāstram hi vatsalataram mātā pitṛ sahasrataḥ iti 
NP_5.2.10^4	 evam sthite pravāha an ādi sāmagrī cakra vaśāt aniyata samaya samāgata sakala saiddha antika samālambanīya sucar ita paripāka nivṛtta pratibandha parama puruṣa kaṭākṣa viśeṣa samunmiṣita sattva sāmarthyena kara tala āmalaka vat ālokita heya upādeya vibhāgasya anādi ananta bahuvidha durviṣaha duḥkha anuṣaṅga dūṣita alpa asthira sāṃsārika sukha maya viṣa madhu viraktasya samasta durita varga apavargāyamāṇa nitya niratiśaya ānanda mukunda caraṇa aravinda sevā makaranda lampaṭasya yathāśakti varṇa aśrama ucita nitya naimittika niṣiddha parihāra saha kṛtam darśana samāna ākāra dhruva anusmṛti rūpam bhagavat upāsanam hitatamam vihitam tat ca sat akṣara nyāsa vaiśvānara madhu bhūmat a harādi bhedena bahuvidham traivarṇika sarva āśrama sādhyam tasya ca mahānīya viṣaya niratiśaya prīti rūpa tvena bhakti śabda vācya tvam 
NP_5.2.10^5	 ayam eva ca paramaḥ yogaḥ trayī anta anuvidhāyiṣu sarveṣu mokṣa śāstreṣu pratipādyate yathā āha bhagavān parāśaraḥ ātma prayatna sāpekṣā viśiṣṭā yā manogatiḥ tasyāḥ brahmaṇi saṃyogaḥ yogaḥ iti abhidhīyate iti smarati ca bhagavān śāṇḍilī arḥ idṛśaḥ paramātmā ayam pratyagātmā ava tathā īdṛśaḥ tad saṃbandha anusaṃdhānam iti yogaḥ prakīrtitaḥ iti tatra cit acit viveka ādi mātre sāṃkhyam upakurute yama niyama ādi samādhi parikara śodhane yogaḥ itikartavya tā viśeṣe karma kāṇḍa ādayaḥ sarvatra eva pañca rātram niṣiddha kāmya vargeṣu vyarthān āvaśyakeṣu ca śama ādi vidhiḥ anyatra pravṛttyā na virudhyate soyam evaṃvidhaḥ parama yoga ākhyaḥ dharmaḥ mayi eva manaḥ ādhatsvaḥ iti gīyate tat aśaktasya atha cittam samādhātum na śaknoṣi mayi sthiram 
NP_5.2.10^6	 abhyāsa yogena gataḥ mām icchā āptum dhanañjaya abhyāseṣu asamarthosi mad karma paramaḥ bhava ityādinā pūrva parvāṇi vidhīyante yaḥ prīti pūrva bhagavat asā dhāraṇa karmaṇi api na samarthaḥ tasya viṣaya rasa vaimukhya jananāya samasta vaiṣayika sukha śeṣi tvena cirataram anusaṃhitasya api sva ātmanaḥ sāṃsārika samasta sukha samadhika ānanda svarūpam ālokayitum āntara cakṣuḥ virodhi timira paṭala pāṭanāya jñāna karma yoga ākhye dve bheṣaje tatra ātma cintana rūpaḥ jñāna yogaḥ tad ālokanentaraṅga bhūtaḥ tatra api asamarthasya tad adhikāra siddhi artham karma yogaḥ tena tatra siddha adhikārasya api śiṣṭa tayā vyapadeśyasya antargata ātma jñānaḥ karma yogaḥ eva kāryaḥ anyathā kṛtsna vidā upyasya jñāna yoga aśakta akṛtsna vedi puruṣa buddhi bheda janana mūla mahattara durita vaśena jñāna yoga upi pratibadhyeta 
NP_5.2.10^7	 tādṛśena eva ca karma yogena sukara tva ādi guṇavatā cirataram anuṣṭhitena jñāna yoga vyavadhānam antareṇa api ātma avalokanam sidhyati karma yoga īpya samarthaḥ tu vikalam api karma yogam ārabheta na iha abhikramanā aśosti pratyavāyaḥ na vidyate su alpam api asya dharmasya trāyate mahataḥ bhayāt ityādibhiḥ vaiṅkalya viccheda ādi saṃbhava ipi phala avinābhā= a ādi pratipādanāt prakrama mātreṇa api prasannaḥ bhagavān pauṣkalyam āpādayati sarveṣu ca amīṣu parvasu tad tad sāmagrī cakra ghaṭanāya tad tad phala pradānāya ca saḥ eva hi śaraṇam anusaraṇīyaḥ tathā ca āmananti sā kāṣṭhā sā parā gatiḥ iti saḥ eva parama puruṣaḥ vaśī kārya kāṣṭhā parama prāpyaḥ ca iti arthaḥ tasya ca vaśīkaraṇam tat śaraṇa āgatiḥ eva iti bhāṣyam evam hitatamasya upāsanasya diś mātram darśitam phalam ca apavarga rūpam prāk eva lakṣitam 
NP_5.2.10^8	 anyeṣām tu deha viccheda mātra sahasra yuvati saṃbhoga samaḥ tālīka viṣaya vijñāna saṃtāna uccheda vāsanā atyanta virāma viṣaya uparāga vaidhurya n i t y o r d h v a g a m a n a s a k a l a l o k a m a s t a k o p a r i n i v i ṣ ṭ a s ā d h ā r a ṇ a d e h a v i ś e ṣ ā n u p r a v e ś a n i r ā v a r a ṇ a t v asvānanda anubhava svātantrya lābha śiva sārūpya śiva āpatti cid śakti pariśeṣa avidyā nivṛtti upādhi nivṛtti sakala vaiśeṣika guṇa uccheda prabhṛtayo niḥśreyasa vikalpā d e h ādi atirikta ātma sadbhāva bāhya artha pāramārthika tva tad tad āgama aprāmāṇya brahma nirvikāra tva nirdeṣa tva tad jñāna ānanda nitya tva ādi samarthakaiḥ śārīraka paryantaiḥ śāstraiḥ pratikṣepyāḥ iti tatra tatra vistaraḥ draṣṭavyaḥ iha tu pramāṇa cintāyāḥ parama prayojanam darśayitum prameyasya saṃgraha uktiḥ sa parikara pramāṇa maryādā pratipādana para tvāt nyāya vistara śāstrasya iti 
NP_5.2.11	 svātantryeṇa mitam sukha itara tayā yat bhāti jantoḥ idam sarvam yasya vibhūtiḥ ivi avasitam svādam vyanakti svakam antar sva antam ananta nandathu nidhiḥ medaḥ dṛśām mādṛśām āvirbhāvayatu svayam sa bhagavān ātmānam ātma īśvaraḥ yatra udāsata jaimini prabhṛtayaḥ śruti artha cintā parāḥ yasyām kandalayanti manda matayaḥ pāriplavān viplavān viśveṣām iha veṅkaṭeśa viduṣā viśrāntaye vādinām prācī nītiṣu paryaśodhi saraṇiḥ pracchāya niṣkaṇṭakāḥ śuddhim bibhrati mādṛśām bhaṇitayaḥ cūḍa anvaye kevalam prānte miśram abhāṇi nīti nipuṇaiḥ kim teṣu amantavya tā yuktam varga yuge vimṛśya saradhā puṣpa kramam yauktikaiḥ aṅgīkartum aśaki anihnava guṇa granthaḥ nibandhaḥ mama nirūḍha nigama traye nikhila loka cintāmaṇau prasattim upaseduṣi praṇidadhāna bhāva āspade ratim bhajati bhāvanā layam iva upayāti drutam rama avasu matī saha ācarita dharmaṇi brahmaṇi
